// function UpdateCommodities(PackageIndex) // returns undefined
    function UpdateCommodities (PackageIndex)
    {
      /* Click the active tab, just to refresh the commodities.  This will only work on the first commodity added. */
      $('div.ui-tab-container > div.ng-isolate-scope > ul > li.active > a').click();

      /* Clicking the button below refreshes the full commodities list in the UI. */
      $('#goods').find('div.ng-table-counts.btn-group').find('button:not(.active):first').click();
    }

// function GetTranslatedUnitOfMeasurement(sVal) // returns translated unit code or original value
    function GetTranslatedUnitOfMeasurement (sVal)
    {
      switch (sVal.toUpperCase())
      {
        case "EACH":
          return "EA";
        case "YARDS":
        case "YARD":
          return "YD";
        case "METER":
          return "M";
        case "SF":
          return "SFT";
        case "PAIR":
          return "PR";
        case "SR":
          return "ROL";
        default:
          return sVal;
      }
    }

// function CheckForMatchingConsignee(CustomerOrderObject) // returns boolean
      CheckForMatchingConsignee: function (CustomerOrderObject)
      {
        try
        {
          var con = $('name-address[nameaddress="vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Consignee"]');

          let a = {
            //conCompany: $(con).find('input[name="company"]').val().trim().toUpperCase().replaceAll(' ',''),
            conAddress1: $(con).find('input[name="address1"]').val().trim().toUpperCase(),
            conCity: $(con).find('input[name="city"]').val().trim().toUpperCase(),
            conState: $(con).find('input[name="stateProvince"]').val().trim().toUpperCase(),
            conPostalCode: $(con).find('input[name="postalCode"]').val().trim().substring(0, 5)
          };

          let b = {
            //conCompany: CustomerOrderObject.shipAddress1.CONSIGNEE_COMPANY.trim().toUpperCase().replaceAll(' ', ''),
            conAddress1: CustomerOrderObject.shipAddress1.trim().toUpperCase(),
            conCity: CustomerOrderObject.shipCity.trim().toUpperCase(),
            conState: CustomerOrderObject.shipState.trim().toUpperCase(),
            conPostalCode: CustomerOrderObject.shipZipCode.trim().substring(0, 5)
          };

          /* Remove all the spaces in the strings so we get a good comparison, not one that's thrown off by an extra space. */
          let aa = JSON.stringify(a).replaceAll(' ', '');
          let bb = JSON.stringify(b).replaceAll(' ', '');

          /* Quick comparison to see if the strings match. */
          if (aa != bb)
          {
            Logger.Log({ Source: 'CheckForMatchingConsignee()', Message: 'Could not add order ' + CustomerOrderObject.orderNumber + ' (' + CustomerOrderObject.orderId + '). Primary order data to follow.', Data: a });
            Logger.Log({ Source: 'CheckForMatchingConsignee()', Message: 'Could not add order ' + CustomerOrderObject.orderNumber + ' (' + CustomerOrderObject.orderId + '). Subsequent order data to follow.', Data: b });
          }

          return (aa == bb);
        }
        catch (error)
        {
          Logger.Log({ Source: 'CheckForMatchingConsignee()', Error: error });
        }
      }

// function UpdateReferencesWithOrderNumbers(OrderNumber) // returns undefined
      UpdateReferencesWithOrderNumbers: function (OrderNumber)
      {
        var inputShipperReference = $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].ShipperReference"]');
        var inputMiscReference07 = $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference7"]');
        var shipperReferenceVal = $(inputShipperReference).val() + ',' + OrderNumber;

        var newUniqueString = Tools.GetUniqueCSVStringFromString(shipperReferenceVal);

        /* Set these input values.  ShipperReference is used by the customer, MiscReference7 is used by the SBR to update each record post-ship. */
        /* ShipperReference ONLY keeps the first order number when it goes to PostShip, before the comma, MiscReference7 keeps the entire string. */
        /* On the server-side, if MiscReference7 contains a comma, each item in the csv list gets posted back.  If MiscReference7 is empty, the ShipperReference is used instead for a single post-back. */
        $(inputShipperReference).val(newUniqueString);
        $(inputMiscReference07).val(newUniqueString);
      }

// function NewShipment(shipmentRequest) // returns undefined
    this.NewShipment = function (shipmentRequest) {
        $(document).ready(function() {
            $('[id="Consignee Name Address"]').on('keydown', $('[id="Consignee Name Address"]').find("input[name='code']"), function(e) { 
                var keyCode = e.keyCode || e.which; 

                if (keyCode == 9) { 
                    e.preventDefault(); 
                    // look up the address on tab
                    $('[caption="Consignee Name Address"]').find('button[ng-click="search(nameaddress)"]').click();
                } 
            });
        });
    }

// this.PreLoad(loadValue, shipmentRequest, userParams) // returns void
this.PreLoad = function (loadValue, shipmentRequest, userParams) {
        shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.UserData1 = $("#cboBatches select option:selected").val().replace('string:','');
        thisShipper = shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Shipper;
        thisBatchName = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference5;
    };

// this.PostLoad(loadValue, shipmentRequest) // returns void
this.PostLoad = function (loadValue, shipmentRequest) {
        shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Shipper = thisShipper;
        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference5 = thisBatchName;
    };

// this.NewShipment(shipmentRequest) // returns void
this.NewShipment = function (shipmentRequest) {
        // set focus into the Load ID box
         $("input:text").first().focus();
         
        // Populate existing Batches into custom shipping template Batch List drop down
        //  ... This also auto populates package misc_reference 5 
         this.vm.batches = this.GetBatches(client.userContext);
    };

// this.GetBatches(context) // returns batches
this.GetBatches = function (context) {        
        var batches;
        var data = { SearchCriteria: null, CompanyId: context.CompanyId };
        this.thinClientAPIRequest('GetBatches', data, false).done(function (response) {
            batches = response.Batches;
            console.log(batches);
        });
        
        return batches;
    };

// this.AddPackage(shipmentRequest, packageIndex) // returns void
this.AddPackage = function (shipmentRequest, packageIndex) {
       
        shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex].MiscReference2 = shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex - 1].MiscReference1;
	    shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex].MiscReference2 = shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex - 1].MiscReference2;
    };

// Source: Alight Solutions (ALISOL)_DirectToMobileCBR_2434.cs
// function PreShip(shipmentRequest, userParams) // returns void
    this.PreShip = function (shipmentRequest, userParams) 
	{
		debugger;
		
		shipmentRequest = SetShipmentRequestUserData(shipmentRequest);
		
		if (CurrentShipmentIsD2M())
		{
			
			var loadedEmailValue = shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Email;
			
			if(loadedEmailValue === '')
			{
				alert("Recipient email address is required for Direct to Mobile shipments");
				return false;
			}
			
			SetReturnDeliveryCheckBoxAndInsurance(true,shipmentRequest);
			
			SetReturnDeliveryAddressEmail(shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Email);			
					
			if (shipmentRequest.Packages !== undefined) 
			{
				for (var x = 0; x < shipmentRequest.Packages.length; x++) 
				{
					shipmentRequest.Packages[x].ReturnDeliveryAddressEmail = shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Email;
					shipmentRequest.Packages[x].CommercialInvoiceMethod = 0;
				}
			}												
		}		
    };

// function AddPackage(shipmentRequest, packageIndex) // returns void
    this.AddPackage = function (shipmentRequest, packageIndex) {
		if(CurrentShipmentIsD2M())
		{
			SetReturnDeliveryAddressEmail(shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Email);	   	
		}  
		shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex].MiscReference2 = shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex - 1].MiscReference1;		
    };

// function SetReturnDeliveryCheckBoxAndInsurance(enabled, shipmentRequest) // returns void
	function SetReturnDeliveryCheckBoxAndInsurance(enabled = false,shipmentRequest)
	{		
		debugger;
		if (shipmentRequest != undefined && enabled == true)
		{			
			if ((shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Country.toUpperCase() != USCOUNTRY) 
				&& (shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Country.toUpperCase() != USACRONYM))
			{
				$('select option[value="number:1"]').prop("selected",true);				
			}
			else	
			{
				$('select option[value="number:1"]').prop("selected",false);				
			}
		}
	}

// function SetReturnDeliveryShipmentConfiguration() // returns void
	function SetReturnDeliveryShipmentConfiguration()
	{		
		SetDescription('Returned Goods');	
		//SetReturnDeliveryAddressEmail('');
		SetReturnDeliveryCheckBoxAndInsurance(true,undefined);
		//$('input[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].ReturnDeliveryAddressEmail"]').val();
		LoadReturnAddressFromShipperAddress("SetReturnDeliveryShipmentConfiguration()");	
	}

// function ClearReturnDeliveryShipmentConfiguration() // returns void
	function ClearReturnDeliveryShipmentConfiguration()
	{		
		SetDescription('');
		SetReturnDeliveryAddressEmail('');
		SetReturnDeliveryCheckBoxAndInsurance(false,undefined);	
		$('select[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].CommercialInvoiceMethod"]').val('');
		//ClearAllSelect();
	}

// function CurrentShipmentIsD2M() // returns boolean
	function CurrentShipmentIsD2M()
	{	
		
		var cond1 = CurrentUserIsD2MEnabled();
		var cond2 = $("#"+D2M_TEMPLATE_CHECKBOX_SHIPMENT_ID).is(":checked");
		var cond3 = CurrentShipperIsD2MEnabled();
		return cond1 && cond2  && cond3;
	}

// function CurrentSessionIsCapableOfD2MShipments() // returns boolean
	function CurrentSessionIsCapableOfD2MShipments()
	{		
		return CurrentUserIsD2MEnabled() && CurrentShipperIsD2MEnabled();
	}

// function CurrentShipperIsD2MEnabled() // returns boolean
	function CurrentShipperIsD2MEnabled(){ 
	
		LogStartMethod("CurrentShipperIsD2MEnabled()");
		
		//var currentShipperSymbol = vm?.currentShipment?.PackageDefaults?.Shipper;
		
		var currentShipperSymbol =  $('select[ng-change="vm.shipperChange()"]').val().substring(7).toUpperCase();
		
		var authorizedD2MShipperList = [{"ShipperName": "Alight Solutions (Lincolnshire_D2M)","ShipperSymbol":"LINCOLNSHIRE_D2M"}];
		
		var infoMessage = "D2M shipping for current shipper symbol " + currentShipperSymbol + " is ";
		
		var result =  false;
		
		var isCurrentShipperEnabledForD2M = authorizedD2MShipperList.find(x => x.ShipperSymbol === currentShipperSymbol);
		
		result = (isCurrentShipperEnabledForD2M != undefined) ? true : false;
		
		infoMessage = result? infoMessage + "authorized" : "WARNING " + infoMessage + "NOT authorized";
		
		LogMethodInfo(infoMessage);
		
		return result;		 
    }

// function CurrentUserIsD2MEnabled() // returns boolean
	function CurrentUserIsD2MEnabled(){
		
		LogStartMethod("CurrentUserIsD2MEnabled()");
		
		var currentUserData = vm?.profile?.UserInformation?.Address.CustomData;
		
		var isD2MEnableForCurrentUser = GetUserCustomData(currentUserData, D2M_USER_CUSTOM_DATA_KEY);
		
		var infoMessage ="";
		
		var result =  false;
		
		if ($.isEmptyObject(isD2MEnableForCurrentUser) === false)
		{
				 var d2mCustomEntry = JSON.stringify(isD2MEnableForCurrentUser);
			 
				 var d2mEnabledValue = JSON.parse(d2mCustomEntry).Value;
			 
				 if (d2mEnabledValue.toUpperCase() === D2M_USER_ENABLED_VALUE)
				 {
					 infoMessage = "D2M User ENABLED";
					 result = true;
				 }
				 else
				 {
					infoMessage = "D2M User DISABLED";
					result = false;
				 }
		}
		else
		{
				 infoMessage = "WARNING:" + D2M_USER_CUSTOM_DATA_KEY + " NOT DETECTED";
		}
		
		LogMethodInfo(infoMessage);
		
		return result;
    }

        $saveShipmentProfileModal = angular.element('#saveShipmentProfileModal');
        $saveShipmentProfileModal.on('shown.bs.modal', function() {
            angular.element('[ng-model="vm.currentShippingProfile"]').focus();
            });
        $deleteShipmentProfileModal = angular.element('#deleteShipmentProfileModal');
        $processEODModal = angular.element('#processEODModal');
        
        vm.showSaveShippingProfileModal = function(shipmentRequest)
            {
            $saveShipmentProfileModal.modal('show');
            }

        vm.showDeleteShippingProfileModal = function(shipmentRequest)
            {
            $deleteShipmentProfileModal.modal('show');
            }
        
        vm.saveShippingProfile = function(shipmentRequest)
            {
            var selsvc = this.selectedServices[0].Symbol;
            shipmentRequest.Action = 'S';
            shipmentRequest.ShippingProfileName = vm.currentShippingProfile;
            shipmentRequest.SelService = selsvc;
            var data = { Data: JSON.stringify(shipmentRequest) };
            client.httpClient('UserMethod', data).then(
                function(ret) {
                var curprofilelist = JSON.parse(atob(ret.Data));
                vm.shippingProfiles = curprofilelist;
                })
            
            $saveShipmentProfileModal.modal('hide');
            }

        vm.deleteShippingProfile = function(shipmentRequest)
            {
            shipmentRequest.Action = 'D';
            shipmentRequest.ShippingProfileName = vm.currentShippingProfile;
            var data = { Data: JSON.stringify(shipmentRequest) };
            client.httpClient('UserMethod', data).then(
                function(ret) {
                var curprofilelist = JSON.parse(atob(ret.Data));
                vm.shippingProfiles = curprofilelist;
                })
            
            $deleteShipmentProfileModal.modal('hide');
            }

        vm.shippingProfileChange = function (shipmentRequest)
            {
            var tmpShippingProfile = vm.shippingProfiles.find(({ ShippingProfileName }) => ShippingProfileName === this.currentShippingProfile);
            var newShippingProfile = structuredClone(tmpShippingProfile);    
            if( newShippingProfile !== null && newShippingProfile !== undefined) {
                var selsvc = newShippingProfile.SelService;
                var myservice = {Symbol: selsvc };
                if( newShippingProfile.Packages[0].ProactiveRecovery === true) {
                    newShippingProfile.Packages[0].SelectedProactiveRecoveryInstructions = [4096,2048,32];                    
                }

                var today = new Date();
                var curdate = {Year: today.getFullYear(), Month: today.getMonth() + 1, Day: today.getDate()};
                newShippingProfile.PackageDefaults.Shipdate = curdate;
                this.currentShipment = newShippingProfile;
                this.selectedServices[0] = myservice;
                }
            }

        vm.CreateReturnLabelFromPrevious = function ()
            {
            vm.currentShipment = structuredClone(vm.lastShipmentRequest);
            vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].ReturnDelivery = true;
            vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].ReturnDeliveryMethod = 0;
            vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].ProactiveRecovery = false;
            vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].DirectDelivery = false;
            vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].Proof = false;
            vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].ProofRequireSignature = false; 
            vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Service = { Symbol: "CONNECTSHIP_UPS.UPS.2DA" };
            if (!vm.selectedServices) {
                vm.selectedServices = [];
            }
            vm.selectedServices.push(vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Service);
            };

        vm.showProcessEODModal = function(shipmentRequest)
            {
            $processEODModal.modal('show');
            }

        vm.ProcessEOD = function(shipmentRequest)
            {
            shipmentRequest.Action = 'EOD';
            var data = { Data: JSON.stringify(shipmentRequest) };
            client.httpClient('UserMethod', data).then(
                function(ret) {
                var eodresult = ret.Data;
                $processEODModal.modal('hide');                
                })
            }

        }

// vm.shippingProfileChange(shipmentRequest) // returns undefined
vm.shippingProfileChange = function (shipmentRequest)
            {
            var tmpShippingProfile = vm.shippingProfiles.find(({ ShippingProfileName }) => ShippingProfileName === this.currentShippingProfile);
            var newShippingProfile = structuredClone(tmpShippingProfile);    
            if( newShippingProfile !== null && newShippingProfile !== undefined) {
                var selsvc = newShippingProfile.SelService;
                var myservice = {Symbol: selsvc };
                if( newShippingProfile.Packages[0].ProactiveRecovery === true) {
                    newShippingProfile.Packages[0].SelectedProactiveRecoveryInstructions = [4096,2048,32];                    
                }

                var today = new Date();
                var curdate = {Year: today.getFullYear(), Month: today.getMonth() + 1, Day: today.getDate()};
                newShippingProfile.PackageDefaults.Shipdate = curdate;
                this.currentShipment = newShippingProfile;
                this.selectedServices[0] = myservice;
                }
            }

vm.CreateReturnLabelFromPrevious = function ()
            {
            vm.currentShipment = structuredClone(vm.lastShipmentRequest);
            vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].ReturnDelivery = true;
            vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].ReturnDeliveryMethod = 0;
            vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].ProactiveRecovery = false;
            vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].DirectDelivery = false;
            vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].Proof = false;
            vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].ProofRequireSignature = false; 
            vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Service = { Symbol: "CONNECTSHIP_UPS.UPS.2DA" };
            if (!vm.selectedServices) {
                vm.selectedServices = [];
            }
            vm.selectedServices.push(vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Service);
            };

// importerOfRecordSameAsConsignee(checked) // returns undefined
        function importerOfRecordSameAsConsignee(checked) {
            if (checked) {
                this.currentShipment.Packages[this.packageIndex].ImporterOfRecord = {
                    Company: this.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Company,
                    Contact: this.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Contact,
                    Address1: this.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Address1,
                    Address2: this.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Address2,
                    Address3: this.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Address3,
                    City: this.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Consignee.City,
                    StateProvince: this.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Consignee.StateProvince,
                    PostalCode: this.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Consignee.PostalCode,
                    Country: this.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Country
                }
            } else {
                this.currentShipment.Packages[this.packageIndex].ImporterOfRecord = {}
            }
        }

// addSameAsConsigneeCheckbox() // returns undefined
        function addSameAsConsigneeCheckbox () {
            var interval = setInterval(function(vm) {
                var $target = $(client.shipping.intl.importerOfRecordBtnSelector);
                if ($target.length) {
                    clearInterval(interval)
                    client.shipping.intl.$iorSameAsConsignee = $('<input type="checkbox">');
                    client.shipping.intl.$iorSameAsConsignee.click(function(e) { vm.importerOfRecordSameAsConsignee(e.target.checked) });
                    $target.before(client.shipping.intl.$iorSameAsConsignee, '<label style="padding-left: 6px;">Same As Consignee</label>');
                }
            }, 10, this)
        }

// this.PreShip(shipmentRequest, userParams) // returns void
this.PreShip = function(shipmentRequest, userParams) {
        shipmentRequest.SendViewModelToClient = this.GetViewModelFromTemplate;

	    // Verify all items have been packed
	    var omscheck = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference4;

	    // If OMS check for items not fully packed and prompt, otherwise disallow partial packs
	    if( omscheck == "OMS") {
	    	if( orderItemList !== null)	{
	    		var orderItemListCount1 = orderItemList.length;
	    		for (var i = 0; i < orderItemListCount1; i++) {
	    			if( orderItemList[i].qtyordered != orderItemList[i].qtyshipped ) {
	    				var msg = 'SKU: ' + orderItemList[i].itemsku + ' has not been fully packed. Click OK to continue or Cancel to continue packing.';
	    				var r = confirm(msg);
	    				if( r === false )
	    					throw Error("Ship cancelled - please continue packing.");
	    			}
	    		}
	    	}
	    } else {
	    	if( orderItemList !== null)	{
	    		var orderItemListCount = orderItemList.length;
	    		for (var j = 0; j < orderItemListCount; j++) {
	    			if( orderItemList[j].qtyordered != orderItemList[j].qtyshipped ) {
	    				var msg2 = 'SKU: ' + orderItemList[j].itemsku + ' has not been fully packed.';
	    				throw Error(msg2);
	    			}
	    		}
	    	}
	    }
	    var itempackedlist = JSON.stringify(orderItemList);

	    //alert("itempackedlist JSONized: " + itempackedlist);

  	    userParams.PACKEDDATA = itempackedlist;
        };

// this.handleItemSkuTextChanged(event) // returns void
this.handleItemSkuTextChanged = function(event) {

        var newitemsku = this.Packages[0].MiscReference10;
		if( newitemsku.trim().length === 0 )
			return;

        //debugger;
        
		//alert("Item number: " + orderItemList[1].itemcode + "  qtyordered: " + orderItemList[1].qtyordered + " qtyshipped: " + orderItemList[1].qtyshipped);

		// Check for item code SHIPCOMPLETE indicating that this order is complete
		if( newitemsku == "SHIPCOMPLETE") {

            vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference5 = "SHIPCOMPLETE";
		    //var pkg = sox_current_shipment.packages[sox_current_package_idx];
			//pkg.misc_reference_5 = "SHIPCOMPLETE";
			//$("#item_sku_txt").val("");			
            vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference10 = "";
			vm.checkShip();
			return;
		}

		// Check for SHIP indicating that this box is complete but not the whole order
		if( newitemsku == "SHIP") {
            vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference5 = "";		    
		    //var pkg = sox_current_shipment.packages[sox_current_package_idx];
			//pkg.misc_reference_5 = "";
			//$("#item_sku_txt").val("");			
            vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference10 = "";			
			vm.checkShip();
			return;
		}

		// Pad the input sku to 14 digits with leading zeros
		var skulen = newitemsku.length;
		var newitemskupad = "";
		if( skulen == 6)
			newitemskupad = '00000000' + newitemsku;
		else if( skulen == 7)
			newitemskupad = '0000000' + newitemsku;
		else if( skulen == 8)
			newitemskupad = '000000' + newitemsku;
		else if( skulen == 9)
			newitemskupad = '00000' + newitemsku;
		else if( skulen == 10)
			newitemskupad = '0000' + newitemsku;
		else if( skulen == 11)
			newitemskupad = '000' + newitemsku;
		else if( skulen == 12)
			newitemskupad = '00' + newitemsku;
		else if( skulen == 13)
			newitemskupad = '0' + newitemsku;
		else
			newitemskupad = newitemsku;
			
		newitemsku = newitemskupad;

		//alert("newitemsku: " + newitemsku);

        //alert("orderItemList length: " + orderItemList.length);
        
        //alert("orderItemList itemsku: " + orderItemList[0].itemsku);
       
       //debugger;
       
		// Verify item sku is on this order
		var itemFound = false;
		var orderItemListCount = orderItemList.length;
		for (var i = 0; i < orderItemListCount; i++) {
		    if( itemFound === true)
		        break;
			var skuarr = orderItemList[i].itemsku.split(",");
			for(var j = 0; j < skuarr.length; j++) {
				if( skuarr[j] == newitemsku ) {
					itemFound = true;
					break;
				}
			}
		}
		
		//alert("itemFound: " + itemFound);
		
		if( itemFound === false) {
			ShowAlert("Pack Error","This SKU (" + newitemsku + ") does not belong in this shipment. Please remove it before proceeding.");
            $("#mr10").css("background-color","Red");        	        				
            vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference10 = "";
            angular.element('[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference10"]').focus();    	                                
            return;			
		}

		// Search for itemcode
		itemFound = false;
		var fullyPacked = false;
		var svSkuCode = "";
		var orderItemListCount = orderItemList.length;
		for (var i = 0; i < orderItemListCount; i++) {
			if( itemFound == true)
				break;
			
			var nextitem = false;
			var skuarr = orderItemList[i].itemsku.split(",");
			for(var j = 0; j < skuarr.length; j++) {
				if( skuarr[j] == newitemsku ) {
					if( orderItemList[i].qtyshipped == orderItemList[i].qtyordered ) {
						fullyPacked = true;
						nextitem = true;
						break;
					} else {
						itemFound = true;
						fullyPacked = false;
						var tmpqtyshipped = Number(orderItemList[i].qtyshipped);
						var tmptotqtyshipped = Number(orderItemList[i].totqtyshipped);
						var tmpqtyordered = Number(orderItemList[i].qtyordered);
						if( (tmpqtyshipped + tmptotqtyshipped) < tmpqtyordered) {
							var calcqty1 = tmpqtyshipped + 1 + tmptotqtyshipped;
							var calcqty2 = tmpqtyordered - tmpqtyshipped - tmptotqtyshipped;
							/*alert("Calc quantity 1: " + calcqty1 + " qtyordered: " + tmpqtyordered);*/
							/*alert("Calc quantity 2: " + calcqty2);*/
							if( calcqty1 <= tmpqtyordered) {
								var tmpnewqty = tmpqtyshipped + 1;
								orderItemList[i].qtyshipped = tmpnewqty;
								orderItemList[i].modified = true;
								svSkuCode = newitemsku;
								/*alert("Item added to box ok");*/
							} else {
							    ShowAlert("Pack Error","Scanned quantity for SKU (" + newitemsku + ") would exceed order quantity. Please remove extras from the shipment and try again.");
								$("#mr10").css("background-color","Red");        	        				
                                vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference10 = "";
                                angular.element('[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference10"]').focus();    	                                
								return;						
							}
						} else {
							ShowAlert("Pack Alert","This item has been fully packed");
							$("#mr10").css("background-color","Red");        	        				
                            vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference10 = "";
                            angular.element('[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference10"]').focus();    	                                
							return;						
						}
					}
				}
			}
			if( nextitem == true)
				continue;
		}

		if( fullyPacked == true) {
			ShowAlert("Pack Alert","This item has been fully packed");
			$("#mr10").css("background-color","Red");        	        				
			vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference10 = "";
			angular.element('[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference10"]').focus();    	                                
			return;					
		}

		$("#mr10").css("background-color","Green");        	    	

		//if( itemFound == false) {
		//	ShowAlert("Pack Error 2","This SKU (" + newitemsku + ") does not belong in this shipment. Please remove it before proceeding.");
		//} else {
        //    $("#mr10").css("background-color","Green");        	    	
		//}

        vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference10 = "";
        angular.element('[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference10"]').focus();    	                                
		}

// function LoadCostCenter() // returns void
    function LoadCostCenter()
    {
        var currentUserData = vm?.profile?.UserInformation?.Address.CustomData;
        var costCenter = GetUserData(currentUserData, "CostCenter");
        if ($.isEmptyObject(costCenter) === false)
        {
             console.log ("CostCenter detected: " + JSON.stringify(costCenter));
             vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].ShipperReference = costCenter.Value;
             $('[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].ShipperReference"]').prop( "disabled", true );
        }
        else
        {
            console.log ("Error: CostCenter not found");
        }
    }

// this.NewShipment(shipmentRequest) // returns void
    this.NewShipment = function(shipmentRequest) { 
		debugger;
       shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ShipperReference =   this.GetCustom("Custom1", "User", shipmentRequest);
       shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ConsigneeReference =  this.GetCustom("Custom2", "User", shipmentRequest);
       // shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference1 =  this.GetCustom("Custom3", "User", shipmentRequest);
    };

// this.GetCustom(fieldName, customDataType, shipmentRequest) // returns string
    this.GetCustom = function(fieldName, customDataType, shipmentRequest) {
        var returnValue = "";
        var customData = null;
        if (customDataType === "User") {
            if (shipmentRequest &&
                shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults &&
                shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.OriginAddress &&
                shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.OriginAddress.CustomData)
                customData = shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.OriginAddress.CustomData;
        }

        if (customData) {
            customData.forEach(function(customField) {
                if (fieldName === customField.Key) returnValue = customField.Value;
            });
        }
        return returnValue;

    };

// GetCustom(fieldName, customDataType) // returns string
   GetCustom(fieldName, customDataType) {
      var returnValue = "";
      var customData = null;
      if (customDataType === "User") customData = this.ShipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.OriginAddress.CustomData;
      if (customDataType === "To") customData = this.ShipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.CustomData;

      if (customData) {
         customData.forEach(function (customField) {
            if (fieldName === customField.Key) returnValue = customField.Value;
         })
      }
      return returnValue;
   }

// GetEmail() // returns string
   GetEmail(){
      var emailText = "";
      var tags = document.getElementsByTagName("a"); 
      Array.from(tags).forEach(function(tag){
         if(tag.innerHTML.includes("Hello")) emailText = tag.innerHTML.replace("Hello", "").replace("!","").trim(); 
      });
      return emailText;
   }

// ShowAssignGoodsPane() // returns void
    ShowAssignGoodsPane()
    {
      let that = this;

      //get rid of any previous entries
      $('#listItemContainer li:gt(0)').remove();

      //change the column width to make the descriptions longer
      //change this back when the user clicks the 'Apply' button
      $('div.ui-tab-container').toggleClass('col-md-8 col-md-6').siblings('div').toggleClass('col-md-4 col-md-6')

      //set a reference to the packages object as well as the commodities objects
      this.packages = this.viewModel.currentShipment.Packages;
      this.goods = this.json.data.map(m => m.boxes).flat();
      this.goods.sort((a, b) => { return a.skuId - b.skuId });

      //loop the commodities to create a master list item for each
      $(this.goods).each(function(a, b)
      {
        let k = 'e' + (Math.random() + 1).toString(36).substring(2);
        b.UniqueId = k;

        //copy the source element
        let item = $('#liClone').clone(true).data(b);

        //change the id of the main containing element so we don't run into issue later
        //each clone is a discreet list item which corresponds to a commodity
        $(item).attr('id', k);

        //the customer is sending amounts that have sometimes 10 digits after the decimal point which is throwing exceptions when trying
        //to parseFloat so this is the simplest way to get around that.
        //let cost = Math.round(b.UnitValue.Amount * 100) / 100;

        $(item).find('.goods-sku').html('SKU: <strong>' + b.skuId + '</strong>');
        $(item).find('.goods-quantity').html('Quantity: <strong>' + b.quantity + '</strong>');
        $(item).find('.goods-declared-value').html('Unit Cost: <strong>$' + b.unitPrice + '</strong>');

        //append it to our list
        $('#divAssignCommodities ul.list-group').append(item);

        //assign all goods to the first package
        that.packages[0].CommodityContents.push(that.GetCommodityContentObject(b));

        //update the weight and declared value in the root of the object
        let weight = that.packages[0].Weight;
        let dva = that.packages[0].DeclaredValueAmount;
        const thisWeight = (+b.quantity * +b.weightLbs);
        const thisValue = (+b.quantity * +b.unitPrice);

        if (!weight.Amount) { weight.Amount = 0; }
        that.packages[0].Weight.Amount += (+b.quantity * +b.weightLbs).toFixed(2);

        if (!dva.Amount) { dva.Amount = 0; }
        that.packages[0].DeclaredValueAmount.Amount += Math.round((+b.quantity * +b.unitPrice) * 100) / 100;

        //show it gracefully
        $(item).show();
      });

      //that.UpdatePackageCounts();
      //$('li[heading=Goods] a:first').click();
      $('#divAssignCommodities').show().animate({ left: 0 }, 400);
      $('.scan-input:visible').first().focus();
      $('#divAssignCommodities').find('[data-toggle="tooltip"]').tooltip();
    }

// HideAssignGoodsPane() // returns void
    HideAssignGoodsPane()
    {
      let u = $('#divAssignCommodities').outerWidth() + 100;
      $('#divAssignCommodities').animate({ left: -u }, 400, function() { $(this).hide(); });
      $('div.ui-tab-container').toggleClass('col-md-8 col-md-6').siblings('div').toggleClass('col-md-4 col-md-6');
    }

// GetCommodityContentObject(data) // returns object
    GetCommodityContentObject(data)
    {
      let cc = {};
      cc.Quantity = data.quantity;
      cc.ProductCode = data.skuId;
      cc.QuantityUnitMeasure = 'EA';
      cc.UnitValue = { Currency: 'USD', Amount: +data.unitPrice };
      cc.UnitWeight = { Units: 'LB', Amount: +data.weightLbs };
      cc.UniqueId = data.UniqueId;
      cc.PkgIndex = data.PkgIndex || 1;
      cc.PVTotalWeight = (+data.quantity * +data.weightLbs);
      cc.PVTotalValue = (+data.quantity * +data.unitPrice);

      return cc;
    }

// MoveGoodToBox(li, destBox) // returns false|void
    MoveGoodToBox(li, destBox)
    {
      let vm = this.ClassViewModel;
      let that = this;
      let data = $(li).data();
      let destCC = this.packages[destBox - 1].CommodityContents || [];

      //find the box the item currently resides in
      //split this statement up over a few calls to make it easier to read
      let allGoods = this.packages.map(m => m.CommodityContents).flat();
      let item = allGoods.find(cc => cc.UniqueId == data.UniqueId);

      if (+item.PkgIndex == +destBox) { console.log('Item already exists in box.'); return false; }

      //remove the item from its current box
      this.packages[item.PkgIndex - 1].CommodityContents = this.packages[item.PkgIndex - 1].CommodityContents.filter(p => p.UniqueId != data.UniqueId);

      //add it to the new box
      item.PkgIndex = destBox;
      destCC.push(item);
      $(li).find('.pkg-index-text').fadeOut().promise().done(function(e) { $(this).text(destBox).fadeIn(); });

      //console.log(vm.currentShipment.Packages);
      $('li[heading="Goods"]:visible:first > a').trigger('click');
      $('#goods .btn-group').find('.btn:gt(0)').not('.active').first().trigger('click');

      //update the weights and values
      //this data will have changed by now so get a new reference to the object
      allGoods = this.packages.map(m => m.CommodityContents).flat();
      //the items array will have the CommodityContents object for every package in the shipment

      //sort by package index
      //update the weight and declared values for all the packages in the shipment
      allGoods = allGoods.sort((a, b) => { return a.PkgIndex - b.PkgIndex });
      $(allGoods).each(function(a, b)
      {
        let pkg = that.packages[b.PkgIndex - 1];

        if ((a == 0) || (b.PkgIndex != allGoods[a - 1].PkgIndex))
        {
          pkg.Weight.Amount = 0;
          pkg.DeclaredValueAmount.Amount = 0;
        }

        pkg.Weight.Amount += +b.PVTotalWeight;
        pkg.DeclaredValueAmount.Amount += +b.PVTotalValue;
      });
    }

// InitiateDelegates() // returns void
    InitiateDelegates()
    {
      let that = this

      $('body').delegate('#btnAssignCommodities', 'click', function()
      {
        if ($('#divAssignCommodities:visible').length > 0) return;
        that.ShowAssignGoodsPane();
      });

      $('body').delegate('#btnApplyCommodityAssignments', 'click', function(e)
      {
        that.ApplyCommodityAssignments();
      });

      $('body').delegate('#btnCancelAssignGoods', 'click', function(e)
      {
        that.HideAssignGoodsPane();
      });

      $('body').delegate('.assign-to-new-box', 'click', function(e)
      {
        let li = $(e.target).closest('li');
        $('button[ng-click="vm.addPackage();"]').trigger('click').promise().done((e) =>
        {
          const cp = +$('#spanCurrentPackageIndex').text();
          that.MoveGoodToBox(li, cp);
        });
      });

      $('body').delegate('.assign-to-current-box', 'click', function(e)
      {
        let li = $(e.target).closest('li');
        const cp = +$('#spanCurrentPackageIndex').text();
        that.MoveGoodToBox(li, cp);
      });

      $('body').delegate('.undo-box-assignment', 'click', function(e)
      {
        let li = $(e.target).closest('li');
        that.MoveGoodToBox(li, 1);
      });

    }

// Source: Asia Waterjet FZCO (ASIAWATERJETFZCO)_Asia_WaterJet_CBR_1870.cs
// PageLoaded(location) // returns void
this.PageLoaded = function(location) {
        //22 May 2023 - Below Code (Line 4 to 7) is added to navigate to Shipping screen on login instead of Welcome Screen.
        if (location === '/') {
            document.location = '#!/shipping';
        }

        $(".dropdown-menu li:first a").text("Shipping");
        if (location === '/shipping') {
            //06 June 2023 - Below Code (Line 14 to 20) is added to remove the unwanted weight Units.
            $(document).ready(function() {
                setTimeout(function() {
                    $('select:eq(24) option[label="OZ"]').remove();
                    $('select:eq(24) option[label="MG"]').remove();
                    $('select:eq(24) option[label="G"]').remove();
                }, 1500);
            });

           
            this.vm.returnStatus = this.GetReturnStatus();
            
            var UserCountry=this.vm.profile.UserInformation.Address.Country.toLowerCase();
            pickuplink='https://www.ups.com/'+ UserCountry +'/en/business-solutions/pickup-dropoff-options/ups-on-call-pickup.page';
             var desc = [
                '<span style="font-weight:bold;">Instructions</span><br>Shipments using service level as UPS Worldwide Express Freight must be palletized, stackable, fork-liftable, shrink-wrapped and banded to the skip.<br/>Shipments destined to Saudi Arabia must be packaged separately.<br/><b>For shipments originating from USA:</b><br>i.	Email all export documents ( Ex : Invoice, Shipper’s export declaration and packing list) to <a href="mailto:internationaldocs.us@ups.com">internationaldocs.us@ups.com</a> with the tracking number as the subject header of the email on the same day the shipment is picked up<br>ii.	For shipments valued over USD 2,500: <br>1.	Shippers filing directly with the Census Bureau must supply the AES Internal Transaction Number (ITN) at the time of pickup by UPS. The ITN should be placed on the label or on the invoice as close to the total value as possible.<br>2.	UPS can file the AES information on behalf of the shipper for a fee. The shipper must supply all necessary information for the filing, including their EIN number, License/License Exemption/License Exception and Export Control Classification Number (ECCN).<br><b>For shipments originating from EU countries:</b><br>i.	Shippers Export Declaration (SED)/ Export Procedure:<br>1.	First step: the exporter or his representative has to lodge an export declaration at the customs house of export responsible for supervising the place where the exporter is established. The customs house of export is responsible for granting the release for export and issue an Export Accompanying Document (EAD) with a unique Movement Reference Number (MRN).<br>2.	Second step: the carrier launches the MRN electronically to the customs house of exit that is responsible to supervise the physical export.<br><b>Please contact your local UPS customer care to schedule a pick-up at your convenience.'
            ];
            
            var name = document.querySelector("body > div.main-container > div.container-fluid.body-content.body > div > div.ng-scope > div > div > div:nth-child(2)");
            name.appendChild(document.createElement('div')).innerHTML = desc;
            
            alert('Please click on "Close Manifest" to transfer all your shipping information to UPS.')
        }
		
		 if (location === '/closemanifest') {
        $('.panel-footer').append('<div style="margin-left:10px"><b>For scheduling pick-up, please <a target="_blank" href="'+ pickuplink +'">click here</a> to access the contact details of nearest UPS center.</div>'); 
    
    }
    }

// PreShip(shipmentRequest, userParams) // returns void
this.PreShip = function(shipmentRequest, userParams) {

        var freightfound = 0;
        var frieghterr = 0;

        for (var i = 0; i <= shipmentRequest.Packages.length - 1; i++) {
            if (parseInt(shipmentRequest.Packages[i].Weight.Amount) >= 70) {
                freightfound = "1";
            }
            if (freightfound == "1") {
                if (parseInt(shipmentRequest.Packages[i].Weight.Amount) < 70) {
                    frieghterr = "1";
                }
            }
        }
        if (freightfound == "0") {
            shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Service = {
                Symbol: "CONNECTSHIP_UPS.UPS.EXPSVR"
            }
        } else {
            if (frieghterr == "0") {
                shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Service = {
                    Symbol: "CONNECTSHIP_UPS.UPS.EXPFRT"
                }
            } else {
                alert("Cannot create one shipment with 2 different service levels.");
            }
        }
        for (var i = 0; i <= shipmentRequest.Packages.length - 1; i++) {
            if (shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Service.Symbol == "CONNECTSHIP_UPS.UPS.EXPFRT") {
                shipmentRequest.Packages[i].Packaging = "CUSTOMER_PALLET";
            }
            shipmentRequest.Packages[i].ImportDelivery = true;

        }
        if (shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.OriginAddress.Country == "US") {
            if ($('select[name="CarrierInstructions"]').val() == '?') {
                alert("Please confirm shipment value");
                throw ("Excpetion");
            } else {
                if (shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ConsigneeReference == null || shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ConsigneeReference == "") {
                    if ($('select[name="CarrierInstructions"]').val() == 'string:Yes') {
                        alert("Please Enter ITN/ EES number in ConsigneeReference");
                        throw ("Excpetion");
                    }
                }
            }
        } else {
            if (shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.OriginAddress.Country != "undefined") {
                alert("For EU Exports : Shipments above 1000 EUR, a formal export declaration is required. A formal electronic export declaration must be sent to customs authorities by the exporter or their representative. Customs authorities grant the release for export and issue an Export Accompanying Document (EAD) with a unique Movement Reference Number (MRN). The EAD has to accompany the shipment. UPS is responsible for the exit clearance at the EU border.")
            }
        }
    }

// Source: Barnes & Noble Education, Inc. (BNEDUCAT)_BarnesAndNoble Client BR_1588.cs
// PreShip(shipmentRequest, userParams) // returns void
this.PreShip = function(shipmentRequest, userParams) {   
        var cont = this.ValidateShipment(shipmentRequest);
        if(!cont){
            throw {errorCode:999,message:"You cannot ship  greater than 50lb."};
        }
    }

// ValidateShipment(shipmentRequest) // returns boolean
this.ValidateShipment = function(shipmentRequest){
    var weight = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].Weight;
    var weightLimit = 0;
    var totalWeight = 0;
            weightLimit = 50;
    var i;
    for(i = 0; i < shipmentRequest.Packages.length; i++)
    {
        var pkgWeight = parseFloat(shipmentRequest.Packages[i].Weight.Amount);
        if(pkgWeight > weightLimit){
           return confirm("One or more packages is 50lb or greater.  Are you sure you want to continue?");
        //throw {errorCode:999,message:"You cannot ship  greater than " + weightLimit + " " + weight.Units + "."};
    } else{
        return true;
    }
    }

}

// ValidatePackage(pkg) // returns void
this.ValidatePackage = function(pkg){
    debugger;
    var weight = pkg.Weight;
    var weightLimit = 0;
    var totalWeight = 0;
            weightLimit = 50;

        var pkgWeight = parseFloat(pkg.Weight.Amount);
        if(pkgWeight > weightLimit){
            alert("Previous package weight is greater than 50lb.");
        } 
    }

// Source: BHARTIYA HANDICRAFTS (BHARTIYAHCFT)_ISMEA_FTP_1584.cs
// getFTPUploaded() // returns void
function getFTPUploaded() {
        var selectedShipper = document.getElementById("Shipper").value;
		var shipper = '';
		debugger;
		if (selectedShipper !== "")
		{
			selectedShipper = JSON.parse(selectedShipper);
			shipper = selectedShipper.Name;
		}
        var data = { Action: 'ExportFTP', Shipper: shipper };

        $.post('api/ShippingService/UserMethod',
            {UserContext: userContext, Data: JSON.stringify(data) },
            function(response, status, xhr) {
            }
        ).done(function(response) {
            debugger;
            var resp = JSON.stringify(response);
            resp = JSON.parse(resp);
            debugger;
            if (resp.Data !== "" && resp.Data !== undefined)
            {
                alert('Lastest File: \n' + DecodeReturnString(resp.Data).substring(0,resp.Data.length -1));
            }
            else if (resp.ErrorMessage !== undefined)
            {
                if (resp.ErrorCode == '104')
                {
                    alert('Lastest File: \nNo files found!');
                }
                else
                {
                    alert(resp.ErrorMessage);
                }
            }
        });
    }

// Source: Boston Scientific (BOSTON)_Admin_Profile_CBR_2481.cs
// function(shipmentRequest, userParams) // returns void
    this.PreShip = function(shipmentRequest, userParams) {  
     // We will require the actual shipment to send weight and dims in kg/cm
     // However, because US Vendors are sending the product the client gui needs to be in Lb/In.
    
      debugger;
      
       //cm=in/0.39370
     this.vm.currentShipment.Packages.forEach(pkg => {
         
         if(pkg.Dimensions === undefined || pkg.Dimensions.Units === undefined ||  pkg.Dimensions.Length === undefined ||  pkg.Dimensions.Width === undefined ||  pkg.Dimensions.Height === undefined){
           throw Error('ERROR:' + " Missing Dimensions");
         }
         
         
         if (pkg.Dimensions.Units === 0){
             pkg.Dimensions.Length = Number(pkg.Dimensions.Length/0.39370).toFixed(2);
             pkg.Dimensions.Width = Number(pkg.Dimensions.Width/0.39370).toFixed(2);
             pkg.Dimensions.Height = Number(pkg.Dimensions.Height/0.39370).toFixed(2);
             pkg.Dimensions.Units = 1;
         }
         
     });
      
      
     //kg = lbs*0.453592    
     this.vm.currentShipment.Packages.forEach(pkg => {
         if (pkg.Weight.Units === "LB"){
             pkg.Weight.Amount = Number(pkg.Weight.Amount * 0.453592).toFixed(2);
             pkg.Weight.Units = "KG";
         }
         
     });
     
      if(shipmentRequest.Packages[0].AesTransactionNumber !== null){
              shipmentRequest.Packages[0].Comments = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].Comments + "\n ITN/AES Filer " + shipmentRequest.Packages[0].AesTransactionNumber;
             
          }
   
    }

// Source: Boston Scientific (BOSTON)_Boston Coyol Client Business Rules_2474.cs
// this.PreShip(shipmentRequest, userParams) // returns void
this.PreShip = function(shipmentRequest, userParams) {    
  
    // We will require the actual shipment to send weight and dims in kg/cm
    // However, because US Vendors are sending the product the client gui needs to be in Lb/In.
    
    debugger;
    //kg = lbs*0.453592 
    totalShipWeight = 0;
    totalVolumetricResult = 0;
    
    vm.currentShipment.Packages.forEach(pkg => {
        totalShipWeight += Number(pkg.Weight.Amount);
        totalVolumetricResult += ((Number(pkg.Dimensions.Length).toFixed(2)*Number(pkg.Dimensions.Width).toFixed(2)*Number(pkg.Dimensions.Height)).toFixed(2))/166;
    });
              
    totalShipWeight = Number(totalShipWeight).toFixed(2);
    console.log(totalShipWeight);
    console.log(totalVolumetricResult);
    if (totalShipWeight > 150)
    {
        alert("Total Shipment Weight Exceeds Shipment Weight Limit of 150lbs")
        throw new Error("Shipping halted due to Over Maximum Weight Rule " + totalShipWeight);
    }
    
    if (totalVolumetricResult > Number(maxvolumetric))
    {
        alert("Total Shipment Weight Exceeds Total Shipment Volumetric Weight Limit of " + Number(maxvolumetric))
        throw new Error("Shipping halted due to Total Shipment Volumetric Weight Rule " + Number(totalVolumetricResult).toFixed(2));
    }
    
     vm.currentShipment.Packages.forEach(pkg => {
         if (pkg.Weight.Units === "LB"){
             pkg.Weight.Amount = Number(pkg.Weight.Amount * 0.453592).toFixed(2);
             pkg.Weight.Units = "KG";
         }
         
     });
     
    //cm=in/0.39370
     vm.currentShipment.Packages.forEach(pkg => {
         if (pkg.Dimensions.Units === 0){
             pkg.Dimensions.Length = Number(pkg.Dimensions.Length/0.39370).toFixed(2)
             pkg.Dimensions.Width = Number(pkg.Dimensions.Width/0.39370).toFixed(2)
             pkg.Dimensions.Height = Number(pkg.Dimensions.Height/0.39370).toFixed(2)
             pkg.Dimensions.Units = 1;
         }
         
     });
     
     
    // debugger;
      if(Number(vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].DeclaredValueCustoms.Amount).toFixed(2) > 2500 ){
          if(vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].ExportInformationCode === null){
              vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].ExportInformationCode = "OS";
          }
          if(vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].AesTransactionNumber === null){
              vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].SedMethod = 2;
              $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].AesTransactionNumber"]').focus();
              throw new Error('Missing AES/ITN Number');
          } 
          if(shipmentRequest.Packages[0].AesTransactionNumber !== null){
              shipmentRequest.Packages[0].Comments = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].Comments + "\n ITN/AES Filer " + shipmentRequest.Packages[0].AesTransactionNumber;
             
          }
      }
     
    console.log(shipmentRequest);
  
};

// this.ShippingLoaded() // returns void
this.ShippingLoaded = function(){
    this.vm.populateReturnAddress = this.PopulateReturnAddress;
    this.vm.populateShipToAddress = this.PopulateShipToAddress;
    this.vm.serviceOption = serviceOption;
    this.vm.serviceOptions = serviceOptions(this.vm.profile);
    this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].ShipperReference = user_orderNumber;
    this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].MiscReference1 = user_orderNumber;
    this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].ConsigneeReference = cost_Center;
    this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].MiscReference2 = cost_Center;
    this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].MiscReference3 = user_partNumber;
    this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].Description = user_description;
   

    function serviceOption() {
        this.selectedServices = [this.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Service];
    }
    function serviceOptions(profile) {
        //debugger;
        var filterServices = [];
        var customData3 = uPS_Service.split(',');
        for (var item of customData3) {
            var symbol = getServiceSymbol(item.toLowerCase());
            for (var service of profile.Services) {
                if (service.Symbol === symbol) {
                    service.Name = service.Name.replace('(UPS Adapter)','').trim();
                    if (service.Name.includes("Expedited")){
                        service.Name = service.Name + " (MAIN SERVICE)";
                    }
                    if (service.Name.includes("Saver")){
                        service.Name = service.Name + " (Only with Boston's Authorization)";
                    }
                    filterServices.push(service);
                    break;
                }
            }
        }
        return filterServices;
        function getServiceSymbol(code) {
            if (code == '2dn') return 'UPSAPI.UPS.2DA'
            else if (code == '3dd') return 'UPSAPI.UPS.3DS'
            else if (code == 'exp') return 'UPSAPI.UPS.EXPEDITED'
            else if (code == 'ess') return 'UPSAPI.UPS.EXPRESS'
            else if (code == 'nda') return 'UPSAPI.UPS.NDA'
            else if (code == 'dae') return 'UPSAPI.UPS.NDAEAM'
            else if (code == 'grn') return 'UPSAPI.UPS.GND'
            else if (code == 'uwe') return 'UPSAPI.UPS.EXPEDITED'
            else if (code == 'wep') return 'UPSAPI.UPS.EXPRESSSP'
            else if (code == 'swe') return 'UPSAPI.UPS.EXPRESS'
            else if (code == 'uws') return 'UPSAPI.UPS.SAVER'
            else if (code == 'std') return 'UPSAPI.UPS.STANDARD'
        }
        
    }
    
    if(dims.includes(',')){
        var dimensions = dims.split(',');
        this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].Weight.Amount = Number(dimensions[0]);
        maxvolumetric = Number(dimensions[4]);
        console.log("Max Volumetric: " + maxvolumetric);
        this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].Dimensions = {
            Length: Number(dimensions[1]),
            Height: Number(dimensions[2]),
            Width: Number(dimensions[3]),
            Units: 0
        };
    }
   
    vm = this.vm;
};

// this.NewShipment(shipmentRequest) // returns void
this.NewShipment = function(shipmentRequest) { 
  // debugger;
  
    this.vm.populateReturnAddress = this.PopulateReturnAddress;
    this.vm.populateShipToAddress = this.PopulateShipToAddress
  
    $('#sf_Address').focus();
    $("#sf_Address").prop("selectedIndex", 0);
    $("#st_Address").prop("selectedIndex", 0);
   // $('#billable_weight_text').html(0.00 + ' Lbs');
   // $('#volumetric_value_text').html(0.00 +' Lbs');
    
   
    this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].ShipperReference = user_orderNumber;
    this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].MiscReference1 = user_orderNumber;
    this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].ConsigneeReference = cost_Center;
    this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].MiscReference2 = cost_Center;
    this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].MiscReference3 = user_partNumber;
    this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].Description = user_description;
    //debugger;
     this.vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Service = {
         Symbol:"UPSAPI.UPS.EXPEDITED"
     };
     
     this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].SedMethod = 2;
     this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].AesTransactionNumber = null;
     this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].ExportInformationCode = 'OS';
     this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].DeclaredValueCustoms.Amount = null;
     
    

};

// this.AddPackage(shipmentRequest, packageIndex) // returns void
this.AddPackage = function(shipmentRequest, packageIndex) {
    // debugger;
    
        shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex].ShipperReference = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ShipperReference;
        shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex].ConsigneeReference = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ConsigneeReference;
        shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex].MiscReference1 = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference1;
        shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex].MiscReference2 = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference2;
        shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex].MiscReference3 = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference3;
        shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex].Packaging = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].Packaging;
        shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex].Description = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].Description;
        shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex].AesTransactionNumber = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].AesTransactionNumber;
        shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex].ExportInformationCode = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ExportInformationCode;
        shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex].SedMethod = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].SedMethod;
}

// PreShip(shipmentRequest, userParams) // returns undefined
this.PreShip = function(shipmentRequest, userParams) {    
    // We will require the actual shipment to send weight and dims in kg/cm
    // However, because US Vendors are sending the product the client gui needs to be in Lb/In.
    
    // debugger;
    
    totalShipWeight = 0;
    totalVolumetricResult = 0;
    
    vm.currentShipment.Packages.forEach(pkg => {
        totalShipWeight += Number(pkg.Weight.Amount);
        totalVolumetricResult += ((Number(pkg.Dimensions.Length).toFixed(2)*Number(pkg.Dimensions.Width).toFixed(2)*Number(pkg.Dimensions.Height)).toFixed(2))/166;
    });
              
    totalShipWeight = Number(totalShipWeight).toFixed(2);
    console.log(totalShipWeight);
    console.log(totalVolumetricResult);
    if (totalShipWeight > 150)
    {
        alert("Total Shipment Weight Exceeds Shipment Weight Limit of 150lbs")
        throw new Error("Shipping halted due to Over Maximum Weight Rule " + totalShipWeight);
    }
    
    if (totalVolumetricResult > Number(maxvolumetric))
    {
        alert("Total Shipment Weight Exceeds Total Shipment Volumetric Weight Limit of " + Number(maxvolumetric))
        throw new Error("Shipping halted due to Total Shipment Volumetric Weight Rule " + Number(totalVolumetricResult).toFixed(2));
    }
    
    //kg = lbs*0.453592    
    vm.currentShipment.Packages.forEach(pkg => {
         if (pkg.Weight.Units === "LB"){
             pkg.Weight.Amount = Number(pkg.Weight.Amount * 0.453592).toFixed(2);
             pkg.Weight.Units = "KG";
         }
         
    });
    
  
    //cm=in/0.39370
    vm.currentShipment.Packages.forEach(pkg => {
         if (pkg.Dimensions.Units === 0){
             pkg.Dimensions.Length = Number(pkg.Dimensions.Length/0.39370).toFixed(2)
             pkg.Dimensions.Width = Number(pkg.Dimensions.Width/0.39370).toFixed(2)
             pkg.Dimensions.Height = Number(pkg.Dimensions.Height/0.39370).toFixed(2)
             pkg.Dimensions.Units = 1;
       }
         
    });
     
   if(Number(shipmentRequest.Packages[0].DeclaredValueCustoms.Amount).toFixed(2) > 2500 ){
          if(shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ExportInformationCode === null){
              shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ExportInformationCode = "OS";
          }
          if(shipmentRequest.Packages[0].AesTransactionNumber === null){
              shipmentRequest.Packages[0].SedMethod = 2;
              $('input[type=text][ng-model="shipmentRequest.Packages[this.vm.packageIndex].AesTransactionNumber"]').focus();
              throw new Error('Missing AES/ITN Number');
          } 
          
          if(shipmentRequest.Packages[0].AesTransactionNumber !== null){
              shipmentRequest.Packages[0].Comments = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].Comments + "\n ITN/AES Filer " + shipmentRequest.Packages[0].AesTransactionNumber;
             
          }
      }
};

// ShippingLoaded() // returns undefined
this.ShippingLoaded = function(){
    this.vm.populateReturnAddress = this.PopulateReturnAddress;
    this.vm.populateShipToAddress = this.PopulateShipToAddress;
    this.vm.serviceOption = serviceOption;
    this.vm.serviceOptions = serviceOptions(this.vm.profile);
    this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].ShipperReference = cost_Center;
    this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].MiscReference1 = cost_Center;
    //this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].ConsigneeReference = po_number;
    //this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].MiscReference2 = po_Number;
    this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].MiscReference3 = user_partNumber;
    this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].Description = user_description;
  
    function serviceOption() {
        this.selectedServices = [this.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Service];
    }
    function serviceOptions(profile) {
        //debugger;
        var filterServices = [];
        var customData3 = uPS_Service.split(',');
        for (var item of customData3) {
            var symbol = getServiceSymbol(item.toLowerCase());
            for (var service of profile.Services) {
                if (service.Symbol === symbol) {
                    //service.Name = service.Name.replace('(UPS Adapter)','').trim();
                    filterServices.push(service);
                    break;
                }
            }
        }
        return filterServices;
        function getServiceSymbol(code) {
             if (code == '2dn') return 'UPSAPI.UPS.2DA'
            else if (code == '3dd') return 'UPSAPI.UPS.3DS'
            else if (code == 'exp') return 'UPSAPI.UPS.EXPEDITED'
            else if (code == 'ess') return 'UPSAPI.UPS.EXPRESS'
            else if (code == 'nda') return 'UPSAPI.UPS.NDA'
            else if (code == 'dae') return 'UPSAPI.UPS.NDAEAM'
            else if (code == 'grn') return 'UPSAPI.UPS.GND'
            else if (code == 'uwe') return 'UPSAPI.UPS.EXPEDITED'
            else if (code == 'wep') return 'UPSAPI.UPS.EXPRESSSP'
            else if (code == 'swe') return 'UPSAPI.UPS.EXPRESS'
            else if (code == 'uws') return 'UPSAPI.UPS.SAVER'
            else if (code == 'std') return 'UPSAPI.UPS.STANDARD'
        }
        
    }
    
    if(dims.includes(',')){
        var dimensions = dims.split(',');
        
        this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].Weight.Amount = Number(dimensions[0]);
        maxvolumetric = Number(dimensions[4]);
        console.log("Max Volumetric: " + maxvolumetric);
        this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].Dimensions = {
            Length: Number(dimensions[1]),
            Height: Number(dimensions[2]),
            Width: Number(dimensions[3]),
            Units: 0
        };
    }
    vm = this.vm;
};

// GetShipperAccount() // returns undefined
this.GetShipperAccount = function(){
    //debugger;
    var shippers = this.vm.profile.Shippers;
    shippers.forEach(shipper => {
       if(shipper.Name === "Boston Scientific HEREDIA"){
           var shipperCustomData = shipper.CustomData;
            shipperCustomData.forEach(item => {
                 if(item.Key === "Account"){
                     thisShipperAccount = item.Value;
                     
                 }
                 
            });  
        } 
        else{
            throw ({ message: 'No Shipper Found for User Profile', errorCode: '' });
        }
    });
};

// GetCustomDataItems() // returns undefined
this.GetCustomDataItems = function(){
    //debugger;
    userCustomData = this.vm.profile.UserInformation.Address.CustomData;
   
    st_AddressType = client.getValueByKey('Custom1',userCustomData);   
    sf_AddressType = client.getValueByKey('Custom2',userCustomData);  
    uPS_Service = client.getValueByKey('Custom3',userCustomData);        
    return_Type = client.getValueByKey('Custom4',userCustomData);            
    user_description = client.getValueByKey('Custom5',userCustomData);             
    dims = client.getValueByKey('Custom6',userCustomData);                   
    user_orderNumber = client.getValueByKey('Custom7',userCustomData);     
    cost_Center = client.getValueByKey('Custom8',userCustomData);        
    user_partNumber = client.getValueByKey('Custom9',userCustomData);     
    insured_Value = client.getValueByKey('Custom10',userCustomData);     
    
    
    
};

// GetShipToAddresses() // returns address book entries array
this.GetShipToAddresses = function(){
    var payloadShipToAddress = {
        "Skip": 0,
        "Take": 10,
        "WhereClauses": [{
            "FieldName": "Group",
            "FieldValue": "2",
            "Operator": 0
        }]
    };
    
    var data = {
        CompanyId: client.userContext.CompanyId,
        addressBookIds: shipToAddressBookId,
        SearchCriteria: payloadShipToAddress
    };
    //console.log(data);
  
    ShipToAddressBook = client.thinClientAPIRequest('GetAddressBookEntries_AddressBook', data, false).responseJSON;

    console.log(ShipToAddressBook.AddressBookEntries);
    
    return ShipToAddressBook.AddressBookEntries;
            
};

// GetShipFromAddresses() // returns address book entries array
this.GetShipFromAddresses = function(){
    var payloadShipFromAddress = {
        "Skip": 0,
        "Take": 0,
        "WhereClauses": [{
           "FieldName": "Code",
                    "FieldValue": sf_AddressType,   //'ze-'
                    "Operator": 6
                }]
    };
 
    var sfdata = {
        CompanyId: client.userContext.CompanyId,
        addressBookIds: shipFromAddressBookId,
        SearchCriteria: payloadShipFromAddress
    };
   
    ShipFromAddressBook = client.thinClientAPIRequest('GetAddressBookEntries_AddressBook', sfdata, false).responseJSON;
    
     //debugger;
    
    for(let i = 0; i < ShipFromAddressBook.AddressBookEntries.length; i++){
    
        ShipFromAddressBook.AddressBookEntries[i].Code = ShipFromAddressBook.AddressBookEntries[i].Code.replace("&amp;",'&');
        ShipFromAddressBook.AddressBookEntries[i].Company = ShipFromAddressBook.AddressBookEntries[i].Company.replace("&amp;",'&');
   }


    console.log(ShipFromAddressBook.AddressBookEntries);
    
    return ShipFromAddressBook.AddressBookEntries;
};

// NewShipment(shipmentRequest) // returns undefined
this.NewShipment = function(shipmentRequest) { 
    // debugger;
    this.vm.populateReturnAddress = this.PopulateReturnAddress;
    this.vm.populateShipToAddress = this.PopulateShipToAddress
   
    $('#sf_Address').focus();
    $("#sf_Address").prop("selectedIndex", 0);
    $("#st_Address").prop("selectedIndex", 0);
   // $('#billable_weight_text').html(0.00 + ' Lbs');
  //  $('#volumetric_value_text').html(0.00 +' Lbs');
   
    this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].ShipperReference = cost_Center;
    this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].MiscReference1 = cost_Center;
    //this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].ConsigneeReference = po_Number;
    //this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].MiscReference2 = po_Number;
    this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].MiscReference3 = user_partNumber;
    this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].Description = user_description;
    
    this.vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Service = {
         Symbol:"UPSAPI.UPS.SAVER"
    };
    this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].SedMethod = 2;
    this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].AesTransactionNumber = null;
    this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].ExportInformationCode = 'OS';
    this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].DeclaredValueCustoms.Amount = null;
  
};

// AddPackage(shipmentRequest, packageIndex) // returns undefined
this.AddPackage = function(shipmentRequest, packageIndex) {
     //debugger;
    shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex].ShipperReference = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ShipperReference;
    shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex].ConsigneeReference = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ConsigneeReference;
    shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex].MiscReference1 = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference1;
    shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex].MiscReference2 = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference2;
    shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex].MiscReference3 = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference3;
    //shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex].MiscReference4 = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference4;
    shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex].Packaging = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].Packaging;
    shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex].Description = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].Description;
    shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex].AesTransactionNumber = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].AesTransactionNumber;
    shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex].ExportInformationCode = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ExportInformationCode;
    shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex].SedMethod = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].SedMethod;

}

// RemovePackage(shipmentRequest, packageIndex) // returns undefined
this.RemovePackage = function(shipmentRequest, packageIndex) {
      
      var totalShipWeight = 0;
      vm.currentShipment.Packages.forEach(pkg => {
        totalShipWeight += Number(pkg.Weight.Amount);
      });
      totalShipWeight = Number(totalShipWeight).toFixed(2);
      document.getElementById('totWgt').innerHTML = totalShipWeight;
      
      var totalVolumetricResult = 0;
      vm.currentShipment.Packages.forEach(pkg => {
           totalVolumetricResult += ((Number(pkg.Dimensions.Length).toFixed(2)*Number(pkg.Dimensions.Width).toFixed(2)*Number(pkg.Dimensions.Height)).toFixed(2))/166;
      });
      totalVolumetricResult = Number(totalVolumetricResult).toFixed(2);
      $('#volumetric_value_text').html(totalVolumetricResult+' Lbs');
      document.getElementById('totVolumeWgt').innerHTML = totalVolumetricResult;
      if (totalVolumetricResult > Number(maxvolumetric))
        {
           $('#totVolumeWgt').html('<span>'+totalVolumetricResult+' Lbs <br> <small style="color:red;font-weight:normal;">Weight Over Maximum Allowed Please Review</small></span>');
           throw ({ 'Shipping halted due to Over Maximum Weight Rule': 'Shipping halted due to Over Maximum Weight Rule' });
        }
  
      
}

// Source: Boston Scientific (BOSTON)_Boston_MULTI_2485.cs
// this.PreShip(shipmentRequest, userParams) // returns void
this.PreShip = function(shipmentRequest, userParams) {    
  
     // We will require the actual shipment to send weight and dims in kg/cm
     // However, because US Vendors are sending the product the client gui needs to be in Lb/In.
    
     // debugger;
     
     totalShipWeight = 0;
    totalVolumetricResult = 0;
    
    vm.currentShipment.Packages.forEach(pkg => {
        totalShipWeight += Number(pkg.Weight.Amount);
        totalVolumetricResult += ((Number(pkg.Dimensions.Length).toFixed(2)*Number(pkg.Dimensions.Width).toFixed(2)*Number(pkg.Dimensions.Height)).toFixed(2))/166;
    });
              
    totalShipWeight = Number(totalShipWeight).toFixed(2);
    console.log(totalShipWeight);
    console.log(totalVolumetricResult);
    if (totalShipWeight > 150)
    {
        alert("Total Shipment Weight Exceeds Shipment Weight Limit of 150lbs")
        throw new Error("Shipping halted due to Over Maximum Weight Rule " + totalShipWeight);
    }
    
    if (totalVolumetricResult > Number(maxvolumetric))
    {
        alert("Total Shipment Weight Exceeds Total Shipment Volumetric Weight Limit of " + Number(maxvolumetric))
        throw new Error("Shipping halted due to Total Shipment Volumetric Weight Rule " + Number(totalVolumetricResult).toFixed(2));
    }
     
     //kg = lbs*0.453592    
     vm.currentShipment.Packages.forEach(pkg => {
         if (pkg.Weight.Units === "LB"){
             pkg.Weight.Amount = Number(pkg.Weight.Amount * 0.453592).toFixed(2);
             pkg.Weight.Units = "KG";
         }
         
     });
     
    //cm=in/0.39370
     vm.currentShipment.Packages.forEach(pkg => {
         if (pkg.Dimensions.Units === 0){
             pkg.Dimensions.Length = Number(pkg.Dimensions.Length/0.39370).toFixed(2)
             pkg.Dimensions.Width = Number(pkg.Dimensions.Width/0.39370).toFixed(2)
             pkg.Dimensions.Height = Number(pkg.Dimensions.Height/0.39370).toFixed(2)
             pkg.Dimensions.Units = 1;
         }
         
     });
     
     
    // debugger;
      if(Number(vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].DeclaredValueCustoms.Amount).toFixed(2) > 2500 ){
          if(vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].ExportInformationCode === null){
              vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].ExportInformationCode = "OS";
          }
          if(vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].AesTransactionNumber === null){
              vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].SedMethod = 2;
              $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].AesTransactionNumber"]').focus();
              throw new Error('Missing AES/ITN Number');
          } 
          if(vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].AesTransactionNumber !== null){
              vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].Comments = vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].Comments + "\n ITN/AES Filer " + vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].AesTransactionNumber;
             
          }
      }
     
    console.log(shipmentRequest);
  
};

// this.ShippingLoaded() // returns void
this.ShippingLoaded = function(){
    this.vm.populateReturnAddress = this.PopulateReturnAddress;
    this.vm.populateShipToAddress = this.PopulateShipToAddress;
    this.vm.serviceOption = serviceOption;
    this.vm.serviceOptions = serviceOptions(this.vm.profile);
    this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].ShipperReference = user_orderNumber;
    this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].MiscReference1 = user_orderNumber;
    this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].ConsigneeReference = cost_Center;
    this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].MiscReference2 = cost_Center;
    this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].MiscReference3 = user_partNumber;
    this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].Description = user_description;
   

    function serviceOption() {
        this.selectedServices = [this.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Service];
    }
    function serviceOptions(profile) {
        //debugger;
        var filterServices = [];
        var customData3 = uPS_Service.split(',');
        for (var item of customData3) {
            var symbol = getServiceSymbol(item.toLowerCase());
            for (var service of profile.Services) {
                if (service.Symbol === symbol) {
                    service.Name = service.Name.replace('(UPS Adapter)','').trim();
                    if (service.Name.includes("Expedited")){
                        service.Name = service.Name + " (MAIN SERVICE)";
                    }
                    if (service.Name.includes("Saver")){
                        service.Name = service.Name + " (To Heredia or Only with Boston's Authorization)";
                    }
                    filterServices.push(service);
                    break;
                }
            }
        }
        return filterServices;
        function getServiceSymbol(code) {
            if (code == '2dn') return 'UPSAPI.UPS.2DA'
            else if (code == '3dd') return 'UPSAPI.UPS.3DS'
            else if (code == 'exp') return 'UPSAPI.UPS.EXPEDITED'
            else if (code == 'ess') return 'UPSAPI.UPS.EXPRESS'
            else if (code == 'nda') return 'UPSAPI.UPS.NDA'
            else if (code == 'dae') return 'UPSAPI.UPS.NDAEAM'
            else if (code == 'grn') return 'UPSAPI.UPS.GND'
            else if (code == 'uwe') return 'UPSAPI.UPS.EXPEDITED'
            else if (code == 'wep') return 'UPSAPI.UPS.EXPRESSSP'
            else if (code == 'swe') return 'UPSAPI.UPS.EXPRESS'
            else if (code == 'uws') return 'UPSAPI.UPS.SAVER'
            else if (code == 'std') return 'UPSAPI.UPS.STANDARD'
        }
        
    }
    
    if(dims.includes(',')){
        var dimensions = dims.split(',');
        this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].Weight.Amount = Number(dimensions[0]);
        maxvolumetric = Number(dimensions[4]);
        console.log("Max Volumetric: " + maxvolumetric);
        this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].Dimensions = {
            Length: Number(dimensions[1]),
            Height: Number(dimensions[2]),
            Width: Number(dimensions[3]),
            Units: 0
        };
    }
   
    vm = this.vm;
};

// this.PopulateReturnAddress() // returns void
this.PopulateReturnAddress = function(){
   // debugger;
   
    if(SelectedReturnAddress !== undefined && SelectedReturnAddress !== null){
         this.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Consignee = {
            Code : SelectedReturnAddress.Code,
            Company : SelectedReturnAddress.Company,
            Contact : SelectedReturnAddress.Contact,
            Address1 : SelectedReturnAddress.Address1,
            Address2 : SelectedReturnAddress.Address2,
            Address3 : SelectedReturnAddress.Address3,
            City : SelectedReturnAddress.City,
            StateProvince : SelectedReturnAddress.StateProvince,
            PostalCode : SelectedReturnAddress.PostalCode,
            Country : SelectedReturnAddress.Country,
            Email : SelectedReturnAddress.Email,
            Phone : SelectedReturnAddress.Phone
        };
    }
};

 // debugger;

            Address1 : SelectedShipToAddress.Address1,

            StateProvince : SelectedShipToAddress.StateProvince,
            PostalCode : SelectedShipToAddress.PostalCode,

        };
    }
};

// function PageLoaded(location) // returns void
    this.PageLoaded = function (location) {
