// function GetCustom(shipmentRequest, fieldName, customDataType) // returns string
    function GetCustom(shipmentRequest, fieldName, customDataType) {
        var returnValue = "";
        var customData = null;
        if (customDataType === "User") customData = shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.OriginAddress.CustomData;
        if (customDataType === "To") customData = shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.CustomData;

        if (customData) {
            customData.forEach(function (customField) {
                if (fieldName.toUpperCase() === customField.Key.toUpperCase()) returnValue = customField.Value;
            });
        }
        return returnValue;
    }

// function SendFreightCollect(shipmentRequest) // returns void
    function SendFreightCollect(shipmentRequest) {
        var selection = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference20;
        if (selection.indexOf("-") > -1) {
            var position = selection.indexOf("-");
            shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Account = selection.substring(position + 2);
            shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Terms = "CONSIGNEE";
        } else {
            throw new error({ "number": "001", "description": "Receiver Billing Information not found." });
        }
    }

// Source: Cabinet Works Group (MASCO)_Masco Client Side Business Rules_1752.cs
// this.SWOGShipment() // returns void
    this.SWOGShipment = function () {
        // Custom function that fires when SWOG button is clicked
        // If Shipper is "MCD" "MCT" or "MCC" there is no validation done on SWOGS and then focus on Dimensions when completed
        
        // Get current Shipper from screen       
        var shipper = this.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Shipper;        

        debugger;
        // Define initial SWOG array and counter
        var swogArray = ["SWOG_START"];
        var counter = 0;

        // If the masterOrderNumber has an initial SWOG value from PreLoad, push that into the swogArray before collecting new ones.  Set the counter to 1.
        if (masterOrderNumber != '') {
            swogArray.push(masterOrderNumber);
            swogArray = unique(swogArray);
            counter = 1;
        }

        do {
            // Prompt for SWOG data entry until END_SWOG is scanned
            var swog = window.prompt("Enter SWOG order number.  Scan END_SWOG Barcode when complete", "");
            debugger;
            // Make sure swog is not empty
            if (swog != '') {
                if (counter > 0 && swogArray.length > 1) {
                    // This check is only done when the Shipper is NOT MCD, MCT or MCC
                    if (shipper != "MCD" && shipper != "MCT" && shipper != "MCC") {
                        // Make sure the entry is valid (not 'END_SWOG' AND length is greater than 9, not the same as the first entry in the array)
                        if (swog != 'END_SWOG' && swog.length > 9 && swog.substring(0, 9) != swogArray[1].substring(0, 9)) {
                            alert("The order that you scanned = " + swog + " is invalid for this SWOG and will be removed.");
                            swog = '';
                        }
                    }
                }
                // If masterOrderNumber is not empty, this function was called from PreShip.  Otherwise it came from clicking SWOG
                if (masterOrderNumber != '') {
                    // function called from PreShip...validate length of swog
                    if ((swog != '' && swog.length > 9) || swog == 'END_SWOG') {
                        // Add the swog to the swogArray
                        swogArray.push(swog);
                        // Make sure that only unique entries are in the swogArray
                        swogArray = unique(swogArray);
                        counter++;
                    }
                }
                else {
                    // function called from clicking button...do not validate length of swog
                    if (swog != ''  || swog == 'END_SWOG') {
                        // Add the swog to the swogArray
                        swogArray.push(swog);
                        // Make sure that only unique entries are in the swogArray
                        swogArray = unique(swogArray);
                        counter++;
                    }
                }                
            }
        } while (swog != 'END_SWOG');        

        // Put '|' between each SWOG number
        var swogOrderNumbers = "";
        swogArray.forEach(function (item, index, array) { swogOrderNumbers = swogOrderNumbers + "|" + item; });
        swogOrderNumbers = removeFirstChar(swogOrderNumbers);

        // Store final swog data in UserData1
        //this.currentShipment.Packages[0].ShipperReference = 123;
        //this.currentShipment.Packages[0].ConsigneeReference = swogOrderNumbers;
        this.currentShipment.Packages[0].UserData1 = swogOrderNumbers;

        // If Shipper IS MCD, MCT or MCC then put focus on length field in dimensions
        if (shipper == "MCD" || shipper == "MCT" || shipper == "MCC") {
            lengthText = ('[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].Dimensions.Length"]');
            setFocus(lengthText);
        }
        // Clear out masterOrderNumber
        masterOrderNumber = "";
        debugger;
    }

// this.PreLoad(loadValue, shipmentRequest, userParams) // returns void
  this.PreLoad = function (loadValue, shipmentRequest, userParams) {

    // 🔄 Reset any previous SWOG starter
    masterOrderNumber = "";

    // 🧾 First prompt: general input
    var firstInput = window.prompt(
        'Enter Package Dimensions (###x###x###)\n' +
        '— OR type PACKSIZE_CONTINUE to skip dimensions\n' +
        '— OR enter a SWOG Order Number to start the SWOG function:',
        ''
    );

    if (firstInput === null) {
        userParams.dimensions = "";
        return;  // ❌ Cancelled
    }

    firstInput = firstInput.trim();
    var dimRegex = /^[0-9]+\s*x\s*[0-9]+\s*x\s*[0-9]+$/i;

    if (firstInput.toUpperCase() === 'PACKSIZE_CONTINUE') {
        userParams.dimensions = 'PACKSIZE_CONTINUE';
        return;  // ✅ Skip dimensions
    }

    if (dimRegex.test(firstInput)) {
        userParams.dimensions = firstInput.toLowerCase();
        return;  // ✅ Valid dimensions directly
    }

    // 🌀 Else: treat as SWOG starter
    masterOrderNumber = firstInput;
    this.vm.swogShipment();

    // 🧾 Second prompt after SWOG
    var dimsAfterSwog = window.prompt(
        'Enter Package Dimensions (###x###x###), type PACKSIZE_CONTINUE to skip, or leave blank:',
        ''
    );

    if (dimsAfterSwog === null) {
        userParams.dimensions = "";  // ❌ Cancelled
        return;
    }

    dimsAfterSwog = dimsAfterSwog.trim();

    if (dimsAfterSwog.toUpperCase() === 'PACKSIZE_CONTINUE') {
        userParams.dimensions = 'PACKSIZE_CONTINUE';  // ✅ PACKSIZE_CONTINUE accepted in second prompt too
    } else if (dimRegex.test(dimsAfterSwog)) {
        userParams.dimensions = dimsAfterSwog.toLowerCase();  // ✅ Dimensions entered
    } else {
        userParams.dimensions = "";  // ❌ Nothing valid entered
    }
}

// Source: Carrier Misroute (CMR) (CMR)_Client Business Rules_2487.cs
// function getShipperCustomers(shippers) // returns an array of customer options for shipment setup
            function getShipperCustomers(shippers) {
                var shipper = shippers.find(shipper => shipper.Symbol == vm.shipping.slic);
                if (shipper == undefined)
                     return [{ name: '--- No Shipper Configured ---', disabled: true }];

                var customData = shipper.CustomData.filter(c => c.Key.toUpperCase() == "CUSTOMER");
                var customers = customData.map(function(c) {
                    var customer = c.Value.toUpperCase();

                    if (customer == 'AMAZON')
                        return { name: "Amazon", value: customer, hasLoad: true, hasReturn: true, autoShip: true };
                    else if (customer == 'UPS')
                        return { name: "UPS", value: customer, hasCameraImage: true, hasFileImage: true, autoShip: false };
                    else if (customer == 'DEMO')
                        return { name: "Demo", value: customer, hasLoad: false, hasReturn: true, hasCameraImage: true, hasFileImage: false, autoShip: false };
                    else if (customer == 'FANATICS')
                        return { name: "Fanatics", value: customer, hasReturn: true, hasCameraImage: true, autoShip: false };
                    else
                        return { name: `--- ${customer} ---`, disabled: true };
                });

                customers.sort(function(a, b) {
                    if (a.disabled && !b.disabled) return 1;
                    if (!a.disabled && b.disabled) return -1;
                    return a.name.localeCompare(b.name);
                });
                return [{ name: '--- Select Customer Option ---', selector: 'select[ng-model="vm.shipping.customer"]', disabled: true }].concat(customers);
            }

// function customerChange() // returns undefined

                vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference19 = vm.shipping.customer.value;
            }

// function uploadCarrierLabelFile() // returns undefined
            function uploadCarrierLabelFile () {
                var $carrierLabelImage = $(vm.shipping.imageFile.selector);
                var imageFile = $carrierLabelImage.prop('files')[0];
                if (imageFile == undefined) {
                    $carrierLabelImage.click();
                    return;
                }
                var reader = new FileReader();
                reader.readAsDataURL(imageFile);
                reader.onload = function () {
                    var dataURL = this.result;
                    getMegapixelsFromFileReader(dataURL).then(function(megapixels) {
                        console.log(`The image is ${megapixels.toFixed(2)} megapixels.`);
                    });

                    vm.loadValue = 'Label Upload';
                    vm.labelImage = dataURL.replace(/^data:.+;base64,/, '');
                    vm.load();
                    $carrierLabelImage.val(null);
                }
            }

// function captureImage() // returns undefined
            function captureImage () {
                // vm.shipping.videoModal.stream.id = vm.shipping.videoModal.stream.selector
                var cameraStream = document.getElementById(vm.shipping.videoModal.stream.id);
                var track = cameraStream.srcObject.getVideoTracks()[0];
                var imageCapture = new ImageCapture(track);

                imageCapture.grabFrame().then(function(imageBitmap) {
                    const canvas = document.createElement('canvas');
                    const ctx = canvas.getContext('2d');

                    // Set canvas dimensions to match the imageBitmap
                    canvas.width = imageBitmap.width;
                    canvas.height = imageBitmap.height;

                    // Draw the imageBitmap onto the canvas
                    ctx.drawImage(imageBitmap, 0, 0);

                    // Get the image data as a Base64 data URL
                    // You can specify format and quality (e.g., 'image/jpeg', 0.8)
                    const base64DataUrl = canvas.toDataURL('image/png', 1.0);
                    // var newTab = window.open('about:blank','image from canvas');
                    // newTab.document.write("<img src='" + base64DataUrl + "' alt='from canvas'/>");

                    vm.loadValue = 'Label Capture';
                    vm.labelImage = base64DataUrl.replace(/^data:.+;base64,/, '');
                    // vm.videoModal.stopVideoStream();
                    vm.shipping.videoModal.stream.stop();
                    vm.load();
                })


                // imageCapture.takePhoto().then(function(blob) {
                //     var reader = new FileReader();
                //     reader.readAsDataURL(blob);
                //     reader.onloadend = function () {

                //         getMegapixelsFromFileReader(dataURL).then(function(megapixels) {

                //         });
                
                //         vm.loadValue = 'Label Capture';
                //         vm.labelImage = dataURL.replace(/^data:.+;base64,/, '');

                //         vm.load();
                //     }
                // })
            }

// function videoStreamStart() // returns undefined
            function videoStreamStart () {
                if (navigator.mediaDevices && navigator.mediaDevices.getUserMedia) {
                    // Request access to the video stream
                    var constraints = {
                        audio: false,
                        video: {
                            zoom: true,
                            facingMode: 'environment',
                            // aspectRatio: { ideal: 9/16 }
                        }
                    };
                    //HD
                    // constraints.video.width = { ideal: 1920 };
                    // constraints.video.height = { ideal: 1080 };

                    //QHD
                    constraints.video.width = { ideal: 2560 };
                    constraints.video.height = { ideal: 1440 };

                    //4K UHD
                    // constraints.video.width = { ideal: 3840 };
                    // constraints.video.height = { ideal: 2160 }

                    navigator.mediaDevices.getUserMedia(constraints).then(function(stream) {
                        // Assign the stream to the video element's source object
                        var cameraStream = document.getElementById(vm.shipping.videoModal.stream.id);
                        cameraStream.srcObject = stream;

                        var [track] = stream.getVideoTracks();
                        var capabilities = track.getCapabilities();

                        vm.videoModal.zoom ??= {
                            min: capabilities.zoom.min,
                            max: capabilities.zoom.max,
                            current: track.getSettings().zoom
                        }
                        var zoomLevel = localStorage.getItem('zoomLevel') ?? getZoomLevel(track.getSettings().zoom);

                        track.applyConstraints({ advanced: [{ zoom: zoomLevel }] });
                        vm.videoModal.track = track;
                        // if (capabilities.zoom) {
                        //     track.applyConstraints({ advanced: [{ zoom: capabilities.zoom.max }] });
                        // }
                    }).catch(function(error) {
                        console.error("Error accessing the camera: ", error);
                    });
                } else {
                    // Fallback for older browsers
                    console.error("Your browser does not support the getUserMedia API.");
                }

                function getZoomLevel(currentZoom) {
                    localStorage.setItem('zoomLevel', currentZoom);
                    return currentZoom;
                }
            }

// function videoStreamStop(isCanceled) // returns undefined
            function videoStreamStop(isCanceled) {
                vm.labelImage = isCanceled ? null : vm.labelImage;

                var cameraStream = document.getElementById(vm.shipping.videoModal.stream.id);
                if (cameraStream.srcObject) {
                    var tracks = cameraStream.srcObject.getTracks();
                    tracks.forEach(track => track.stop()); // Stop each track in the stream
                    cameraStream.srcObject = null;
                }
            }

// Source: Clarios (CLRS)_Clarios_Rule_1705.cs
// this.PreShip(shipmentRequest, userParams) // returns undefined
    this.PreShip = function(shipmentRequest, userParams) {   
        debugger;
        var usCountry = "UNITED_STATES";
        var usAcronym = "US";
        var PackageRequests=shipmentRequest.Packages;
        
        $(PackageRequests).each(function (x, item)
          {
              var value = item.DeclaredValueCustoms.Amount;
              var tN = item.AesTransactionNumber;
              if (value >= 2500 && tN ===null)
              {
                    alert("Please check with clarios-na-trade@clarios.com if EEI filing is needed");
              }             
             item.Description=$('input[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].Description"]').val();
            
          });
          
          // For International Destination Rule Applies to all use cases and all carriers
          if ((shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Country != usCountry) && (shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Country != usAcronym))
                {
                    shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.MiscReference8 = "Y";
                }
                else
                {
                    shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.MiscReference8 = "N";
                }
             
    }

// this.NewShipment(shipmentRequest) // returns undefined
    this.NewShipment = function(shipmentRequest) { 
        
          $(function ()
  {
    $('body').delegate('select[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Terms"]', 'change', function ()
    {
       
      var chkBox = $('input[type=checkbox][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.ThirdPartyBilling"]');
      var chkVal = $(chkBox).prop('checked');

   
      if (($(this).val() === 'string:SHIPPER') && (chkVal === false))//Freight Collect -> uncheck 3rd party billing box
      {
        $(chkBox).click();
        //$('[nameaddress="vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Consignee"]').find($('input[ng-model="nameaddress.Account"]').attr('ng-required', true).css('border-color', '#a94442'));
$('[nameaddress="vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Consignee"]').find($('input[ng-model="nameaddress.Account"]').attr('ng-required', 'account.isRequired()').css('border', '1px solid #ccc'));
      }

      else if (($(this).val() === 'string:CONSIGNEE') && (chkVal === true))//Prepaid -> check 3rd party billing box
      {
        $(chkBox).click();
        //$('[nameaddress="vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Consignee"]').find($('input[ng-model="nameaddress.Account"]').attr('ng-required', 'account.isRequired()').css('border', '1px solid #ccc'));
$('[nameaddress="vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Consignee"]').find($('input[ng-model="nameaddress.Account"]').attr('ng-required', true).css('border-color', '#a94442'));
      }

    });
  });
    }

// Source: Clarios (CLRS)_Clarios_Rule_Paperless_2440.cs
// this.PreShip(shipmentRequest, userParams) // returns void
    this.PreShip = function (shipmentRequest, userParams) {
        console.log("PreShip In");
        
        userParams.paperless = JSON.stringify(this.vm.paperless);
        console.log('paperless:', userParams.paperless);
        
        var usCountry = "UNITED_STATES";
        var usAcronym = "US";
        var PackageRequests = shipmentRequest.Packages;

        $(PackageRequests).each(function (x, item) {
            var value = item.DeclaredValueCustoms.Amount;
            var tN = item.AesTransactionNumber;
            if (value >= 2500 && tN === null) {
                alert("Please check with clarios-na-trade@clarios.com if EEI filing is needed");
            }
            item.Description = $('input[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].Description"]').val();

        });

        // For International Destination Rule Applies to all use cases and all carriers
        if ((shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Country != usCountry) && (shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Country != usAcronym)) {
            shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.MiscReference8 = "Y";
        }
        else {
            shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.MiscReference8 = "N";
        }

        console.log("PreShip Out");
    };

// function CloseAllShippers() // returns void
    function CloseAllShippers() {
        debugger;

        var getManifestItemsList, getManifestItemsemethod, methodParams, authorizationToken;
        var allOrdersSelectedCarrier = [];
        var allShipperSelectedCarrier, getShipperCarriersmethod, getShipperCarriersmethodParams, CloseAllShippersResponse, CloseAllShippersResults

        getShipperCarriersmethod = 'api/ShippingService/GetShipperCarriers';
        getManifestItemsemethod = 'api/ShippingService/GetManifestItems';
        authorizationToken = clientService.authorizationToken();


        let selectedValCarrier = AllCarriersList.find(Carriers => Carriers.Id == $("#CarriersList option:selected").val()).Symbol;

        $.each(Array(AllShipperList.length), function (i) {

            getShipperCarriersmethodParams = { "ShipperId": AllShipperList[i].Id, "CompanyId": userContextDetails.CompanyId };
            allShipperSelectedCarrier = $.post({ url: clientService.config.ApiUrl + '/' + getShipperCarriersmethod, data: getShipperCarriersmethodParams, async: false, headers: authorizationToken }).responseJSON;

            if (allShipperSelectedCarrier.Carriers && allShipperSelectedCarrier.Carriers.length != 0) {

                methodParams = { "Carrier": selectedValCarrier, "Shipper": AllShipperList[i].Symbol, "SearchCriteria": { "OrderByClauses": [{ "FieldName": "ShipDate", "Direction": "DESC" }] }, "IncludeImported": false, "CompanyId": userContextDetails.CompanyId };
                getManifestItemsList = $.post({ url: clientService.config.ApiUrl + '/' + getManifestItemsemethod, data: methodParams, async: false, headers: authorizationToken }).responseJSON;


                if (getManifestItemsList.ManifestItems && getManifestItemsList.ManifestItems.length != 0) {
                    debugger;
                    var CloseManifestmethod, methodParams, CloseAllShippersResults
                    CloseManifestmethod = 'api/ShippingService/CloseManifest';
                    $.each(Array(getManifestItemsList.ManifestItems.length), function (j) {


                        allOrdersSelectedCarrier.push({ "Attributes": getManifestItemsList.ManifestItems[j].Attributes, "ShipDate": getManifestItemsList.ManifestItems[j].ShipDate, "Symbol": getManifestItemsList.ManifestItems[j].Symbol, "Name": getManifestItemsList.ManifestItems[j].Name });
                    });
                    methodParams = { "Carrier": selectedValCarrier, "ManifestItems": allOrdersSelectedCarrier, "Shipper": AllShipperList[i].Symbol, "Print": true, "UserParams": {}, "CompanyId": userContextDetails.CompanyId };
                    CloseAllShippersResponse = $.post({ url: clientService.config.ApiUrl + '/' + CloseManifestmethod, data: methodParams, async: false, headers: authorizationToken }).responseJSON;
                    allOrdersSelectedCarrier = [];
                }
            }


        });

        if (CloseAllShippersResponse != undefined) {
            if (CloseAllShippersResponse.ErrorCode == -1) {

                $('#divAllshippersErrorMsg').show();
                $('#divAllshippersunsuccessfulcloseoutMsg').hide();
                $('#divAllshippersAndCarriersErrorMsg').hide();
                $('#divAllshipperAndCarrierssunsuccessfulcloseoutMsg').hide();

                ShowAlert('ErrorModalCloseShippers');

            } else {
                CloseAllShippersResults = CloseAllShippersResponse.CloseManifestResults[0].ErrorCode;
                if (CloseAllShippersResults != 0) {

                    $('#divAllshippersErrorMsg').hide();
                    $('#divAllshippersunsuccessfulcloseoutMsg').show();
                    $('#divAllshippersAndCarriersErrorMsg').hide();
                    $('#divAllshipperAndCarrierssunsuccessfulcloseoutMsg').hide();

                    ShowAlert('ErrorModalCloseShippers');

                } else if (CloseAllShippersResults == 0) {

                    $('#divsuccessfulAllShippers').show();
                    $('#divsuccessfulAllShippersAndAllCarriers').hide();

                    ShowAlert('successfulModalCloseShippers');

                }
            }
        } else {
            $('#divAllshippersErrorMsg').show();
            $('#divAllshippersunsuccessfulcloseoutMsg').hide();
            $('#divAllshippersAndCarriersErrorMsg').hide();
            $('#divAllshipperAndCarrierssunsuccessfulcloseoutMsg').hide();

            ShowAlert('ErrorModalCloseShippers');

        }

        $('#loaderspinnerImg').hide();


    }

    function ClosecOutAllShippersAndAllCarriers() {

        var CloseAllShippersAllCarrierResponse, closeallgetManifestItemsemethod, CloseAllShippersAllCarriermethod, methodParams, authorizationToken, CloseAllShippersAllCarrierResults, getallShipperallCarriersmethod
        CloseAllShippersAllCarriermethod = 'api/ShippingService/CloseManifest';
        getallShipperallCarriersmethod = 'api/ShippingService/GetShipperCarriers';
        closeallgetManifestItemsemethod = 'api/ShippingService/GetManifestItems';

        var allOrdersSelectedCarrierfromallclose = [];
        debugger;

        $.each(Array(AllCarriersList.length), function (k) {
            $.each(Array(AllShipperList.length), function (i) {
                var getShipperCarriersmethodParameters = { "ShipperId": AllShipperList[i].Id, "CompanyId": userContextDetails.CompanyId };
                authorizationToken = clientService.authorizationToken();
                var allShipperallCarrierSelectedCarrier = $.post({ url: clientService.config.ApiUrl + '/' + getallShipperallCarriersmethod, data: getShipperCarriersmethodParameters, async: false, headers: authorizationToken }).responseJSON;

                if (allShipperallCarrierSelectedCarrier.Carriers && allShipperallCarrierSelectedCarrier.Carriers.length != 0) {

                    var closeallmethodParams = { "Carrier": AllCarriersList[k].Symbol, "Shipper": AllShipperList[i].Symbol, "SearchCriteria": { "OrderByClauses": [{ "FieldName": "ShipDate", "Direction": "DESC" }] }, "IncludeImported": false, "CompanyId": userContextDetails.CompanyId };
                    var getManifestItemsList = $.post({ url: clientService.config.ApiUrl + '/' + closeallgetManifestItemsemethod, data: closeallmethodParams, async: false, headers: authorizationToken }).responseJSON;

                    if (getManifestItemsList.ManifestItems && getManifestItemsList.ManifestItems.length != 0) {
                        var CloseManifestmethod, methodParams, authorizationToken, CloseAllShippersResults
                        authorizationToken = clientService.authorizationToken();

                        $.each(Array(getManifestItemsList.ManifestItems.length), function (j) {

                            allOrdersSelectedCarrierfromallclose.push({ "Attributes": getManifestItemsList.ManifestItems[j].Attributes, "ShipDate": getManifestItemsList.ManifestItems[j].ShipDate, "Symbol": getManifestItemsList.ManifestItems[j].Symbol, "Name": getManifestItemsList.ManifestItems[j].Name });
                        });
                        var closeallmethodParams = { "Carrier": AllCarriersList[k].Symbol, "ManifestItems": allOrdersSelectedCarrierfromallclose, "Shipper": AllShipperList[i].Symbol, "Print": true, "UserParams": {}, "CompanyId": userContextDetails.CompanyId };
                        CloseAllShippersAllCarrierResponse = $.post({ url: clientService.config.ApiUrl + '/' + CloseAllShippersAllCarriermethod, data: closeallmethodParams, async: false, headers: authorizationToken }).responseJSON;
                        allOrdersSelectedCarrierfromallclose = [];
                    }
                }
            });
        });

        if (CloseAllShippersAllCarrierResponse != undefined) {
            if (CloseAllShippersAllCarrierResponse.ErrorCode == -1) {

                $('#divAllshippersErrorMsg').hide();
                $('#divAllshippersunsuccessfulcloseoutMsg').hide();
                $('#divAllshippersAndCarriersErrorMsg').show();
                $('#divAllshipperAndCarrierssunsuccessfulcloseoutMsg').hide();

                ShowAlert('ErrorModalCloseShippers');
            } else {
                CloseAllShippersAllCarrierResults = CloseAllShippersAllCarrierResponse.CloseManifestResults[0].ErrorCode;
                if (CloseAllShippersAllCarrierResults != 0) {

                    $('#divAllshippersErrorMsg').hide();
                    $('#divAllshippersunsuccessfulcloseoutMsg').hide();
                    $('#divAllshippersAndCarriersErrorMsg').hide();
                    $('#divAllshipperAndCarrierssunsuccessfulcloseoutMsg').show();

                    ShowAlert('ErrorModalCloseShippers');
                } else if (CloseAllShippersAllCarrierResults == 0) {

                    $('#divsuccessfulAllShippers').hide();
                    $('#divsuccessfulAllShippersAndAllCarriers').show();

                    ShowAlert('successfulModalCloseShippers');
                }
            }
        } else {

            $('#divAllshippersErrorMsg').hide();
            $('#divAllshippersunsuccessfulcloseoutMsg').hide();
            $('#divAllshippersAndCarriersErrorMsg').show();
            $('#divAllshipperAndCarrierssunsuccessfulcloseoutMsg').hide();

            ShowAlert('ErrorModalCloseShippers');
        }
        $('#loaderspinnerImg').hide();


    }

Please contact DL-SmallParcelDeliveryService@conagra.com with questions or for specific instructions and restrictions";

            alert(DINote);
            throw new Error("Package # " + (index + 1) + " dry ice amount is over allowable weight, please check your Dry Ice value or unit of measure for accuracy.");

        } else {

      case "G":
            if (shipmentRequest.Packages[index].DryIceWeight.Amount > 2494.76) {
                alert(DINote);
                throw new Error("Package # " + (index + 1) + " dry ice amount is over allowable weight, please check your Dry Ice value or unit of measure for accuracy.");
        } else {
           
        }
      break;
      case "OZ":
            if (shipmentRequest.Packages[index].DryIceWeight.Amount > 88) {
                alert(DINote);
                throw new Error("Package # " + (index + 1) + " dry ice amount is over allowable weight, please check your Dry Ice value or unit of measure for accuracy.");
        } else {
           
        }
      break;
      default:

    }}}
  
  
   this.PreShip = function (shipmentRequest, userParams) {

    };
    

   function GetKeyValue(key, arr) {
      for (var index in arr) {
          if (arr[index].Key.toLowerCase() === key.toLowerCase()) return arr[index].Value;
      }
      return '';
  }
}

// function PreShip(shipmentRequest, userParams) // returns void
this.PreShip = function (shipmentRequest, userParams) {

        debugger;
        if (shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ReturnDelivery == undefined || shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ReturnDelivery == false) {
            shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.UserData1 = JSON.stringify(shipmentRequest);
            shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference20 = $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference20"]').val();
            shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.MiscReference20 = $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference20"]').val();
        }
        else if (shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ReturnDelivery != undefined && shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ReturnDelivery == true) {
            shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.UserData1 = null;
        }
        debugger;
    }

// function NewShipment(shipmentRequest) // returns void
this.NewShipment = function (shipmentRequest) {
        if (cbr.historyShipment != null) {
            var historyRequest = JSON.parse(cbr.historyShipment);
            this.vm.totalPackages = historyRequest.Packages.length;

            shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults = historyRequest.PackageDefaults;
            shipmentRequest.Packages = historyRequest.Packages;
            shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Description = "PC Equipment";

            shipmentRequest.Packages.forEach(function (pkg) {
                pkg.ReturnDelivery = true;
                pkg.ReturnDeliveryMethod = 4;
                pkg.ReturnDeliveryAddressEmail = historyRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Email;
                pkg.Description = "PC Equipment";
            });
            cbr.historyShipment = null;
        }
        cbr.bulk.create.itemReferences = [];
    }

// this.NewShipment(shipmentRequest) // returns void
this.NewShipment = function (shipmentRequest) {
		//debugger;
		vmTemp = this.vm;
		
		console.log(vmTemp);

		shipmentRequest.Packages[this.vm.packageIndex].CommodityClass = "CLASS_65";
		//document.getElementById("autoship_checkbox").checked = false;
		this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[this.vm.packageIndex].MiscReference20 = false;   // autoship checkbox

		if (shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Service) {
			shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Service.Symbol = "x";
		}

		// clear Markup Percentage
		$("#custom_markup_id").val("");

		// set dialog values/events
		$('#newOrderNumber').val('');
		$('#newWeight').val('');
		$('#newWeight').keypress(function(e) {
			// enforce weight mask
			if (!String.fromCharCode(e.which).match(/[0-9.]+/g)) {
				return false;
			}
		})
		$('#newBoxType').change(function() {
			if ($(this).find('option:selected').val() !== '') {
				// show dimensions string if box was selected
				let length = vmTemp.currentShipment.Packages[vmTemp.packageIndex].Dimensions.Length;
				let width = vmTemp.currentShipment.Packages[vmTemp.packageIndex].Dimensions.Width;
				let height = vmTemp.currentShipment.Packages[vmTemp.packageIndex].Dimensions.Height;
				let units = vmTemp.currentShipment.Packages[vmTemp.packageIndex].Dimensions.Units === 0 ? "IN" : "CM";
				$('#newDimensions').val(length + "x" + width + "x" + height + " " + units);
				
				if (vmTemp.loadValue) {
					$('#newShipmentDialog button[ng-click="vm.load()"').prop('disabled', false);
				}
			}
			else {
				$('#newDimensions').val('');
			}
		});
		$('#newDimensions').val('');
		$('#newDimensions').keyup(function(e) {
			let loadButton = $('#newShipmentDialog button[ng-click="vm.load()"');
			if (this.value.trim() === '' && vmTemp.loadValue) {
				loadButton.prop('disabled', false);
			}
			else {
				// enforce dimensions mask if entered LxWxH (IN/CM optional)
				let regEx = /(\d+)x(\d+)x(\d+)( IN| CM)?/
				if (!regEx.test(this.value)) {
					loadButton.prop('disabled', true);
				}
				else if (vmTemp.loadValue) {
					loadButton.prop('disabled', false);
				}
			}
		});

		// show Load Shipment dialog and set focus
		if (!$('#newShipmentDialog').is(':visible')) {
			$('#newShipmentDialog').modal('show');
			$('#newShipmentDialog').on('shown.bs.modal', function() {
				$(this).find('[autofocus]').focus();
			});
		}
	};

// this.AddPackage(shipmentRequest, packageIndex) // returns void
this.AddPackage = function(shipmentRequest, packageIndex) {
		//debugger;

		// if ("$("#ctl00_cphContent_ship_mode_list").val() == "0")
		// {
		shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex].UserData1 = shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex - 1].UserData1;
		shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex].ShipperReference = shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex - 1].ShipperReference;
		shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex].ConsigneeReference = shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex - 1].ConsigneeReference;
		shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex].MiscReference1 = shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex - 1].MiscReference1;
		shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex].MiscReference2 = shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex - 1].MiscReference1;
		shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex].MiscReference3 = shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex - 1].MiscReference3;
		shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex].MiscReference4 = shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex - 1].MiscReference4;
		shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex].MiscReference5 = shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex - 1].MiscReference5;
		shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex].Description = shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex - 1].Description;
		shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex].CommercialInvoiceMethod = shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex - 1].CommercialInvoiceMethod;
		shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex].SaturdayDelivery = shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex - 1].SaturdayDelivery;
		//}

		getWeight(this.vm);
	};

// this.PreLoad(value, shipmentRequest, params) // returns void
this.PreLoad = function(value, shipmentRequest, params) {
		//debugger;
		if (shipmentRequest.Packages[this.vm.packageIndex].BoxType === undefined || shipmentRequest.Packages[this.vm.packageIndex].BoxType === null) {
			// if box is empty, add custom dimensions from dialog
			let dims = $('#newDimensions').val().trim().split(/x| /);
			if (dims !== null && dims.length >= 3) {
				$('form[name="generalForm"]').find('input[name="length"]').val(dims[0]).change();
				$('form[name="generalForm"]').find('input[name="width"]').val(dims[1]).change();
				$('form[name="generalForm"]').find('input[name="height"]').val(dims[2]).change();
				
				let index = 1;
				if (dims.length === 4) {
					dims[3] = dims[3].toUpperCase();
					index = (dims[3] === 'IN' ? 1 : 2);
				}
				$('form[name="generalForm"]').find('select[name="units"] option:eq(' + index + ')').prop('selected', true);
			}
		}

		let oChk = this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[this.vm.packageIndex].MiscReference20;		// autoship
		if (oChk === true) {
			params.autoship = oChk;
		}

		$('#newShipmentDialog').modal('hide');
		showLoading(true);
	};

// this.PostLoad(value, shipmentRequest) // returns void
this.PostLoad = function(value, shipmentRequest) {
		debugger;
		let errorMessage = shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ErrorMessage;
		
		if (errorMessage === undefined) errorMessage = "";
		if (errorMessage === null) errorMessage = "";

		if (shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Service !== undefined && shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Service.Symbol === "x") {
			showLoading(false);
			alert("No service selected!");
		}
		
		if (errorMessage !== undefined && errorMessage === 'validate') {
			//$("#ctl00_cphContent_left_tabs_consignee_tab_consignee_na_ab_ctrl_na_ctrl_validate_addr_btn").click();
			showLoading(false);
			return;
		}

		if (errorMessage !== undefined && errorMessage.substring(0, 4) === "pop:") {
			showLoading(false);
			alert(errorMessage.substring(4));
			return;
		}

		if (errorMessage !== undefined && errorMessage !== '') {
			showLoading(false);
			alert(errorMessage);
			let errors = ["not found", "already shipped", "too many"];
			if (errors.some(errorText => errorMessage.includes(errorText))) {
				// open Load Shipment dialog
				this.vm.newShipment();
			}
			return;
		}

		if (shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Country === 'US') {
			this.vm.shipMode = 1;
		} else {
			this.vm.shipMode = 0;
		}

		$("#custom_markup_id").val(shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference3);

		//getWeight();

		if (shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.MiscReference5 !== null && shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.MiscReference5 === 'autoship') {
			this.vm.checkShip();
			return;
		}

		// select all services before rate
		setTimeout(function() {
			// check Select All after delay to allow UI update
			vmTemp.isAllServicesSelected = true;
			vmTemp.selectAllServices();
			vmTemp.rate();
		}, 100);
		
	};

// this.PreShip(shipmentRequest, userParams) // returns void
this.PreShip = function (shipmentRequest, userParams) {
		console.log("🚀 [PreShip] Starting PreShip function...");
	    shipmentRequest = vmTemp.currentShipment;
		// Validate shipmentRequest and Packages array
		if (!shipmentRequest || !shipmentRequest.Packages || !Array.isArray(shipmentRequest.Packages)) {
			console.error("❌ [PreShip Error] Shipment request is invalid or missing required properties.");
			//alert("[PreShip Error] Shipment request is invalid or missing required properties.");
			return;
		}
	
		let validDimensions = [];
	
		console.log(`📦 [PreShip] Processing ${shipmentRequest.Packages.length} package(s)...`);
	
		// Retrieve current package dimensions from vmTemp
		try {
			let currentPackage = vmTemp.currentShipment.Packages[vmTemp.packageIndex];
			if (!currentPackage || !currentPackage.Dimensions) {
				console.warn("⚠️ [PreShip Warning] vmTemp.currentShipment package or dimensions not found.");
			} else {
				let dims = currentPackage.Dimensions;
				console.log(`📏 [PreShip] Current Package Dimensions from vmTemp: ${dims.Length}x${dims.Width}x${dims.Height} 0`);
			}
		} catch (error) {
			console.error("❌ [PreShip Error] Unable to retrieve package dimensions from vmTemp.");
		}
	
		// Loop through all packages to validate their dimensions
		for (let i = 0; i < shipmentRequest.Packages.length; i++) {
			console.log(`🔍 [PreShip] Checking package at index ${i}...`);
	
			let packageData = shipmentRequest.Packages[i];
	
			if (!packageData) {
				console.error(`❌ [PreShip Error] Package at index ${i} is undefined.`);
				//alert(`[PreShip Error] Package at index ${i} is undefined.`);
				return;
			}
	
			if (!packageData.Dimensions) {
				console.warn(`⚠️ [PreShip Warning] Package at index ${i} does not contain 'Dimensions'.`);
				//alert(`[PreShip Error] Package at index ${i} does not contain 'Dimensions'.`);
				return;
			}
	
			let dims = packageData.Dimensions;
	
			// Ensure all dimension values exist and are valid numbers
			if (dims.Length > 0 && dims.Width > 0 && dims.Height > 0) {
				let dimensionString = `${dims.Length}x${dims.Width}x${dims.Height} 0`; // Always append "0"
	
				// Validate format (three numeric values + "0" at the end)
				let dimParts = dimensionString.split(new RegExp("[x ]"), 4); // Split on 'x' and space
	
				if (dimParts.length === 4 && !isNaN(dimParts[0]) && !isNaN(dimParts[1]) && !isNaN(dimParts[2]) && dimParts[3] === "0") {
					validDimensions.push(dimensionString);
					console.log(`✅ [PreShip] Package ${i} Dimensions: ${dimensionString}`);
				} else {
					console.error(`❌ [PreShip Error] Package at index ${i} has incorrectly formatted dimensions: ${dimensionString}`);
					//alert(`[PreShip Error] Package at index ${i} has incorrectly formatted dimensions.`);
					return;
				}
			} else {
				console.error(`❌ [PreShip Error] Package at index ${i} has invalid dimensions.`);
				//alert(`[PreShip Error] Package at index ${i} has invalid dimensions.`);
				return;
			}
		}
	
		// Store only valid dimensions in MiscReference5
		if (validDimensions.length > 0) {
			shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.MiscReference5 = validDimensions.join(", ");
			console.log(`✅ [PreShip] All dimensions successfully stored in MiscReference5: ${shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.MiscReference5}`);
		} else {
			console.warn("⚠️ [PreShip Warning] No packages had valid dimensions.");
		}
	
		// Retrieve weight and markup values
		userParams.weight = $('div[caption="Weight"]').find('input[name="unitValue_txt"]').val();
		userParams.markup = $("#custom_markup_id").val();
		console.log(`📏 [PreShip] Retrieved weight: ${userParams.weight}, Markup: ${userParams.markup}`);
	
		// Custom code to hide/filter on postship errors - must be started here
		$("<style> .alert-danger { display: none; } </style>").appendTo("head");
		console.log("🚫 [PreShip] Hidden alert-danger elements to prevent UI issues.");
	
		alertInterval = setInterval(function () {
			var errAlert = $('div.alert-danger');
		
			// Filter and show alert
			if (errAlert.length > 0) {
				clearInterval(alertInterval);
				let msg = errAlert.text();
				if (msg.indexOf('-1') === -1 && msg.indexOf('CONNECTSHIP') === -1) {
					errAlert.show();
					console.warn(`⚠️ [PreShip Warning] PostShip Alert Detected: ${msg}`);
				}
			}
		}, 200);
	
		console.log("✅ [PreShip] Function completed successfully.");
	};

// this.PostShip(shipmentRequest, shipmentResponse) // returns void

// Source: EATON CORPORATION (EATON)_Eaton Business Rules_1772.cs
// PostSelectAddressBook(shipmentRequest, nameaddress) // returns undefined
    this.PostSelectAddressBook = function (shipmentRequest, nameaddress) {
        var stName;
        var vmExists = false;

        var customData1 = PullCustomData(nameaddress.CustomData, "Custom1");
        var customData2 = PullCustomData(nameaddress.CustomData, "Custom2");
        var customData3 = PullCustomData(nameaddress.CustomData, "Custom3");

        if (typeof objVM === "undefined") {
            stName = shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.OriginAddress.Company;
            shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ConsigneeReference = customData2 + "~" + stName;
        } else {
            vmExists = true;
            stName = objVM.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.OriginAddress.Company;
            objVM.currentShipment.Packages[0].ConsigneeReference = isDefined(customData2) + "~" + stName;
        }
        // alert("customData2 = " + customData2);


        if (isDefined(customData3) == "FC") {
            if (vmExists === true) {
                objVM.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Terms = "CONSIGNEE";
            } else {
                shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Terms = "CONSIGNEE";
            }
            nameaddress.Account = isDefined(customData1);
        }

        function PullCustomData(consignee, field) {
            //alert(JSON.stringify(consignee));

            for (var item in consignee) {
                if (consignee[item].Key == field) return consignee[item].Value;
            }
        }

        function isDefined(referenceValue) {
            var goodValue = null;
            if (typeof referenceValue == "undefined" ||
                referenceValue === null) {
                goodValue = "";
            } else {
                goodValue = referenceValue;
            }
            return goodValue;
        }
    };

// PreShip(shipmentRequest, userParams) // returns undefined
    this.PreShip = function (shipmentRequest, userParams) {
        if (shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ReturnDeliveryMethod !== null &&
            typeof shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ReturnDeliveryMethod !== "undefined") shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Terms = "SHIPPER";
    };

// PreRate(shipmentRequest, userParams) // returns undefined
    this.PreRate = function (shipmentRequest, userParams) {
        shipmentRequest.Packages.forEach(function (pkg) {
            // Updates code to get UserId from the vm instead of an API call
            pkg.MiscReference20 = vm.UserInformation.UserId;  
        });

        for (var i = 0; i < shipmentRequest.Packages.length; i++) {
            var sfState = getStateAbbreviation(shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.OriginAddress.StateProvince);
            if (sfState !== null &&
                typeof sfState !== "undefined") {
                shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.OriginAddress.StateProvince = sfState;
            }
        }
    };

// setInternationalPackaging(shipmentRequest, nameAddress) // returns undefined
function setInternationalPackaging(shipmentRequest, nameAddress) {
        var isInternational = nameAddress.Country != 'US';
        $('[property="Packaging"] select').prop('disabled', isInternational);
        if (isInternational) {
            var packages = shipmentRequest.Packages;
            for (var i = 0; i < packages.length; i++) {
                packages[i].Packaging = 'LETTER';
            }
        }
    }

// PageLoaded(location) // returns void
  this.PageLoaded = function(location)
  {

    if (location == '/shipping')
    {
      $(function()
      {
        $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].Description"]').val('DOCUMENTS');
        $('div[ng-hide="vm.profile.FieldOptions.Consignee.IsHidden"]').delegate('input[ng-model="nameaddress.Code"]', 'blur', function(e)
        {
          $('div[ng-hide="vm.profile.FieldOptions.Consignee.IsHidden"] button[ng-click="search(nameaddress)"]').trigger('click');
        });
      });
    }

    if (location == '/batchmanager')
    {
      $(document).ready(function()
      {
        $.globalEval('var userContext;');

        $('#batchUpdateTabs').delegate('li', 'click', function(e)
        {
          e.preventDefault();
          e.stopImmediatePropagation();
          e.stopPropagation();

          var i = $(this).attr('index');
          UIMethods.SwitchToTab(i);
        });

        $('body').delegate('input[required]', 'keydown', function(e)
        {
          $(this).removeClass('has-error');
        });

        $('body').delegate('#buttonBulkEditBatch', 'click', function(e)
        {
          BatchClass.EditThisBatch(this);
        });

        $('body').delegate('#checkboxthirdparty', 'click', function(e)
        {
          BatchClass.CheckForThirdPartyBilling();
        });

        $('body').delegate('#buttonBulkUpdateBatch', 'click', function(e)
        {
          BatchClass.UpdateCurrentBatch();
        });

        $('body').delegate('#buttonCancelBulkUpdateBatch', 'click', function(e)
        {
          BatchClass.CancelUpdateCurrentBatch();
        });

      });
    }
  }

// UpdateCurrentBatch() // returns void
      UpdateCurrentBatch: function()
      {
        if (CheckForRequiredValues() == false) { return false; }

        //var UserMethod = {};
        //UserMethod.ServerMethod = 'UpdateBatchData';

        var dataObject = {};

        dataObject.BatchReference = $('.batch-id').text();
        dataObject.Shipper = $('#selectshippers option:selected').val();
        dataObject.PackageType = $('#selectpackagetype option:selected').val();
        dataObject.DeliveryConfirmation = $('#checkboxdeliveryconfirmation').prop('checked');
        dataObject.SignatureRequired = $('#deliveryconfirmationcontainer input[type=radio]:checked').val();
        dataObject.BillingOption = $('#selectbilling option:selected').val();

        dataObject.Telephone = $('#inputphone').val();
        dataObject.PackageWeight = $('#inputweight').val();
        dataObject.PackageDeclaredValue = $('#inputdeclared').val();
        dataObject.Client = $('#inputclient').val();
        dataObject.GoodsDescription = $('#inputgoods').val();
        dataObject.ConsigneeAccount = $('#inputaccountnumber').val();

        dataObject.DomesticServiceMethod = $('#selectdomesticservice option:selected').val();
        dataObject.InternationalServiceMethod = $('#selectintlservice option:selected').val();
        dataObject.DomesticSaturday = $('#checkboxdomesticsaturdaydel').prop('checked');
        dataObject.DomesticInternational = $('#checkboxintlsaturdaydel').prop('checked');

        dataObject.ThirdPartyBilling = false;

        if ($('#checkboxthirdparty').prop('checked') == true)
        {
          /* Need to add 3rd party billing data. */
          dataObject.ThirdPartyBilling = true;
          dataObject.ThirdPartyCompany = $('#inputThirdPartyCompany').val().trim();
          dataObject.ThirdPartyContact = $('#inputThirdPartyContact').val().trim();
          dataObject.ThirdPartyAddress1 = $('#inputThirdPartyAddress1').val().trim();
          dataObject.ThirdPartyAddress2 = $('#inputThirdPartyAddress2').val().trim();
          dataObject.ThirdPartyAddress3 = $('#inputThirdPartyAddress3').val().trim();
          dataObject.ThirdPartyCity = $('#inputThirdPartyCity').val().trim();
          dataObject.ThirdPartyState = $('#inputThirdPartyState').val().trim();
          dataObject.ThirdPartyPostalCode = $('#inputThirdPartyPostalCode').val().trim();
          dataObject.ThirdPartyAccount = $('#inputThirdPartyAccount').val().trim();
          dataObject.ThirdPartyCountry = $('#selectThirdPartyCountry option:selected').val().replace("string:", "");
        }

        this.MakeUserMethodRequest('UpdateBatchData', dataObject).then(function() { $('#divCustomTabContainer').fadeOut(); });

        //UserMethod.MethodData = dataObject;
      }

// Source: F Schumacher (FSCHUMAC)_Product Area (8942X4) CBR_1801.cs
// AddCommoditiesToPackage(CommodityContents, CurrentPackage) // returns void
      AddCommoditiesToPackage: function(CommodityContents, CurrentPackage)
      {
        /* The commodityContent object has a number of items that can't be pushed to the shipmentRequest array. */
        /* Create a new object just with the items needed in the shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex].CommodityContents array. */
        try
        {
          if (!CurrentPackage.CommodityContents)
          {
            CurrentPackage.CommodityContents = [];
          }

          /* GetTranslatedUnitOfMeasurement() can be handled on the server side, it's only here because I pulled this code out of the PackVerify class. */
          /* EntryId is not needed. */
          $(CommodityContents).each(function(x, item)
          {
            /* Map the CommodityContent object here that will be used on the server.  */
            var CommodityObject =
            {
              UnitWeight: { Amount: '1' },
              Quantity: item.COMMODITY_CONTENTS_QUANTITY,
              ProductCode: item.COMMODITY_CONTENTS_PRODUCT_CODE,
              UnitValue: { Amount: item.COMMODITY_CONTENTS_UNIT_VALUE, Currency: 'USD' },
              QuantityUnitMeasure: GetTranslatedUnitOfMeasurement(item.COMMODITY_CONTENTS_QUANTITY_UNIT_MEASURE),
              Description: item.COMMODITY_CONTENTS_DESCRIPTION,
              OriginCountry: item.COMMODITY_CONTENTS_ORIGIN_COUNTRY.length > 0 ? item.COMMODITY_CONTENTS_ORIGIN_COUNTRY : 'US',
              ConsigneePostalCode: item.CONSIGNEE_POSTALCODE ? item.CONSIGNEE_POSTALCODE.substring(0, 5) : null,
              EntryId: GetRandomNumber(8),
              OrderNumber: item.Order_Number,
              HarmonizedCode: item.COMMODITY_CONTENTS_TARRIFFCODE1,
              HarmonizedCode2: item.COMMODITY_CONTENTS_TARRIFCODE2,
              AverageWeight: item.COMMODITY_CONTENTS_AVERAGEWEIGHT,
              UserData1: item.COMMODITY_CONTENTS_COMMENTS
            };

            CurrentPackage.CommodityContents.push(CommodityObject);
          });

          /* The UpdateCommodities function updates the view in the UI by clicking the pagination buttons. */
          UpdateCommodities(CurrentPackage.CommodityContents);
        }
        catch (error)
        {
          console.log(error.message);
        }
      }

// GetTranslatedUnitOfMeasurement(sVal) // returns translated unit code string
      function GetTranslatedUnitOfMeasurement(sVal)
      {
        switch (sVal.toUpperCase())
        {
          case 'EACH':
            return 'EA';
          case 'YARDS':
          case 'YARD':
            return 'YD';
          case 'METER':
            return 'M';
          case 'SF':
            return 'SFT';
          case 'PAIR':
            return 'PR';
          case 'SR':
            return 'ROL';
          default:
            return sVal;
        }
      }

// CheckForMatchingConsignee(CustomerOrderObject) // returns true if consignee fields match, otherwise false
      CheckForMatchingConsignee: function(CustomerOrderObject)
      {
        try
        {
          var con = $('name-address[nameaddress="vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Consignee"]');
          var a = {
            conCompany: $(con).find('input[name="company"]').val().trim().toUpperCase(),
            conAddress1: $(con).find('input[name="address1"]').val().trim().toUpperCase(),
            conCity: $(con).find('input[name="city"]').val().trim().toUpperCase(),
            conState: $(con).find('input[name="stateProvince"]').val().trim().toUpperCase(),
            conPostalCode: $(con).find('input[name="postalCode"]').val().trim().substring(0, 5).toUpperCase()
          };

          var hdr = CustomerOrderObject.Header;
          console.log(hdr);
          var b = {
            conCompany: hdr.CONSIGNEE_COMPANY.trim().toUpperCase(),
            conAddress1: hdr.CONSIGNEE_ADDRESS_LINE_1.trim().toUpperCase(),
            conCity: hdr.CONSIGNEE_CITY.trim().toUpperCase(),
            conState: hdr.CONSIGNEE_STATEPROVINCE.trim().toUpperCase(),
            conPostalCode: hdr.CONSIGNEE_POSTALCODE.trim().substring(0, 5).toUpperCase()
          };

          /* Remove all the spaces in the strings so we get a good comparison, not one that's thrown off by an extra space. */
          let aa = JSON.stringify(a).replaceAll(' ', '');
          let bb = JSON.stringify(b).replaceAll(' ', '');

          /* Quick comparison to see if the strings match. */
          if (aa != bb)
          {
            console.log(`CheckForMatchingConsignee(), Message: Could not add order ${CustomerOrderObject.orderNumber} (${CustomerOrderObject.orderId}). Primary order data to follow.`);
            console.log('Primary order: ', a);
            console.log('Secondary order: ', b);
          }

          return aa == bb;
        }
        catch (error)
        {
          console.log(error.message);
        }
      }

// UpdateReferencesWithOrderNumbers(OrderNumber) // returns void
      UpdateReferencesWithOrderNumbers: function(OrderNumber)
      {
        var inputShipperReference = $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].ShipperReference"]');
        var inputMiscReference07 = $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference7"]');
        var shipperReferenceVal = $(inputShipperReference).val() + ',' + OrderNumber;
        var newUniqueString = Tools.GetUniqueCSVStringFromString(shipperReferenceVal);

        /* Set these input values.  ShipperReference is used by the customer, MiscReference7 is used by the SBR to update each record post-ship. */
        /* ShipperReference ONLY keeps the first order number when it goes to PostShip, before the comma, MiscReference7 keeps the entire string. */
        /* On the server-side, if MiscReference7 contains a comma, each item in the csv list gets posted back.  If MiscReference7 is empty, the ShipperReference is used instead for a single post-back. */
        $(inputShipperReference).val(newUniqueString).trigger('change');
        $(inputMiscReference07).val(newUniqueString).trigger('change');
      }

// UpdateCommodities(PackageIndex) // returns undefined
function UpdateCommodities (PackageIndex)
    {
      /* Click the active tab, just to refresh the commodities.  This will only work on the first commodity added. */
      $('div.ui-tab-container > div.ng-isolate-scope > ul > li.active > a').click();

      /* Clicking the button below refreshes the full commodities list in the UI. */
      $('#goods').find('div.ng-table-counts.btn-group').find('button:not(.active):first').click();
    }

// GetTranslatedUnitOfMeasurement(sVal) // returns translated unit string
function GetTranslatedUnitOfMeasurement (sVal)
    {
      switch (sVal.toUpperCase())
      {
        case "EACH":
          return "EA";
        case "YARDS":
        case "YARD":
          return "YD";
        case "METER":
          return "M";
        case "SF":
          return "SFT";
        case "PAIR":
          return "PR";
        case "SR":
          return "ROL";
        default:
          return sVal;
      }
    }

// ProcessDataFromCustomer(jsonData) // returns undefined
ProcessDataFromCustomer: function (jsonData)
      {
        try
        {
          $(jsonData).each(function (a, b)
          {
            /* For testing, this is set to '!== true' so it will return order data.  This needs to be set to '=== true' for any other case. */
            if (ConsolidatedOrders.CheckForMatchingConsignee(b) == true)
            {
              var currentPackage = Tools.GetCurrentPackage();
              if (!currentPackage)
              {
                Tools.ShowErrorAlert('ERROR:  Could not add commodities to package for order ' + b.orderId + '.  See error console for details.');
                return false;
              }
              ConsolidatedOrders.UpdateReferencesWithOrderNumbers(b.orderId, b.orderNumber);
            }
            else
            {
              Tools.ShowErrorAlert('ERROR 500:  Could not add commodities for order ' + b.orderId + '.  Address mismatch.');
            }
          });
        }
        catch (error)
        { 
          console.log(error);
        }
      }

// CheckForMatchingConsignee(CustomerOrderObject) // returns boolean or undefined on error
CheckForMatchingConsignee: function (CustomerOrderObject)
      {
        try
        {
          var con = $('name-address[nameaddress="vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Consignee"]');

          let a = {
            //conCompany: $(con).find('input[name="company"]').val().trim().toUpperCase().replaceAll(' ',''),
            conAddress1: $(con).find('input[name="address1"]').val().trim().toUpperCase(),
            conCity: $(con).find('input[name="city"]').val().trim().toUpperCase(),
            conState: $(con).find('input[name="stateProvince"]').val().trim().toUpperCase(),
            conPostalCode: $(con).find('input[name="postalCode"]').val().trim().substring(0, 5)
          };

          let b = {
            //conCompany: CustomerOrderObject.shipAddress1.CONSIGNEE_COMPANY.trim().toUpperCase().replaceAll(' ', ''),
            conAddress1: CustomerOrderObject.shipAddress1.trim().toUpperCase(),
            conCity: CustomerOrderObject.shipCity.trim().toUpperCase(),
            conState: CustomerOrderObject.shipState.trim().toUpperCase(),
            conPostalCode: CustomerOrderObject.shipZipCode.trim().substring(0, 5)
          };

          /* Remove all the spaces in the strings so we get a good comparison, not one that's thrown off by an extra space. */
          let aa = JSON.stringify(a).replaceAll(' ', '');
          let bb = JSON.stringify(b).replaceAll(' ', '');

          /* Quick comparison to see if the strings match. */
          if (aa != bb)
          {
            Logger.Log({ Source: 'CheckForMatchingConsignee()', Message: 'Could not add order ' + CustomerOrderObject.orderNumber + ' (' + CustomerOrderObject.orderId + '). Primary order data to follow.', Data: a });
            Logger.Log({ Source: 'CheckForMatchingConsignee()', Message: 'Could not add order ' + CustomerOrderObject.orderNumber + ' (' + CustomerOrderObject.orderId + '). Subsequent order data to follow.', Data: b });
          }

          return (aa == bb);
        }
        catch (error)
        {
          Logger.Log({ Source: 'CheckForMatchingConsignee()', Error: error });
        }
      }

// UpdateReferencesWithOrderNumbers(OrderId, OrderNumber) // returns undefined
UpdateReferencesWithOrderNumbers: function (OrderId, OrderNumber)
      {
        var inputShipperReference = $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].ShipperReference"]');
        var inputMiscReference07 = $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference7"]');
        var inputConsigneeReference = $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].ConsigneeReference"]');
        var shipperReferenceVal = $(inputShipperReference).val() + ',' + OrderId;
        var consigneeReferenceVal = $(inputConsigneeReference).val() + ',' + OrderNumber;
        
        var newUniqueString = Tools.GetUniqueCSVStringFromString(shipperReferenceVal);
        var newConsigneeReferenceString = Tools.GetUniqueCSVStringFromString(consigneeReferenceVal);

        /* Set these input values.  ShipperReference is used by the customer, MiscReference7 is used by the SBR to update each record post-ship. */
        /* ShipperReference ONLY keeps the first order number when it goes to PostShip, before the comma, MiscReference7 keeps the entire string. */
        /* On the server-side, if MiscReference7 contains a comma, each item in the csv list gets posted back.  If MiscReference7 is empty, the ShipperReference is used instead for a single post-back. */
        $(inputShipperReference).val(newUniqueString);
        $(inputMiscReference07).val(newUniqueString);
        $(inputConsigneeReference).val(newConsigneeReferenceString);
      }

// function SendFreightCollect(shipmentRequest) // returns undefined
function SendFreightCollect(shipmentRequest) {
        var selection = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference20;
        if (selection.indexOf("-") > -1) {
            var position = selection.indexOf("-");
            shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Account = selection.substring(position + 2);
            shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Terms = "CONSIGNEE";
        } else {
            throw new error({ "number": "001", "description": "Receiver Billing Information not found." });
        }
    }

// Source: FortessaTS (FTS)_FortessaCBR_1897.cs
// customGetWeight() // returns undefined
        function customGetWeight() {
            if (this.profile.ScaleConfiguration) {
                var url = client.config.ClientSupportServiceUrl + '/api/Scale/Read'
                var ret = $.post({ url: url, data: this.profile.ScaleConfiguration.ScaleDefinition, async: false }).responseJSON;
                if (ret != undefined) {
                    if (ret.ErrorCode == 0) {
                        this.currentShipment.Packages[this.packageIndex].Weight = {
                            "Amount": ret.Weight.toFixed(2),
                            "Units": ret.WeightUnit.toUpperCase()
                        };
                    }
                }
            }
        }

// replaceSelectBoxTypeWithInputText(boxTypes) // returns undefined
        function replaceSelectBoxTypeWithInputText(boxTypes) {
            var interval = setInterval(function () {
                client.shipping.$selectBoxType = $('select[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].BoxType"]');
                if (client.shipping.$selectBoxType.length > 0) {
                    clearInterval(interval);
                    client.shipping.$inputBoxType = $('<input type="text" />').attr({ class: client.shipping.$selectBoxType.attr('class') });
                    client.shipping.$selectBoxType.hide();
                    client.shipping.$inputBoxType.insertAfter(client.shipping.$selectBoxType);

                    client.shipping.$inputBoxType.keyup(boxTypes, function (e) {
                        if (e.key === 'Tab' || e.key === "Enter") {
                            for (var boxType of e.data) {
                                if (boxType.Name == this.value) {
                                    this.value = '';
                                    client.shipping.$selectBoxType.val(boxType.Id).change();
                                    client.shipping.addPackageButton.focus();
                                }
                            }
                        }
                    });

                }
            }, 10);
        }

// this.GetShipToAddressCustomData() // returns the consignee address book CustomData object
this.GetShipToAddressCustomData = function(){
        //debugger;
        var payloadShipToAddress = {
            "Skip": 0,
            "Take": 10,
            "WhereClauses": [{
                "FieldName": "Id",
                "FieldValue": consigneeId,
                "Operator": 0
            }]
        };
        
        var data = {
            CompanyId: client.userContext.CompanyId,
            addressBookIds: addrsBookId,
            SearchCriteria: payloadShipToAddress
        };
        //console.log(data);
      
        ShipToAddressBook = client.thinClientAPIRequest('GetAddressBookEntries_AddressBook', data, false).responseJSON;
    
        console.log(ShipToAddressBook.AddressBookEntries[0].CustomData);
        
        return ShipToAddressBook.AddressBookEntries[0].CustomData;
                
    };

// this.PreShip(shipmentRequest, userParams) // returns void
this.PreShip = function(shipmentRequest, userParams) { 
        debugger;
        const st_company = shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Company.toUpperCase();
        addrsBookId = shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.AddressBookId;
        consigneeId = shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Id;
        
        if(st_company == "UPS MI" || st_company.includes("MAIL INNOVATIONS"))
        {
            console.log("Mail Innovatoins Shipment");
            console.log(shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.AddressBook);
            console.log(addrsBookId);
            console.log(consigneeId);
                
            addressCustomData = this.GetShipToAddressCustomData();
            mi_flag = client.getValueByKey('Custom1',addressCustomData);
                  
            if(mi_flag !== "MI_TPB"){
               throw new Error("Please contact GAP ShipExec Admin for Mail Innovation Authorization [Ship-Exec-stores-dg@gap.com].");
            }
            else
            {
               shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ThirdPartyBilling = true;
               shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ThirdPartyBillingAddress = {
                    Company : "UPS Mail Innovations",
                    Contact : "Shipping",
                    Address1 : "13050 Marlay Ave",
                    Address2 : "Suite 100",
                    City : "Fontana",
                    StateProvince : "CA",
                    PostalCode : "92337",
                    Country : "US",
                    Email : "upsusmi01transportation@ups.com",
                    Account : "7500YW"
                };
                      
            }
        }

        if (pooler)
        {
            if (document.getElementById("pooler").checked)
            {
                for (var p of shipmentRequest.Packages)
                {
                    p.MiscReference4 = vm.profile.Shippers[0].Email.replace("@", "").replace(" ", "").replace(".pool", "").replace(".POOL", "").toUpperCase();
                }               
            }
        }

        var misc3reference = "200.30.6035.5102.90059";
        for (var i = 0; i < shipmentRequest.Packages.length; i++) {
            shipmentRequest.Packages[i].MiscReference1 = shipmentRequest.Packages[i].ShipperReference;
            shipmentRequest.Packages[i].ShipperReference = "";
            //Address 1
            if(shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Address1 == "1112 Turkey Mountain Rd.")
            {
                console.log('found 1/4 address');
                shipmentRequest.Packages[i].MiscReference3 = misc3reference;
                shipmentRequest.Packages[i].ShipperReference = misc3reference;
            }
             //Address 2
            if(shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Address1 == "102R Demi Rd.")
            {
                                console.log('found 1/4 address');

                shipmentRequest.Packages[i].MiscReference3 = misc3reference;
                                shipmentRequest.Packages[i].ShipperReference = misc3reference;

            }
              //Address 3
            if(shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Address1 == "17511 S. Susana Rd.")
            {
                                console.log('found 1/4 address');

                shipmentRequest.Packages[i].MiscReference3 = misc3reference;
                                shipmentRequest.Packages[i].ShipperReference = misc3reference;

            }
               //Address 4
            if(shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Address1 == "200 Terminal St.")
            {
                                console.log('found 1/4 address');

                shipmentRequest.Packages[i].MiscReference3 = misc3reference;
                                shipmentRequest.Packages[i].ShipperReference = misc3reference;

            }
        }
        console.log('PRESHIP');
        console.log(shipmentRequest);

    };

this.PreRate = function(shipmentRequest, userParams) {

        if (pooler)
        {
            if (document.getElementById("pooler").checked)
            {  
                //alert( shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Shipper);
                for (var p of shipmentRequest.Packages)
                {
                    p.MiscReference4 = vm.profile.Shippers[0].Email.replace("@", "").replace(" ", "").replace(".pool", "").replace(".POOL", "");

                } 
            }
            else
            {
                for (var p of shipmentRequest.Packages)
                {
                    p.MiscReference4 = ""
                }
            }
        }
    };

// this.PostShip(shipmentRequest, shipmentResponse) // returns void
    this.PostShip = function(shipmentRequest, shipmentResponse) {
        canadaSelected = false;
        var misc3reference = "200.30.6035.5102.90059";
        for (var i = 0; i < shipmentRequest.Packages.length; i++) {
            shipmentRequest.Packages[i].MiscReference1 = shipmentRequest.Packages[i].ShipperReference;
            shipmentRequest.Packages[i].ShipperReference = "";
            //Address 1
            if(shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Address1 == "1112 Turkey Mountain Rd.")
            {
                console.log('found 1/4 address');
                shipmentRequest.Packages[i].MiscReference3 = misc3reference;
                shipmentRequest.Packages[i].ShipperReference = misc3reference;
            }
             //Address 2
            if(shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Address1 == "102R Demi Rd.")
            {
                                console.log('found 1/4 address');
     
                shipmentRequest.Packages[i].MiscReference3 = misc3reference;
                                shipmentRequest.Packages[i].ShipperReference = misc3reference;
     
            }
              //Address 3
            if(shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Address1 == "17511 S. Susana Rd.")
            {
                                console.log('found 1/4 address');
     
                shipmentRequest.Packages[i].MiscReference3 = misc3reference;
                                shipmentRequest.Packages[i].ShipperReference = misc3reference;
     
            }
               //Address 4
            if(shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Address1 == "200 Terminal St.")
            {
                                console.log('found 1/4 address');
     
                shipmentRequest.Packages[i].MiscReference3 = misc3reference;
                                shipmentRequest.Packages[i].ShipperReference = misc3reference;
     
            }
            
            var company = shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Company.toLowerCase();
            if(company.indexOf("mail innov") != -1 || company.startsWith("ups mi") || company.startsWith("ups mail"))
            {
                if (mi_tpb_stores.find(element => element == this.vm.profile.Shippers[0].Symbol) !== null)
                {
                    console.log("Billing MI as TPB");
                    shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ThirdPartyBilling = true;
                    var tpb = {};
                    angular.copy(shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee, tpb);
                    tpb.Account = "7500YW";
                    tpb.Company = "UPS MAIL INNOVATIONS";
                    tpb.Contact = "REBECA CARBRERA";
                    tpb.Address1 = "13050 MARLAY AVE";
                    tpb.City = "FONTANA";
                    tpb.StateProvince = "CA";
                    tpb.PostalCode = "92337";
                    tpb.Country = "US";
                    tpb.Phone = "555-555-555";
                    shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ThirdPartyBillingAddress = tpb;
                }
            }
            
        }
        console.log('PRESHIP');
        console.log(shipmentRequest);
    }

// Source: GAP INC (GAPMailrooms)_DirectToMobileCBR_1918.cs
// function ConfigureD2MShipment(calleeMethod) // returns void
function ConfigureD2MShipment(calleeMethod){
        
        debugger;
        		
		LogStartMethod("ConfigureD2MShipment()",calleeMethod);
				
		var infoMessage = "D2M shipment ";
		
		if (location.hash === '#!/shipping')		
		{
			if (CurrentShipperIsD2MEnabled() && CurrentUserIsD2MEnabled()) 
			{
				infoMessage += "is ENABLED for current shipper and current user";
				
				var originAddressCompany;
				
				var originAddressLoadedInterval = setInterval(function(){
					originAddressCompany = $('[name="company"]:eq(1)').val();
					if (originAddressCompany!=undefined && originAddressCompany.length)
					{
						EnableReturn();
						clearInterval(originAddressLoadedInterval);	
					}
				},50);
			}
			else
			{
				infoMessage += "is NOT ENABLED for shipper and user";
				var isLoaded;
				var removeD2M = setInterval(function(){
					isLoaded = $('#DirectToMobileShipmentID').is(":checked");
					if (isLoaded!=undefined && (isLoaded === false || isLoaded === false))
					{												
						$('#d2m_checkbox_div_id').remove();						
						DisableReturn();
						clearInterval(removeD2M);	
					}
				},50);
				
				
			}
		}
		else
		{
			infoMessage = "WARNING " + infoMessage + "called outside of shipping action";
		}
		LogMethodInfo(infoMessage);
    }

        $('[name="address2"]:eq(1)').trigger("change");

        $('[name="stateProvince"]:eq(1)').trigger("change");
