// function EnableReturn() // returns void
function EnableReturn()
	{		
		vm.profile.FieldOptions["ReturnAddress.Account"].IsHidden = true;
		vm.profile.FieldOptions["ReturnAddress.Address1"].IsRequired = true;
		vm.profile.FieldOptions["ReturnAddress.Address2"].IsHidden = true;
		vm.profile.FieldOptions["ReturnAddress.Address3"].IsHidden = true;
		vm.profile.FieldOptions["ReturnAddress.City"].IsRequired = true;
		vm.profile.FieldOptions["ReturnAddress.Code"].IsHidden = true;
		vm.profile.FieldOptions["ReturnAddress.Company"].IsRequired = true;
		vm.profile.FieldOptions["ReturnAddress.Contact"].IsRequired = true;
		vm.profile.FieldOptions["ReturnAddress.Country"].IsRequired = true;
		vm.profile.FieldOptions["ReturnAddress.Email"].IsHidden = true;
		vm.profile.FieldOptions["ReturnAddress.Fax"].IsHidden = true;
		vm.profile.FieldOptions["ReturnAddress.Group"].IsHidden = true;
		vm.profile.FieldOptions["ReturnAddress.Phone"].IsHidden = true;
		vm.profile.FieldOptions["ReturnAddress.PostalCode"].IsRequired = true;
		vm.profile.FieldOptions["ReturnAddress.StateProvince"].IsRequired = true;
		vm.profile.FieldOptions["ReturnAddress.TaxId"].IsHidden = true;
		vm.profile.FieldOptions["ReturnAddress.AccountNumberTaxIdTab"].IsHidden = true;
		vm.profile.FieldOptions["ReturnAddress.EmailTab"].IsHidden = true;
		vm.profile.FieldOptions["ReturnAddress.PhoneFaxTab"].IsHidden = true;
	}

// function DisableReturn() // returns void
function DisableReturn()
	{
		vm.profile.FieldOptions["ReturnAddress.Account"].IsHidden = true;
		vm.profile.FieldOptions["ReturnAddress.Account"].IsRequired = false;
		vm.profile.FieldOptions["ReturnAddress.Address1"].IsHidden = true;
		vm.profile.FieldOptions["ReturnAddress.Address1"].IsRequired = false
		vm.profile.FieldOptions["ReturnAddress.Address2"].IsHidden = true;
		vm.profile.FieldOptions["ReturnAddress.Address2"].IsRequired = false;
		vm.profile.FieldOptions["ReturnAddress.Address3"].IsHidden = true;
		vm.profile.FieldOptions["ReturnAddress.Address3"].IsRequired = false;
		vm.profile.FieldOptions["ReturnAddress.City"].IsHidden = true;
		vm.profile.FieldOptions["ReturnAddress.City"].IsRequired = false;
		vm.profile.FieldOptions["ReturnAddress.Code"].IsHidden = true;
		vm.profile.FieldOptions["ReturnAddress.Code"].IsRequired = false;
		vm.profile.FieldOptions["ReturnAddress.Company"].IsHidden = true;
		vm.profile.FieldOptions["ReturnAddress.Company"].IsRequired = false;
		vm.profile.FieldOptions["ReturnAddress.Contact"].IsHidden = true;
		vm.profile.FieldOptions["ReturnAddress.Contact"].IsRequired = false;
		vm.profile.FieldOptions["ReturnAddress.Country"].IsHidden = true;
		vm.profile.FieldOptions["ReturnAddress.Country"].IsRequired = false;
		vm.profile.FieldOptions["ReturnAddress.Email"].IsHidden = true;
		vm.profile.FieldOptions["ReturnAddress.Email"].IsRequired = false;
		vm.profile.FieldOptions["ReturnAddress.Fax"].IsHidden = true;

// function GetReturnAddresses() // returns returnAddressList or undefined
function GetReturnAddresses()
	{
		var userMethodParams = { "action": "GetD2MAddressBook"};
		
		var data = { Data: JSON.stringify(userMethodParams), UserContext: client.userContext };
		
		var returnAddressList = undefined;
		
		thinClientAPIRequest('UserMethod', data, false).done(function (response) {
			
			if (response.ErrorCode != 0) 
			{
				alert(response.ErrorMessage);
			} 
			else 
			{
				
				var json = DecodeReturnString(response.Data);
				returnAddressList = json.ReturnAddressList;		
				returnAddressList.forEach(function (returnAddress) {
					var x = returnAddress;
					console.log(x);
				});
			}
		});
		return returnAddressList;
	}

// function DecodeReturnString(data) // returns parsed JSON object or undefined
function DecodeReturnString(data)
	{ 
	  try
	  { 
		return JSON.parse($("<div />").html(data).text());
	  }
	  catch (error)
	  { 
		console.log(error.name);
		console.log(error.message);
		console.log(data);
	  }
	}

// handleSpecificCases() // returns undefined
            handleSpecificCases: function() {
                $('h5:contains("No commodities added")').text('Aucune marchandise ajoutée');
                $('label.control-label.no-left-padding.ng-binding').each(function() {
                    if ($(this).attr('style') === "text-align: center" && $(this).html() === "&nbsp;of&nbsp;&nbsp;1") {

                });

// AddPackage(shipmentRequest, packageIndex) // returns undefined
    this.AddPackage = function(shipmentRequest, packageIndex) {
       
        $('label.control-label.no-left-padding.ng-binding').each(function() {
            // Check if the label has the correct style and text
            if ($(this).attr('style') === "text-align: center" && $(this).html() === "&nbsp;de&nbsp;&nbsp;"+ (packageIndex)) {
                // Change the label's text
                $(this).html('&nbsp;de&nbsp;&nbsp;' + (packageIndex+1));
            }
        });
    }

// RemovePackage(shipmentRequest, packageIndex) // returns undefined
    this.RemovePackage = function(shipmentRequest, packageIndex) {
       
        $('label.control-label.no-left-padding.ng-binding').each(function() {
            // Check if the label has the correct style and text
            if ($(this).attr('style') === "text-align: center" && $(this).html() === "&nbsp;de&nbsp;&nbsp;"+ (packageIndex+2)) {
                // Change the label's text
                $(this).html('&nbsp;de&nbsp;&nbsp;' + (packageIndex+1));
            }
        });
    }

// this.PostLoad(loadValue, shipmentRequest) // returns void
  this.PostLoad = function (loadValue, shipmentRequest)
  {
    try
    {
      //alert = function(){}
      this.vm.getWeight();

    }
    catch (error)
    {
      console.log("Error getting weight")
    }
    if (!shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.UserData1)
    {
      client.alert.Danger("Loaded Value " + loadValue + " not found")
    } else
    {
      const Lines = JSON.parse(shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.UserData1);
      Lines.forEach(line =>
      {
        const fila = document.createElement("tr");
        fila.innerHTML = `
            <td>${line.LineNo}</td>
            <td>${line.ItemNo}</td>
            <td>${line.TotalOrderQuantity}</td>
            <td>${line.SaleUnitOfMeasure}</td>
            <td>${line.SaleUnitPrice}</td>
            <td>${line.ItemDescription}</td>
            <td></td>
            <td>${line.UnitWeight}</td>
            <td></td>
            <td>0</td>
            <td>0</td>
            <td><button class='btn btn-xs btn-success glyphicon glyphicon-plus'></button></td>
            <td hidden>${line.IsKitOrBundle}</td>
            <td hidden>${line.KitDetails ? JSON.stringify(line.KitDetails) : "[]"}</td>
            <td hidden>${line.InternationalDetails ? line.InternationalDetails.CountryOfOrigin : ""}</td>
            <td hidden>${line.InternationalDetails ? line.InternationalDetails.ExportCurrencyCode : ""}</td>
            <td hidden>${line.InternationalDetails ? line.InternationalDetails.ExportTariffCode : ""}</td>
            <td hidden>${line.InternationalDetails ? line.InternationalDetails.ExportUnitPrice : ""}</td>
            `;
        if (line.IsKitOrBundle && line.KitDetails == null)
        {
          client.alert.Danger("WARNING: Kit Details are empty when Commodity Set to Kit");
        }
        document.querySelector("#miTabla").appendChild(fila);
      });
      editableTable();

      const buttons = document.querySelectorAll("#miTabla button");
      buttons.forEach(button =>
      {
        button.addEventListener("click", function ()
        {
          const fila = this.parentElement.parentElement;
          AddCommodity(fila, 1, 0);
        });
      });
      const tabla = document.querySelector("#miTabla");
      tabla.classList.remove("hidden");
    }
    console.log(shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Shipdate)
    var today = new Date();
    shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Shipdate.Day = today.getDate();
    shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Shipdate.Year = today.getFullYear();
    shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Shipdate.Month = today.getMonth() + 1;
    if (shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Country != null && shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Country != 'US')
    {
      for (var ii = 0; ii < shipmentRequest.Packages.length; ii++)
      {
        shipmentRequest.Packages[ii].CommercialInvoiceMethod = 1;
        if (shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Country == 'GB')
        {
            console.log(shipmentRequest.Packages[ii]);
            shipmentRequest.Packages[ii].AdditionalHardcopyDocumentation = false;
        }
      }
      
    }

  }

// function AddAll() // returns void
  function AddAll()
  {
    var rows = document.querySelectorAll("#miTabla")[0].rows;

    for (var ii = 0; ii < rows.length; ii++)
    {
      if (ii != 0)
      {
        var commodityPerPkg = rows[ii].cells[2].textContent;
        rows[ii].cells[10].textContent = commodityPerPkg;
        AddCommodity(rows[ii], 1, 0);
        rows[ii].cells[10].textContent = 0;
      }
    }
  }

// function Split() // returns void
  function Split()
  {
    var TotalPackages = vm.currentShipment.Packages.length - (vm.packageIndex);

    var rows = document.querySelectorAll("#miTabla")[0].rows;

    for (var ii = 0; ii < rows.length; ii++)
    {
      if (ii != 0)
      {
        var commodityPerPkg = Math.floor(rows[ii].cells[2].textContent / (TotalPackages));
        console.log("Packages: " + commodityPerPkg)
        for (let i = vm.packageIndex; i < vm.currentShipment.Packages.length; i++)
        {
          console.log("Adding package: " + i)
          console.log(rows[ii])
          rows[ii].cells[10].textContent = commodityPerPkg;
          AddCommodity(rows[ii], 0, i);
        }
        rows[ii].cells[10].textContent = 0;
      }
    }


  }

// function AddCommodity(fila, Type, newPackageIndex) // returns void
  function AddCommodity(fila, Type, newPackageIndex)
  {
    console.log("Trying to get package for index: " + newPackageIndex)
    if (fila.cells[2].textContent == "" || fila.cells[2].textContent == 0)
    {
      client.alert.Danger("No Commodity Left");
      return;
    }
    if (fila.cells[10].textContent == "" || Number(fila.cells[10].textContent) <= 0 || isNaN(fila.cells[10].textContent))
    {
      client.alert.Danger("Invalid Amount to Ship: ");
      return;
    }
    console.log("10: " + fila.cells[10].textContent)
    console.log("2: " + fila.cells[2].textContent)
    if (Number(fila.cells[10].textContent) > Number(fila.cells[2].textContent))
    {
      client.alert.Danger("Ship Quantity can't be more that QTY ");
      return;
    }
    var packageIndex = 0;
    if (Type == 1)
    {
      packageIndex = vm.packageIndex;
    } else
    {
      packageIndex = newPackageIndex;
    }
    console.log(fila.cells[12].textContent ? fila.cells[12].textContent : "Not found in cell 12");
    console.log("Getting isBundle: " + fila.cells[12].textContent)
    if (fila.cells[12] && fila.cells[12].textContent == "true")
    {
      console.log("Bundle")
      console.log(fila.cells[13].textContent)
      var kitDetails = JSON.parse(fila.cells[13].textContent)
      if (kitDetails.length < 1)
      {
        client.alert.Danger("WARNING: Kit Details are empty when Commodity Set to Kit");
        fila.cells[10].textContent = 0;
        return;
      } else
      {
        kitDetails.forEach(detail =>
        {
          console.log(detail)
          console.log(detail.KitComponentPartDesc)
          detail.UnitsPerAssembly = detail.UnitsPerAssembly * fila.cells[10].textContent;
          console.log("Adding units: " + detail.UnitsPerAssembly)
          addToCommodityList(detail, packageIndex, true)
        });
      }
    } else
    {
      console.log("Not bundle")
      addToCommodityList(fila.cells, packageIndex, false)
    }

    fila.cells[2].textContent = fila.cells[2].textContent - fila.cells[10].textContent;
    fila.cells[10].textContent = 0;
    console.log(vm.currentShipment.Packages[packageIndex].CommodityContents);
  }

// function addToCommodityList(cells, index, isBundle) // returns void
  function addToCommodityList(cells, index, isBundle)
  {
    var OldCommodity = vm.currentShipment.Packages[index].CommodityContents;
    var NewCommodity;
    let min = 5;
    let max = 100;
    let randomNumber = Math.floor(Math.random() * (max - min + 1)) + min;
    let anotherRandom = Date.now().toString(36) + Math.random().toString(36).substr(2, 12);
    if (!cells || cells === "")
    {
      client.alert.Danger("Error: Commodity Data unavailable");
      console.log(cells);
      return;
    }
    if (isBundle)
    {
      let price = 0;
      if (cells.InternationalInfo == null || cells.InternationalInfo.ExportUnitPrice == null)
      {
        price = cells.SaleUnitPrice
        console.log('Value price updated to: ' + price)
      } else
      {
        price = cells.InternationalInfo.ExportUnitPrice
        console.log('Value price updated 2: ' + price)
      }
      NewCommodity = [
        {
          "UnitValue": {
            "Currency": cells.InternationalInfo.ExportCurrencyCode,
            "Amount": price
          },
          "UnitWeight": {
            "Units": "LB",
            "Amount": cells.UnitWeight
          },
          "QuantityUnitMeasure": "PC",
          "ExportQuantityUnitMeasure1": "PC",
          "ExportQuantityUnitMeasure2": "PC",
          "LicenseUnitValue": {
            "Currency": "USD"
          },
          "DdtcUnitMeasure": "PC",
          "packageIndex": index,
          "Origin": {
            "AddressBookIdToProcess": null
          },
          "OriginCountry": cells.InternationalInfo.CountryOfOrigin,
          "ProductCode": cells.KitComponentPart,
          "HarmonizedCode": cells.InternationalInfo.ExportTariffCode,
          "Quantity": cells.UnitsPerAssembly,
          "Description": cells.KitComponentPartDesc,
          "LicenseExpirationDate": null,
          "NaftaRvcAvgStartDate": null,
          "nAFTARVCAvgEndDate": null,
          "$$hashKey": "object:" + index + "1" + anotherRandom
        }];
    } else
    {
      let price = 0;
      if (cells[17].textContent == null || cells[17].textContent == "")
      {
        price = cells[4].textContent
        console.log('Value price updated to: ' + price)
      } else
      {
        price = cells[17].textContent
        console.log('Value price updated 2: ' + price)
      }
      NewCommodity = [
        {
          "UnitValue": {
            "Currency": cells[15].textContent,
            "Amount": price
          },
          "UnitWeight": {
            "Units": "LB",
            "Amount": cells[7].textContent
          },
          "QuantityUnitMeasure": "PC",
          "ExportQuantityUnitMeasure1": "PC",
          "ExportQuantityUnitMeasure2": "PC",
          "LicenseUnitValue": {
            "Currency": cells[16].textContent
          },
          "DdtcUnitMeasure": "PC",
          "packageIndex": index,
          "Origin": {
            "AddressBookIdToProcess": null
          },
          "OriginCountry": cells[14].textContent,
          "ProductCode": cells[1].textContent,
          "HarmonizedCode": cells[16].textContent,
          "Quantity": cells[10].textContent,
          "Description": cells[5].textContent,
          "LicenseExpirationDate": null,
          "NaftaRvcAvgStartDate": null,
          "nAFTARVCAvgEndDate": null,
          "$$hashKey": "object:" + index + "1" + randomNumber
        }];
      //This is wrong an not tested
      //if(line.InternationalDetails!=null && line.InternationalDetails.ExportUnitPrice==null)
      //{
      //    "UnitValue": cells[17].SaleUnitPrice;
      //}
      //else if(line.InternationalDetails!=null && line.InternationalDetails.ExportUnitPrice!=null)
      //{
      //   "UnitValue":cells[15].InternationalInfo.ExportUnitPrice ; 
      //}
    }
    if (!OldCommodity || OldCommodity.length === 0)
    {
      vm.currentShipment.Packages[index].CommodityContents = NewCommodity;
    } else
    {
      vm.currentShipment.Packages[index].CommodityContents = OldCommodity.concat(NewCommodity);
    }
  }

// Source: Hyve Solutions (HYVE)_Hyve_Solutions_CBR_1593.cs
// function PostSelectAddressBook(shipmentRequest, nameaddress) // returns void
this.PostSelectAddressBook = function (shipmentRequest, nameaddress) {
		//alert("Country " + nameaddress.Country);
		
		var clientContext;
		var resp;

        $.ajax({
            type: "GET",
            url: "api/usercontext/GET",
            async: false,
            cache: false,
            success: function (result) {
                debugger;
                clientContext = result;
            },
            error: function (jqXhr, exception) {
                debugger;
            }
        });
     
        $.ajax({
            type: "POST",
            url: "api/ShippingService/UserMethod",
            async: false,
            cache: false,
            dataType: "json",           
            data: { UserContext: clientContext , "Data": nameaddress.Country},    
            success: function (response) {
                debugger;
				resp = JSON.stringify(response);
				resp = JSON.parse(resp);
				if (resp.Data !== "" && resp.Data !== undefined)
				{
					var IOR = JSON.parse(resp.Data);
					shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ImporterOfRecord = IOR;
				}
				else
				{
					alert('No available Importer of Records');
				}
            },
            error: function (xhr) {
                debugger;
                alert(xhr.responseText);
            }
        });
		
	}

// Source: ICON Clinical Research (PRAInternational)_PRA Intl Business Rules_1574.cs
// function checkOriginConsigneeCountry() // returns boolean
function checkOriginConsigneeCountry() {
        var shipFromCountry = getObjectValue(vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.OriginAddress.Country);
        var shipToCountry = getObjectValue(vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Country);

        /* If we have no shipToCountry OR the shipFromCountry is either US or CA, disable the elements, return out. */
        if (!shipToCountry | shipFromCountry == "US" | shipFromCountry == "CA") {
            DisableThirdPartyBillingElements();
            return false;
        }

        if (shipFromCountry != shipToCountry) {
            /* If the shipFromCountry does NOT equal the shipToCountry then ship Third Party. */
            SetThirdPartyBilling(vm.currentShipment);
        }
        else {
            /* Now check to see if both the origin and destination countries are members of the EU. */
            if ((IsMemberOfEu(shipFromCountry)) && (IsMemberOfEu(shipToCountry))) {
                SetThirdPartyBilling(vm.currentShipment);
            }

            //ShipThirdPartyBilling((IsMemberOfEu(shipFromCountry)) && (IsMemberOfEu(shipToCountry)));
        }

        if (shipFromCountry != "US") {
            $('select[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].Weight.Units"]').val('string:KG').change();
            $('select[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].Dimensions.Units"]').val('number:1').change();
        }
    }

// function NewShipment(shipmentRequest) // returns void
this.NewShipment = function (shipmentRequest) {

        this.vm.TemplateInit = this.PageInitialize;
        this.vm.emailNotificationAddress = this.EmailNotificationAddress;
        var originCustomData = shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.OriginAddress.CustomData;
        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference1 = GetKeyValue('Custom1', originCustomData);
        ReturnNameAddressCaption(false);
    };

// function PostSelectAddressBook(shipmentRequest, nameaddress, addressName) // returns void
this.PostSelectAddressBook = function (shipmentRequest, nameaddress, addressName) {
        debugger;
        if (addressName !== '' && addressName !== 'ThirdPartyBillingAddress') {
            var checkExist = setInterval(function () {

                if (($('select[ng-model="nameaddress.Country"]:eq(0)').val().length > 0) && ($('select[ng-model="nameaddress.Country"]:eq(1)').val().length > 0)) {

                    /* Stop the timer. */
                    clearInterval(checkExist);
                    /* The values are stored in the format of 'string:CC'.  We only want the CC. */
                    var shipToCountry = $('select[ng-model="nameaddress.Country"]:eq(0)').val().replace('string:', '');
                    var shipFromCountry = $('select[ng-model="nameaddress.Country"]:eq(1)').val().replace('string:', '');

                    /* If we have no shipToCountry OR the shipFromCountry is either US or CA, disable the elements, return out. */
                    if (!shipToCountry | shipFromCountry == "US" | shipFromCountry == "CA") {
                        DisableThirdPartyBillingElements();
                        return false;
                    }

                    if (shipFromCountry != shipToCountry) {
                        /* If the shipFromCountry does NOT equal the shipToCountry then ship Third Party. */
                        SetThirdPartyBilling(shipmentRequest);
                    }
                    else {
                        /* Now check to see if both the origin and destination countries are members of the EU. */
                        if ((IsMemberOfEu(shipFromCountry)) && (IsMemberOfEu(shipToCountry))) {
                            SetThirdPartyBilling(shipmentRequest);
                        }

                        //ShipThirdPartyBilling((IsMemberOfEu(shipFromCountry)) && (IsMemberOfEu(shipToCountry)));
                    }

                    if (shipFromCountry != "US") {
                        $('select[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].Weight.Units"]').val('string:KG').change();
                        $('select[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].Dimensions.Units"]').val('number:1').change();
                    }
                } /* if ($('div.modal-dialog.modal-md:visible') */

            }, 50); /* var checkExist = setInterval... */
        }
    };

// function SetThirdPartyBilling(shipmentRequest) // returns void
function SetThirdPartyBilling(shipmentRequest) {
        /* This enables the button to edit the Third Party Billing Information. */
        $('input[type=button][ng-disabled="!vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.ThirdPartyBilling"]').prop('disabled', false).attr('disabled', false);

        /* Check the box for Third Party Billing which will bring up the modal.  Fill the modal with values.  Click Save. */
        $('input[type=checkbox][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.ThirdPartyBilling"]').prop('checked', true).attr('checked', true).change();

        shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ThirdPartyBillingAddress = {}
        shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ThirdPartyBillingAddress.Company = 'PRA Global';
        shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ThirdPartyBillingAddress.Address1 = '995 Research Park Blvd';
        shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ThirdPartyBillingAddress.Address2 = 'Suite 300';
        shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ThirdPartyBillingAddress.City = 'Charlottesville';
        shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ThirdPartyBillingAddress.StateProvince = 'VA';
        shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ThirdPartyBillingAddress.PostalCode = '22911';
        shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ThirdPartyBillingAddress.Account = '883F79';
        shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ThirdPartyBillingAddress.Country = 'US'
    }

// function DisableThirdPartyBillingElements() // returns void
function DisableThirdPartyBillingElements() {
        $('input[type=checkbox][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.ThirdPartyBilling"]').prop('checked', false).attr('checked', false);
        $('input[type=button][ng-disabled="!vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.ThirdPartyBilling"]').prop('disabled', true).attr('disabled', true);
    }

// function IsMemberOfEu(v) // returns boolean
function IsMemberOfEu(v) {
        return ($.inArray(v, EuCountries) !== -1) ? true : false;
    }

// Source: Indiana University (INDIANAU)_IU.Ship.Returns_1548.cs
// function NewShipment(shipmentRequest) // returns void
    this.NewShipment = function (shipmentRequest) {

        this.vm.StudyCode = this.SetStudyCode;

        //Default service to NDA.  May change in pre ship to UPS Express if origin is CA.
        var svc = {
            Symbol: "UPSAPI.UPS.NDA"
            , Name: "UPS NEXT DAY AIR (UPS ADAPTER)"
        };
        shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Service = svc;

        shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Shipper = "IURETURNS";
        shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Terms = "SHIPPER";
        shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Description = "Biological Specimens";
        shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.MiscReference18 = "";  //SkipDayCheck

        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference19 = client.userContext.UserId;

        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].Packaging = "CUSTOM";
        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].Description = "Biological Specimens";
        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ReturnDelivery = true;
        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ReturnDeliveryMethod = 0;

        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].DryIceRegulationSet = 2;
        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].DryIcePurpose = 3;
        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ExportReason = "P";

        var data = { UserContext: client.userContext, Data: 'getGroupNames' };
        var response = this.thinClientAPIRequest("UserMethod", data, false);
        var result = JSON.parse($("<div />").html(response["Data"]).text());

        shipmentRequest.IndianUnvStudyData = result;

    };

// function PreShip(shipmentRequest, userParams) // returns void
    this.PreShip = function (shipmentRequest, userParams) {

        var shipDate = new Date(shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Shipdate.Year, shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Shipdate.Month - 1, shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Shipdate.Day);
        var today = new Date();

        if (shipDate.getDay() == 6) {
            throw ({ message: 'Saturday shipping is not allowed. Code[CBR]"', errorCode: '115' });
        }
        
        if (shipDate.getDay() == 7) {
            throw ({ message: 'Sunday shipping is not allowed. Code[CBR]"', errorCode: '115' });
        }
        

        if (shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ShipperReference === undefined || shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ShipperReference === null || shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ShipperReference === '') {
            throw ({ message: 'Study Reference is required.  Please select a valid Study Group in order to continue. [CBR ShipperReference]', errorCode: '115' });
        }
        if (shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ConsigneeReference === undefined || shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ConsigneeReference === null || shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ConsigneeReference === '') {
            throw ({ message: 'Study Reference is required.  Please select a valid Study Group in order to continue. [CBR ConsigneeReference]', errorCode: '115' });
        }

        var diw = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].DryIceWeight;
        var pkgw = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].Weight;

        if (diw.Amount > 0) {
            if (diw.Amount < 10) {
                throw ({ message: 'Shipping Error: Dry Ice Amount must be 10 LBS or more.', errorCode: '115' });
            }
        }

        if (pkgw.Amount < diw.Amount) {
            throw ({ message: 'Shipping Error: Dry Ice Weight MUST be less than the package Weight.', errorCode: '115' });
        }

        var consignee = shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee;
        if (consignee.Country == 'CA') {
            var svc = {
                Symbol: "UPSAPI.UPS.EXPRESS"
                , Name: "UPS Express (UPS ADAPTER)"
            };
            shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Service = svc;

            var uv = { Amount: "150.00", Units: "USD" };
            var uw = { Amount: "1.0", Units: "LB" };
            var cc = {
                ProductCode: "Biological Specimens"
                , Description: "Biological Specimens"
                , Quantity: 1
                , QuantityUnitMeasure: "PC"
                , UnitValue: uv
                , UnitWeight: uw
                , OriginCountry: "CA"
            };
            shipmentRequest.Packages[0].CommodityContents = [cc];
        }
    };

// function PostSelectAddressBook(shipmentRequest, nameaddress) // returns void
    this.PostSelectAddressBook = function (shipmentRequest, nameaddress) {

        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ShipperReference = shipmentRequest.IndianUnvStudyData[shipmentRequest.ConsigneeGroup];
        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ConsigneeReference = this.vm.currentShipment.ConsigneeGroup;
        shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Group = this.vm.currentShipment.ConsigneeGroup;

        var svc;
        if (nameaddress.Country == "CA") {
            svc = {
                Symbol: "UPSAPI.UPS.EXPRESS"
                , Name: "UPS Express (UPS Adapter)"
            };
            shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Service = svc;
        }
        else {
            svc = {
                Symbol: "UPSAPI.UPS.NDA"
                , Name: "UPS NEXT DAY AIR (UPS ADAPTER)"
            };
            shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Service = svc;
        }
    };

// function AddPackage(shipmentRequest, packageIndex) // returns void
     this.AddPackage = function(shipmentRequest, packageIndex)
    {
        
        //Reference
        shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex].ShipperReference = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ShipperReference;
        shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex].ConsigneeReference = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ConsigneeReference;
        shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex].MiscReference1 = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference1;
        shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex].MiscReference2 = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference2;
        shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex].MiscReference3 = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference3;
        shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex].MiscReference4 = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference4;
        shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex].MiscReference5 = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference5;

        //Packaging
       shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex].Packaging = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].Packaging;
       
       

        //LTL
        shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex].WaybillBolNumber = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].WaybillBolNumber;
        shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex].CommodityClass = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].CommodityClass;
        shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex].CarrierInstructions = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].CarrierInstructions;
        shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex].ItemNumber = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ItemNumber;
        shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex].BolLegalStatement = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].BolLegalStatement;

        //COD
        shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex].CodPaymentMethod = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].CodPaymentMethod;

        //Email Notification
        shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex].ShipNotificationEmail = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ShipNotificationEmail;
        shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex].ShipNotificationAddressEmail = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ShipNotificationAddressEmail;
        shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex].DeliveryNotificationEmail = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].DeliveryNotificationEmail;
        shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex].DeliveryNotificationAddressEmail = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].DeliveryNotificationAddressEmail;

        //Signature Required
        shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex].Proof = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].Proof;
        shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex].ProofRequireSignature = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ProofRequireSignature;
        shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex].ProofRequireSignatureAdult = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ProofRequireSignatureAdult;

        //International
        shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex].Description = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].Description;
        shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex].TermsOfSale = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].terms_of_sale;

        //WorldEase
        if (shipmentRequest.Packages[0].WorldEaseFlag == true) {
            shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex].WorldEaseFlag = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].WorldEaseFlag;
            shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex].ImporterOfRecord = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].importer_of_record;
            shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex].ImporterOfRecordAccount = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ImporterOfRecordAccount;
            shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex].WorldEaseCode = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].WorldEaseCode;
        }

        //User_Data_1
        shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex].UserData1 = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].UserData1;

    }

// this.AddPackage(shipmentRequest, packageIndex) // returns void
     this.AddPackage = function(shipmentRequest, packageIndex) {
       
        shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.UserData1 = null;
		var shipService = "";
		if(shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Service!==undefined){
			shipService = shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Service.Symbol;
		}
		var LTLFlag = false;
		if (shipService.includes("_LTL.") || shipService.includes("_UPSFREIGHT")){
			LTLFlag = true;
		}
		if(LTLFlag)
		{
		    if((shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex].MiscReference20 != undefined && shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex].MiscReference20 != null && shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex].MiscReference20 != "")
		        &&(shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex].ParentContainerCode == null || shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex].ParentContainerCode == "") ){
                    shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex].ParentContainerCode ="P" + shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex].MiscReference20 + "-" + packageIndex;
		    }
		var dims = "0x0x0";
		
		var lastPackage = shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex - 1];

		var length =0;
        var width = 0;
        var height =0;
	    if(lastPackage.Dimensions!=undefined){
			if(lastPackage.Dimensions.Length!= undefined && lastPackage.Dimensions.Width!=undefined && lastPackage.Dimensions.Height!=undefined){
				length =lastPackage.Dimensions.Length;
				width = lastPackage.Dimensions.Width;
				height = lastPackage.Dimensions.Height;
			} 	
		}

        const dimArr=[length,width,height];
        
        //To sort dimensions in descending order.
        dimArr.sort(function(a, b){return b-a});
		dims = dimArr[0]+"x"+dimArr[1]+"x"+dimArr[2];
		if(dims!="0x0x0"){
			const   dimtblx ="34,48,52,12,14,18,18,28,37".split(",");  
            const   dimtbly ="32,40,36,52,44,32,52,44,37".split(","); 
			for (let i = 0; i < dimtblx.length; i++){
				var   x = dimtblx[i];
                var   y = dimtbly[i];
				if (i < 3)
                {
                    
                    if (dimArr[0] == x && dimArr[1] == y )
                        break;
                    if (dimArr[0] == x && dimArr[1] == y )
                    {                           
                        dims= x + "x" + y + "x" + dimArr[1];                    
                        break;
                    }
                    if (dimArr[1] == x && dimArr[2] == y )
                    {
                    dims = x + "x" + y + "x" + dimArr[0];           
                    break;
                    }
                }
				else{                  
                     
                    if (dimArr[0] == y && dimArr[1] == x )
                    {
                        dims = x + "x" + y + "x" + dimArr[2];                    
                        break;
                    }
                    if (dimArr[0] == y && dimArr[2] == x )
                    {
                       dims = x + "x" + y + "x" + dimArr[1];
                    
                       break;
                    }
                    if (dimArr[1] == y && dimArr[2] == x )
                    {
                    dims = x + "x" + y + "x" + dimArr[0];                
                    break;
                    }
                }
			}
			if(lastPackage.BolComment == null)
			   lastPackage.BolComment = ""; 
			
			shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex-1].BolComment = lastPackage.BolComment+" "+dims;
			
		}
		//debugger;
		shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex - 1].Description = "DIESEL ENGINE PARTS NMFC # 133300, SUB 4, Class 60 L"+packageIndex; // + " L" + packageIndex-1;
		
		if(shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex - 1].WaybillBolNumber == null || shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex - 1].WaybillBolNumber == "" ){
			shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex - 1].WaybillBolNumber = shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex-1].MiscReference20;
		}
		}
	
	//setRef1Focus script start
	$("#referenceTab").children()[0].click();
	$('div[property = "MiscReference1"]').children().ready(function () {
	     $('div[property = "MiscReference1"]').children().focus();
	});
	//setRef1Focus script end
	 
}

// PageLoaded(location) // returns void
this.PageLoaded = function(location) {  
		if (location == "/shipping")
        {
			var loaded = setInterval(function() {
            const $shipping = $('form[name="shippingForm"]');

            if ($shipping.length > 0) {
                clearInterval(loaded);

                $('input[ng-model="vm.loadValue"]').attr('placeholder','Enter the Delivery Num');
				var divshipper = $('div[property="Shipper"]');
            if (divshipper.length > 0) {
				var div1 = $('div[class="col-sm-8 no-left-right-padding"]');
				let selectship = $('select[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Shipper"]');
                let select = selectship.eq(0);
		        let options = select.find('option');//.eq(0);
                for(var ind=0;ind < options.length; ind++){
					let option = options.eq(ind);
					let opt = option.eq(0).val(); 
				//	debugger;	
					if (opt.includes("string:KARTDRATE")){
					option.hide();				
			}
				}
			}
				
            }
			}, 50);
		}
	}

// this.PostLoad(loadValue, shipmentRequest) // returns void
  this.PostLoad = function(loadValue, shipmentRequest)
  {
    //debugger;
    loadValue = loadValue.replace('!!', '');

    if (typeof shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.MiscReference5 !== 'undefined' && shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.MiscReference5 !== null && shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.MiscReference5.length > 2)
    {
      alertMessage('danger', shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.MiscReference5);
    }

    this.vm.getWeight();
    //$("#overrideRateShopping_Y").prop("checked", true);

    // Warn user if expedited service selected and PO box is checked
    const expServices = "UPS.NDA,UPS.2AM,UPS.2DA,UPS.EXP,USPS.PRIORITY,USPS.EXPR".split(',');

    let hasExpedited = expServices.some(service => shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Service.Symbol.includes(service));
    if (hasExpedited && shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.PoBox)
    {
      alertMessage('warning', "Order " + loadValue + " has an Expedited service selected but a PO box was used. Contact Customer Service for a new address.")
    }

    // if Int'l shipment, show Assign Commodities button, hide Add Package button group, and init AssignGoods
    //sna6dxb - 09-23-2022
    //don't need this any longer, the button is hidden by default in the template
    //$('#btnAssignCommodities').hide();
    if (shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Country !== "US")
    {
      $('#btnAssignCommodities').show();
      $('button[title="Add Package"]').parent().hide();
      const Goods = new AssignGoods(this.vm);
    }
    else {
        // ensure Assign Commodities button is hidden in case they load an Int'l order by mistake, then load domestic
        $('#btnAssignCommodities').hide();
        $('button[title="Add Package"]').parent().show();
    }
  }

// function AssignGoods(ViewModel) // returns constructor instance behavior for commodity assignment
class AssignGoods
{
  constructor(ViewModel)
  {
    this.viewModel = ViewModel;

    if ($('#divAssignCommodities:visible').length > 0) return;

    this.InitiateDelegates();
  }

  viewModel;
  goods;
  packages;

  //working holds a copy of the commodity contents array
  working;

  //this event fires when they click the button to 'Assign Commodities'
  //set references to the objects, build the list items, add a .pkg key to the commodity contents object
  ShowAssignGoodsPane()
  {
    let that = this;
    //get rid of any previous entries
    $('#listItemContainer li:gt(0)').remove();

    //change the column width to make the descriptions longer
    //change this back when the user clicks the 'Apply' button
    $('div.ui-tab-container').toggleClass('col-md-8 col-md-6').siblings('div').toggleClass('col-md-4 col-md-6')

    //set a reference to the packages object as well as the commodities objects
    this.packages = this.viewModel.currentShipment.Packages;

    //get all the commodities in the shipment from all packages
    this.goods = $(this.packages).map(function(x, y)
    {
      return y.CommodityContents;
    });

    //loop the goods array and update the markup within the slideout panel
    $(this.goods).each(function(a, b)
    {
      //debugger;
      let k = 'e' + (Math.random() + 1).toString(36).substring(2);
      b.GoodsKey = k;

      if (b.packageIndex === undefined) {
        // initial index is undefined after loading order, default to fix NaN bug later
        b.packageIndex = 0;
      }
      //copy the source element
      let item = $('#liClone').clone(true).attr({ 'hash-key': b.$$hashKey, 'goods-key': b.GoodsKey, 'pkg-index': b.packageIndex }).removeAttr('id');

      //the customer is sending amounts that have sometimes 10 digits after the decimal point which is throwing exceptions when trying
      //to parseFloat so this is the simplest way to get around that.
      let cost = Math.round(b.UnitValue.Amount * 100) / 100;

      $(item).find('.goods-description').text(b.Description);
      $(item).find('.goods-quantity').html('(<strong>' + b.Quantity + '</strong>');
      $(item).find('.goods-unit-of-measure').text(b.QuantityUnitMeasure + ', ');
      $(item).find('.goods-declared-value').html('<strong>$' + cost + '</strong> ' + b.UnitValue.Currency + ')');
      $(item).find('.pkg-index-text').text(+(b.packageIndex) + 1);
      $(item).find('.header-logo').show();

      //append it to our list
      $('#divAssignCommodities ul.list-group').append(item);

      //show it gracefully
      $(item).show();

    });

    //create a working array object so we can manipulate the data non-destructively
    this.working = $.makeArray(JSON.parse(JSON.stringify(this.goods)));

    $('#divAssignCommodities').show().animate({ left: 0 }, 400);
    $('.assign-to-pkg:visible').first().focus();
  }

  HideAssignGoodsPane()
  {
    // restore the shipping panel sizes first, doing this last sometimes caused a scope issue and left pane wasn't getting resized
    $('div.ui-tab-container').toggleClass('col-md-8 col-md-6').siblings('div').toggleClass('col-md-4 col-md-6');
    let u = $('#divAssignCommodities').outerWidth() + 100;
    //$('#divAssignCommodities').find('[data-toggle="tooltip"]').tooltip('destroy');
    $('#divAssignCommodities').animate({ left: -u }, 400, function() { $(this).hide(); });
  }

  UpdateGoodsObject(pkgCount, listItem)
  {
    const itemkey = $(listItem).attr('hash-key');
    const goodkey = $(listItem).attr('goods-key');
    const findex = +$(listItem).attr('pkg-index');

    let val = $(listItem).find('.goods-declared-value');
    let cost = $(val).find('strong').text().replace('$', '');

    cost = (cost / pkgCount).toFixed(2);

    //get the object that matches the hash-key from the working array
    //this will be the template to use when creating new packages after a split operation
    //working on a copy of the vm commodity object so we can abandon changes if needed
    let src = $.grep(this.working, function(value, i) { return value.$$hashKey == itemkey; })[0];

    //update the declared value for the first package
    src.UnitValue.Amount = cost;

    for (let y = 1; y < pkgCount; y++)
    {
      let ccobj = this.GetNewCommodityObject(src);
      ccobj.packageIndex = findex + y;

      this.working.push(ccobj);

      this.UpdateScreenMarkup(ccobj, listItem);
    }
  }

  //v = the numbers to split the shipment over, li is the parent list item
  UpdateScreenMarkup(ccobj, li)
  {
    //this is all setting up the first list item to be cloned in the next function
    //hide the split button
    $(li).find('.btn-show-split-form').fadeOut();

    //show the input for number of items in this pkg
    $(li).find('.num-of-items-in-pkg').fadeIn();

    //display the header
    $(li).find('.header-logo').css('display', 'block');

    $(li).find('.goods-declared-value').html('<strong>$' + ccobj.UnitValue.Amount + '</strong> ' + 'USD' + ')');

    this.CreateListViewItem(ccobj.packageIndex, li)

    let input = $('#listItemContainer').find('.num-of-items-in-pkg');
    $(input).tooltip({ container: 'body' });

    //when done creating elements, focus on the first visible non-disabled input box
    $('#listItemContainer').find($('.num-of-items-in-pkg:visible:not(:disabled)').first().focus());

    //if there was a single item (i.e a KIT), split evenly and close
    let qty = +$(li).find('.goods-quantity strong').text();
    if (qty === 1)
    {
      let these = $('#listItemContainer').find('li[goods-key=' + $(li).attr('goods-key') + ']');
      $(these).attr('pkg-status', 'packed');
      $(these).find('.num-of-items-in-pkg').val(1).attr('disabled', 'disabled');
      $(these).find('.goods-quantity > strong').text(1);
      $(these).find('.split-pkgs-modal').hide().find('input').val([]);
      //$('#btnApplyCommodityAssignments').trigger('click');
    }
  }

  CreateListViewItem(idx, li)
  {
    //the hash-key attr is the object id for the commodity in relation to the package
    //if we keep it, all packages will have the same hash-key (pkg 0)
    let item = $(li).clone(true).removeAttr('hash-key').removeAttr('id');
    $(item).attr('pkg-index', idx);

    $(item).find('.pkg-index-text').text(idx + 1);
    $(item).find('.goods-quantity').html('(<strong>0</strong>');

    let lastInList = $('#listItemContainer').find('li[goods-key="' + $(li).attr('goods-key') + '"]').last();

    //i have no idea why the opacity changes when i use .show().  first time i've ever seen that.
    //anyway, set it implicitly here so the element shows
    $(item).appendTo('#listItemContainer').insertAfter(lastInList).find('.num-of-items-in-pkg').css('opacity', '1').show();
  }

  UpdatePkgCountsInWorkingObject(li)
  {
    let goodkey = $(li).attr('goods-key');
    let pkgindex = $(li).attr('pkg-index');
    let itemcount = $(li).find('.num-of-items-in-pkg').val();

    //find the object in this.working that has the matching pkg-index and goods-key, then update it
    let w = $.grep(this.working, function(pkg, i) { return pkg.GoodsKey == goodkey && pkg.packageIndex == pkgindex  })[0];

    w.Quantity = itemcount;
  }

  //event handler for user pressing <ENTER> on the input box for number of items to split across
  UpdateListItemPackageQuantities(li)
  {
    this.UpdatePkgCountsInWorkingObject(li);

    let numOfItems = $(li).find('.num-of-items-in-pkg');
    let remItems = $(li).find('.goods-quantity > strong');

    if (!$(numOfItems).val()) { return; }

    let x = (+$(remItems).text() - $(numOfItems).val());

    //sanity check to make sure we didn't pack more items that we had
    if (x < 0)
    {
      $(remItems).addClass('bad-math');
      return;
    }

    $(remItems).removeClass('bad-math');
    $(numOfItems).attr('disabled', 'disabled');
    $(li).attr('pkg-status', 'packed');

    //move to the next list item and update then focus
    $(li).next().find('.goods-quantity > strong').text(x)

    //on the second-to-last list item, use the input value to auto-set the last item
    //to get the number of rows that have already been assigned, count the list items with the goods-key
    //that have disabled input boxes
    let rowsForThisGood = $('#listItemContainer').find('li[goods-key="' + $(li).attr('goods-key') + '"]');
    let rowsDone = $(rowsForThisGood).find('input:disabled:visible').length;

    if (rowsForThisGood.length == (rowsDone + 1))
    {
      let lastLi = $('#listItemContainer').find('li[goods-key="' + $(li).attr('goods-key') + '"]').last();

      $(lastLi).attr('pkg-status', 'packed');

      let lastVal = $(li).next().find('.goods-quantity > strong').text();
      $(lastLi).find('.num-of-items-in-pkg').val(lastVal).attr('disabled', 'disabled');

      $('#listItemContainer').find('.assign-to-pkg:visible').first().focus();

      this.UpdatePkgCountsInWorkingObject(lastLi);
    }
  }

  //event handler for the 'Apply' button
  ApplyCommodityAssignments()
  {
    let that = this;

    //every list item will have a pkg-index attr, get that highest value to determine how many pkgs we need
    //don't use pkg-status.length because that will include multiple commodities and the end result will be wrong
    let packed = $('#listItemContainer').find('li[pkg-status=packed]');

    //first get all the pkg-index attributes, then get the highest number and add one
    let pkgs = $(packed).map(function(x, value) { return +$(this).attr('pkg-index') }).toArray();
    let pkgCount = Math.max(...pkgs) + 1;

    while (this.packages.length < pkgCount)
    {
      //the vm.addPackage isn't firing, just click the button
      $('button[ng-click="vm.addPackage();"]').trigger('click').promise().done(function(e) { });
    }

    //loop the pkg count, get the commodities for that pkg, write the objects to the vm CommodityContents object
    for (let p = 0; p < pkgCount; p++)
    {
      let w = $.grep(this.working, function(item, i) { return item.packageIndex == p });
      this.packages[p].CommodityContents = w;
    }

    //click the General tab
    $('li[heading=General]:visible a').first().click();
    this.HideAssignGoodsPane();

    //after we are done, move back to the first package in the shipment
    while ($('#spanCurrentPackageIndex').text() !== '1')
    {
      $('button[ng-click="vm.previousPackage();"]').first().click();
    }

  }

  GetClassViewModel()
  {
    //the goods data is going to come from vm.currentShipment.Packages[pkgIndex].CommodityContents as an array
    return this.viewModel
  }

  //passing in the commodity object for the first package and copying the non-null values to a new object, then returning
  GetNewCommodityObject(obj)
  {
    let c = {};

    Object.keys(obj).forEach(key =>
    {
      if (key != '$$hashKey' && key != 'packageIndex')
      {
        let value = obj[key];
        if (value) c[key] = value;
      }
    });

    return c;
  }

  //when hiding this modal because the user cancelled out, show the 'Scan Barcode' input and 'Split' button
  CancelSplitOfPackages(li)
  {
    //hide the split modal and clear the input value
    $('.escape-target').hide();
    $(li).find('.split-pkgs-modal').hide().find('input[type=number]').val([]).focus();
    $(li).find('.btn-show-split-form, .assign-to-pkg').fadeIn();
  }

  //delegate the event handlers for the div
  InitiateDelegates()
  {
    let that = this

    $('body').delegate('#btnApplyCommodityAssignments', 'click', function(e)
    {
      that.ApplyCommodityAssignments();
    });

    $('body').delegate('.btn-show-split-form', 'click', function(e)
    {
      let div = $(this).closest('div').find('.split-pkgs-modal').first();
      $(div).tooltip({ container: 'body' });

      $(div).css('display', 'flex').fadeIn();
      $('.split-pkgs-modal:visible').find('input').first().focus();

      //hide the split button now...and the input
      $(this).hide();
      $(this).closest('div').find('.assign-to-pkg').hide();
    });

    $('body').delegate('input.btn-go-split-pkgs', 'click', function(e)
    {
      console.log('btn-go-split-pkgs click event handler');

      let li = $(this).closest('li').first();
      let div = $(this).closest('div').first();

      $(li).find('.pkg-index-text').first().text('1');

      //val - 1 as the first entry will be the first package
      let v = $(div).find('input[type=number]').first().val();

      that.UpdateGoodsObject(v, li);

      $('.split-pkgs-modal').hide();
    });

    $('body').delegate('#btnCancelAssignGoods', 'click', function(e)
    {
      that.HideAssignGoodsPane();
    });

    //if the user escapes out of the split modal, hide the modal and show the previous forms
    $('body').delegate('.split-pkgs-modal', 'keydown', function(e)
    {
      var keycode = (e.keyCode ? e.keyCode : e.which);
      if (keycode === 27)
      {
        //need to show the previous input and button now
        let li = $(this).closest('li');

        that.CancelSplitOfPackages(li);
      }
    });

    //if the user presses enter or tab in the num-of-items number input, move to the next one
    //these are the number inputs after the items have been split across packages
    $('body').delegate('.num-of-items-in-pkg', 'keydown focusout', function(e)
    {
      console.log('.num-of-items-in-pkg keydown focusout event handler');

      $('[data-toggle="tooltip"]').tooltip('hide');

      var keycode = (e.keyCode ? e.keyCode : e.which);
      if (keycode === 13 || keycode === 9)
      {
        //disable the input, update the commodity object, focus on the next box input
        //$(this).closest('div').find('.assign-to-pkg').focus();
        that.UpdateListItemPackageQuantities($(this).closest('li'));
      }
    });

    //user hits enter in the input box, click the button for them
    $('body').delegate('.num-of-pkgs-to-use', 'keyup keydown', function(e)
    {
      console.log('.num-of-pkgs-to-use keyup keydown event handler');
      var keycode = (e.keyCode ? e.keyCode : e.which);
      let btn = $(this).closest('div:visible').find('input.btn-go-split-pkgs');

      $(btn).attr('disabled', $(this).val() < 2);

      if (keycode == 13) //enter
      {
        //let btn = $(this).closest('div:visible').find('input.btn-go-split-pkgs');
        $(btn).trigger('click');
      }
    });

    //this was formerly .scan-input.  as of 9/24/2022, removing the split functionality completely
    //with this change, only need to get the numerical value out of the input
    $('body').delegate('.assign-to-pkg', 'keydown focusout', function(e)
    {
      console.log('.assign-to-pkg keydown focusout event handler');
      var keycode = (e.keyCode ? e.keyCode : e.which);
      debugger;
      if (keycode == 13 || keycode == 9 || e.type == "focusout") //enter
      {
        e.preventDefault();
        //pull only the number from whatever was passed.  make sure it is greater than 0 since we can't assign a good a pkg zero.
        const val = $(this).val().replace(/[^1-9]/g, '');

        let li = $(this).closest('li');
        
        if (val)
        {
          //console.log('assigning this to ', val);
          //assign the integer to the line item header (not shown, but may be shown in the future)
          //this one is easy, just assign the pkg-index attr to whatever they scanned.  when the apply button is clicked it will assign the commodities
          //let li = $(this).closest('li');
          $(li).find('.pkg-index-text').first().text(val);
          $(li).find('button').attr('disabled', 'disabled');
          $(li).attr('pkg-index', val - 1);
          $(li).attr('pkg-status', 'packed');

          //find the matching item in the this.working array and update the package index
          let item = $.grep(that.working, function(good, i) { return good.$$hashKey == $(li).attr('hash-key') })[0];
          item.packageIndex = val - 1;
          //return;
        }
        // set focus to next li input box
        if (e.type !== "focusout") {
          $(li).next().find('.assign-to-pkg').focus().change();
        }
      }
    });

    $('#btnAssignCommodities').on('click', function(e)
    {
      if ($('#divAssignCommodities').is(':visible')) return;
      that.ShowAssignGoodsPane();
    });
  }

function SetAltairDCShipper(Shipper)
    	{
    	     var UserContextmethod,GetClientProfilemethod,authorizationToken,getCompanyId,methodParams,getCustomData,options;
                 UserContextmethod = 'api/usercontext/GET';
                 GetClientProfilemethod='api/ShippingService/GetClientProfile';
                 authorizationToken = clientService.authorizationToken();
                 getCompanyId = $.get({url: clientService.config.ApiUrl + '/' + UserContextmethod, headers: authorizationToken, async: false}).responseJSON;
                 userContextDetails=getCompanyId;
                 methodParams = {"CompanyId":getCompanyId.CompanyId};
                 getCustomData =  $.post({url: clientService.config.ApiUrl + '/' + GetClientProfilemethod, data: methodParams, async: false, headers: authorizationToken }).responseJSON;
                 AllShipperList=getCustomData.Profile.Shippers;
                 Altair_Address = getCustomData.Profile.Shippers[0].CustomData[0].Value;
                
                var loadedShipperValue = $('select[ng-change="vm.shipperChange()"]').text();
    
                        if(AltairDCAddress.toUpperCase() != Shipper.toUpperCase())
                	    {
                	         $("select#IdAltairDCAddress option[value='ShipperAddress']").prop('selected',true);
                             $("select#IdAltairDCAddress option[value='AltairDCAddress']").prop('selected',false);
                	      for (var k = 0; k < getCustomData.Profile.Shippers.length; k++)
                                {

                                       $('input[ng-model="nameaddress.Address1"]:eq(0)').val(getCustomData.Profile.Shippers[k].Address1);

// Source: MarkenLLP (MLLP)_Inbound Returns CBR_CA_TO_US_2497.cs
// this.PreShip(shipmentRequest, userParams) // returns void
this.PreShip = function (shipmentRequest, userParams) {

        debugger;

        var i = 0, len = shipmentRequest.Packages.length;
        for (; i < len; i++) {
            var currentPackage = shipmentRequest.Packages[i];
            debugger;
            if (currentPackage == null
                || currentPackage.CommodityContents == null
                || currentPackage.CommodityContents.length == 0) {
                var errorMsg = 'To obtain a UPS label to ship you must go to the Goods Tab above and process a paperless invoice for this shipment. Instructions on how to do this are located in your Starterpack.'
                console.log(errorMsg);
                $('#uploadErrorModalLabel').html(errorMsg);
                $('#uploadErrorModal').modal('show');
                throw Error(errorMsg);
            }
        }

        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference16 = sessionStorage.getItem('uploadDocumentDataGoods');
        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference17 = sessionStorage.getItem('uploadDocumentDataModal');
    }

// function setCommodityDelegate() // returns void
function setCommodityDelegate() {
        checkElmLoaded('[name="commoditiesModalForm"]').then((elm) => {
            debugger;
            const parentElm = elm;
            if (elm) {
                debugger;
                var footer = elm.querySelector('.modal-footer');
                if (footer) {
                    var saveButton = footer.querySelector('[value="Save"]');
                    if (saveButton) {
                        saveButton.addEventListener('click', function (e) {
                            debugger;
                            var form = e.target.parentElement.parentElement;
                            var quantityUOM = form.querySelector('[ng-model="vm.commodityContent.QuantityUnitMeasure"]');
                            if (quantityUOM && quantityUOM.options) {
                                console.log('clicked');
                                var optionArray = Array.from(quantityUOM.options);

                                if (optionArray && optionArray.length > 0)
                                    var eachOption = optionArray.filter((x) => x.value == 'string:EA');
                                console.log('eachOption');
                                console.log(eachOption);
                                if (eachOption && eachOption.length == 1) {
                                    var indexOfEAOption = optionArray.indexOf(eachOption[0]);
                                    if (indexOfEAOption > 0) {
                                        quantityUOM.selectedIndex = indexOfEAOption;
                                        console.log('index');
                                        console.log(indexOfEAOption);
                                        quantityUOM.dispatchEvent(new window.Event('change', { bubbles: true }));
                                        console.log('dispatched');
                                    }
                                }

                                debugger;
                                setTimeout(setCommodityDelegate, 500);
                            }

                            //that.vm.commodityContent.QuantityUnitMeasure = 'EA';
                        })
                    }
                }
            }
        });
    }

// this.NewShipment(shipmentRequest) // returns void
this.NewShipment = function (shipmentRequest) {


        clearUploadMessages();
        this.clearSessionState();
        setUploadDelegates(shipmentRequest);
        this.currentShipment = shipmentRequest;


        if (location == '/shipping') {
            StudyReferenceCodeModal.InitElements(false);
            $('#LoadStudyReferenceCodeData').click();
            Tools.HideLoader();
        }

        client?.$divReference3?.hide();

        shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee = this.vm.profile.UserInformation.Address;

        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ShipperReference = this.vm.profile.UserInformation.Address.CustomData[0].Value; //Study Reference code

        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference1 = this.vm.profile.UserInformation.Address.CustomData[1].Value;  //Protocol Number

        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference2 = this.vm.profile.UserInformation.Address.CustomData[2].Value;  //Site Number

        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference4 = true;

        //Storing StudyReference codes on the Miscreference17
        var studyReferenceCode = null;
        var studyReferenceCodeList = [];
        for (var i = 0; i < this.vm.profile.FieldOptions.MiscReference17.FieldOptionValidations.length; i++) {
            debugger;
            studyReferenceCode = this.vm.profile.FieldOptions.MiscReference17.FieldOptionValidations[i].Value.split(',').map(x => x.trim());
            studyReferenceCodeList.push(studyReferenceCode);
        }
        var shipper = null;
        $(document).ready(function () {

            $("#OK").on("click", function () {
                debugger;
                var selectedValue = $('#selectShipper').val().trim();
                var shipperReferenceVal = $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].ShipperReference"]').val();
                var arrayOrders = Tools.GetUniqueArrayFromString(shipperReferenceVal);
                if (arrayOrders.includes(selectedValue)) {
                    var selectedIndex = arrayOrders.indexOf(selectedValue);
                    var selectedStudy = arrayOrders[selectedIndex];
                    //Populating the entered Study Reference code in the Shipper reference field.
                    $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].ShipperReference"]').val(selectedStudy);
                    shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ShipperReference = $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].ShipperReference"]').val();

                    var miscReference1Val = $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference1"]').val();
                    var arrayOrders1 = Tools.GetUniqueArrayFromString(miscReference1Val);
                    var selectedProtocol = arrayOrders1[selectedIndex];
                    //Populating the corresponding Protocol number in the Misc reference 1 field.
                    $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference1"]').val(selectedProtocol);
                    shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference1 = $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference1"]').val();

                    debugger;
                    var miscReference2Val = $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference2"]').val();
                    var arrayOrders2 = Tools.GetUniqueArrayFromString(miscReference2Val);
                    var selectedSite = arrayOrders2[selectedIndex];
                    //Populating the corresponding Site number in the Misc reference 2 field.
                    $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference2"]').val(selectedSite);
                    shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference2 = $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference2"]').val();

                    //Assigning Shipper based on StudyReferenceCode available on validation list
                    for (var j = 0; j < studyReferenceCodeList.length; j++) {
                        var firstCode = studyReferenceCodeList[j];
                        if (firstCode.length >= 2 && firstCode[0] == selectedValue) {
                            shipper = "string:" + firstCode[1];
                            $('select[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Shipper"]').val(shipper);
                            shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Shipper = $('select[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Shipper"] option:selected').val().split(":")[1];


                        }
                    }

                }
                else {
                    alert("Please contact Marken to have this study added to your profile.");
                    throw new Error("Please contact Marken to have this study added to your profile.");
                }

                //Calling the SBR Usermethod to get the Shipper Friendly name.    
                //GetUserShipper(selectedStudy, shipmentRequest);

                StudyReferenceCodeModal.CloseDialogWithoutSaving();

            });

        });

        //Setting Proactive recovery
        $(document).ready(function () {
            debugger;
            $('body').delegate('[property="ProactiveRecovery"]', 'change', function (e) {
                debugger;
                if (e.target.checked == true) {
                    shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ProactiveRecovery = true;
                    $('select option[value="number:1"]').prop("selected", true);
                    shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ProactiveRecoveryType = 1;
                    var total = 0;
                    for (var i = 0; i < shipmentRequest.Packages[0].SelectedProactiveRecoveryInstructions.length; i++) {
                        total += shipmentRequest.Packages[0].SelectedProactiveRecoveryInstructions[i]
                    }
                    var inst = [];
                    inst.push(total);
                    debugger;
                    shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ProactiveRecoveryInstructions = inst[0].toString();

                }
                else {
                    $('select option[selected="selected"]').prop("selected", true);
                }
            });


        });

    }

// this.PreShip(shipmentRequest, userParams) // returns void
    this.PreShip = function (shipmentRequest, userParams) {
        debugger;

        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference16 = sessionStorage.getItem('uploadDocumentDataGoods');
        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference17 = sessionStorage.getItem('uploadDocumentDataModal');

        //If the user profile is EU to UK, then Pickup LatestTimeReady can be calculated.
        if (shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference8 == "2") {

            //Storing the Number of Maximum labels in Misc Referene14.
            shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference14 = $('#Maxlabel').val();

            //Validating the maximum label count.
            if (shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference14 == null || shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference14 == "" || shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference14 == undefined || shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference14 % 1 !== 0) {
                alert("Maximum label count is invalid");
                throw new Error("Maximum label count is invalid");
            }
            else if (!(shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference14 >= 1 && shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference14 <= 25)) {
                throw new Error("Number of labels needs to be a valid number between 1 and 25.");
            }
            
        }

    }

                    shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ProactiveRecoveryType = 1;

                    }
                    var inst = [];

                    debugger;
                    shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ProactiveRecoveryInstructions = inst[0].toString();

                }
                else {
                    $('select option[selected="selected"]').prop("selected", true);
                }
            });


        });

        //Adding commodities automatically.
        this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].CommodityContents = [];
