    };

// GetKeyValue(key, arr) // returns string
function GetKeyValue(key, arr) {
      for (var index in arr) {
          if (arr[index].Key.toLowerCase() === key.toLowerCase()) return arr[index].Value;
      }
      return '';
  }

// Source: PackVerify Demos (PACKVERIFY)_PV Sliding Panel CBR_1858.cs
// GetCommodityContentObject(data) // returns commodity content object
GetCommodityContentObject(data)
    {
      let cc = {};
      cc.Quantity = data.quantity;
      cc.ProductCode = data.skuId;
      cc.QuantityUnitMeasure = 'EA';
      cc.UnitValue = { Currency: 'USD', Amount: +data.unitPrice };
      cc.UnitWeight = { Units: 'LB', Amount: +data.weightLbs };
      cc.UniqueId = data.UniqueId;
      cc.PkgIndex = data.PkgIndex || 1;
      cc.PVTotalWeight = (+data.quantity * +data.weightLbs);
      cc.PVTotalValue = (+data.quantity * +data.unitPrice);

      return cc;
    }

// MoveGoodToBox(li, destBox) // returns boolean|undefined
MoveGoodToBox(li, destBox)
    {
      let vm = this.ClassViewModel;
      let that = this;
      let data = $(li).data();
      let destCC = this.packages[destBox - 1].CommodityContents || [];

      //find the box the item currently resides in
      //split this statement up over a few calls to make it easier to read
      let allGoods = this.packages.map(m => m.CommodityContents).flat();
      let item = allGoods.find(cc => cc.UniqueId == data.UniqueId);

      if (+item.PkgIndex == +destBox) { console.log('Item already exists in box.'); return false; }

      //remove the item from its current box
      this.packages[item.PkgIndex - 1].CommodityContents = this.packages[item.PkgIndex - 1].CommodityContents.filter(p => p.UniqueId != data.UniqueId);

      //add it to the new box
      item.PkgIndex = destBox;
      destCC.push(item);
      $(li).find('.pkg-index-text').fadeOut().promise().done(function(e) { $(this).text(destBox).fadeIn(); });

      //console.log(vm.currentShipment.Packages);
      $('li[heading="Goods"]:visible:first > a').trigger('click');
      $('#goods .btn-group').find('.btn:gt(0)').not('.active').first().trigger('click');

      //update the weights and values
      //this data will have changed by now so get a new reference to the object
      allGoods = this.packages.map(m => m.CommodityContents).flat();
      //the items array will have the CommodityContents object for every package in the shipment

      //sort by package index
      //update the weight and declared values for all the packages in the shipment
      allGoods = allGoods.sort((a, b) => { return a.PkgIndex - b.PkgIndex });
      $(allGoods).each(function(a, b)
      {
        let pkg = that.packages[b.PkgIndex - 1];

        if ((a == 0) || (b.PkgIndex != allGoods[a - 1].PkgIndex))
        {
          pkg.Weight.Amount = 0;
          pkg.DeclaredValueAmount.Amount = 0;
        }

        pkg.Weight.Amount += +b.PVTotalWeight;
        pkg.DeclaredValueAmount.Amount += +b.PVTotalValue;
      });
    }

// Source: PRA Developer (PRADeveloper)_PRA Intl Business Rules_1523.cs
// this.PageLoaded(location) // returns void
this.PageLoaded = function (location) {
       
        /* Only apply these functions to the shipping page. */
        if (window.location.hash == "#!/shipping") {
            $('body').delegate('*', 'focus', function (e) {
                $('div.alert-danger:visible').hide();
            })

            var checkExist = setInterval(function () {

                if ((window.jQuery !== undefined) && ($('select[name=Country]').length > 0)) {
                    /* Stop the timer. */
                    clearInterval(checkExist);

                    /* Register the event that fires when a user clicks the 'Reset' button on the main page. */
                    $('body').delegate('button[ng-click="vm.newShipment()"]:eq(0)', 'click', function (e) {
                        DisableThirdPartyBillingElements();
                    });

                    /* Disable the ThirdPartyBilling edit button. */
                    $('input[type=button][ng-disabled="!vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.ThirdPartyBilling"]').prop('disabled', true).attr('disabled', true);

                    /* For select boxes which are enabled, remove the default country of United States. */
                    $('select[name=Country][disabled!=disabled]').prop('selectedIndex', 0);

                    /* Trying to fix a bug where the Ship From country select element is disabled and set to the wrong country. */
                    /* Enable the element. */
                    $('select[ng-model="nameaddress.Country"]:eq(1)').prop('disabled', false);

                    /* Hide the End Of Day dropdown menu. */
                    $('ul.nav.navbar-nav li.dropdown:eq(1) > a.dropdown-toggle').hide();

                    /* Change captions for tabs when processing return shipments. */
                    /* Register the event on change. */
                    $('body').delegate('select[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].ReturnDeliveryMethod"]', 'change', function (e) {
                        var isReturn = $(this).val().length > 0;
                        ReturnNameAddressCaption(isReturn);
                        vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].ReturnDelivery = isReturn;
                    });

                    $('body').delegate('name-address[address-property-name="Consignee"] select[name="Country"]', 'change', checkOriginConsigneeCountry);
                    $('body').delegate('name-address[address-property-name="OriginAddress"] select[name="Country"]', 'change', checkOriginConsigneeCountry);
                } /* if ((window.jQuery... */

            }, 50); /* var checkExist = setInterval... */

        } /* if (window.location.hash... */
    };

// checkOriginConsigneeCountry() // returns boolean
function checkOriginConsigneeCountry() {
        var shipFromCountry = getObjectValue(vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.OriginAddress.Country);
        var shipToCountry = getObjectValue(vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Country);

        /* If we have no shipToCountry OR the shipFromCountry is either US or CA, disable the elements, return out. */
        if (!shipToCountry | shipFromCountry == "US" | shipFromCountry == "CA") {
            DisableThirdPartyBillingElements();
            return false;
        }

        if (shipFromCountry != shipToCountry) {
            /* If the shipFromCountry does NOT equal the shipToCountry then ship Third Party. */
            SetThirdPartyBilling(vm.currentShipment);
        }
        else {
            /* Now check to see if both the origin and destination countries are members of the EU. */
            if ((IsMemberOfEu(shipFromCountry)) && (IsMemberOfEu(shipToCountry))) {
                SetThirdPartyBilling(vm.currentShipment);
            }

            //ShipThirdPartyBilling((IsMemberOfEu(shipFromCountry)) && (IsMemberOfEu(shipToCountry)));
        }

        if (shipFromCountry != "US") {
            $('select[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].Weight.Units"]').val('string:KG').change();
            $('select[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].Dimensions.Units"]').val('number:1').change();
        }
    }

// this.PostSelectAddressBook(shipmentRequest, nameaddress, addressName) // returns void
this.PostSelectAddressBook = function (shipmentRequest, nameaddress, addressName) {
        debugger;
        if (addressName !== '' && addressName !== 'ThirdPartyBillingAddress') {
            var checkExist = setInterval(function () {

                if (($('select[ng-model="nameaddress.Country"]:eq(0)').val().length > 0) && ($('select[ng-model="nameaddress.Country"]:eq(1)').val().length > 0)) {

                    /* Stop the timer. */
                    clearInterval(checkExist);
                    /* The values are stored in the format of 'string:CC'.  We only want the CC. */
                    var shipToCountry = $('select[ng-model="nameaddress.Country"]:eq(0)').val().replace('string:', '');
                    var shipFromCountry = $('select[ng-model="nameaddress.Country"]:eq(1)').val().replace('string:', '');

                    /* If we have no shipToCountry OR the shipFromCountry is either US or CA, disable the elements, return out. */
                    if (!shipToCountry | shipFromCountry == "US" | shipFromCountry == "CA") {
                        DisableThirdPartyBillingElements();
                        return false;
                    }

                    if (shipFromCountry != shipToCountry) {
                        /* If the shipFromCountry does NOT equal the shipToCountry then ship Third Party. */
                        SetThirdPartyBilling(shipmentRequest);
                    }
                    else {
                        /* Now check to see if both the origin and destination countries are members of the EU. */
                        if ((IsMemberOfEu(shipFromCountry)) && (IsMemberOfEu(shipToCountry))) {
                            SetThirdPartyBilling(shipmentRequest);
                        }

                        //ShipThirdPartyBilling((IsMemberOfEu(shipFromCountry)) && (IsMemberOfEu(shipToCountry)));
                    }

                    if (shipFromCountry != "US") {
                        $('select[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].Weight.Units"]').val('string:KG').change();
                        $('select[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].Dimensions.Units"]').val('number:1').change();
                    }
                } /* if ($('div.modal-dialog.modal-md:visible') */

            }, 50); /* var checkExist = setInterval... */
        }
    };

// SetThirdPartyBilling(shipmentRequest) // returns void
function SetThirdPartyBilling(shipmentRequest) {
        /* This enables the button to edit the Third Party Billing Information. */
        $('input[type=button][ng-disabled="!vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.ThirdPartyBilling"]').prop('disabled', false).attr('disabled', false);

        /* Check the box for Third Party Billing which will bring up the modal.  Fill the modal with values.  Click Save. */
        $('input[type=checkbox][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.ThirdPartyBilling"]').prop('checked', true).attr('checked', true).change();

        shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ThirdPartyBillingAddress = {}
        shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ThirdPartyBillingAddress.Company = 'PRA Global';
        shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ThirdPartyBillingAddress.Address1 = '995 Research Park Blvd';
        shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ThirdPartyBillingAddress.Address2 = 'Suite 300';
        shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ThirdPartyBillingAddress.City = 'Charlottesville';
        shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ThirdPartyBillingAddress.StateProvince = 'VA';
        shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ThirdPartyBillingAddress.PostalCode = '22911';
        shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ThirdPartyBillingAddress.Account = '883F79';
        shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ThirdPartyBillingAddress.Country = 'US'
    }

// DisableThirdPartyBillingElements() // returns void
function DisableThirdPartyBillingElements() {
        $('input[type=checkbox][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.ThirdPartyBilling"]').prop('checked', false).attr('checked', false);
        $('input[type=button][ng-disabled="!vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.ThirdPartyBilling"]').prop('disabled', true).attr('disabled', true);
    }

// IsMemberOfEu(v) // returns boolean
function IsMemberOfEu(v) {
        return ($.inArray(v, EuCountries) !== -1) ? true : false;
    }

// this.NewShipment(shipmentRequest) // returns void
this.NewShipment = function (shipmentRequest) {
        this.vm.IsValid = this.IsValidated;
        this.vm.TemplateInit = this.PageInitialize;
        this.vm.emailNotificationAddress = this.EmailNotificationAddress;
        var originCustomData = shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.OriginAddress.CustomData;
        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference1 = GetKeyValue('Custom1', originCustomData);
        ReturnNameAddressCaption(false);
    };

// Source: R.BCC EXPORTERS PRIVATE LIMITED (R.BCC)_ISMEA_FTP_1716.cs
// getFTPUploaded() // returns void
function getFTPUploaded() {
        var selectedShipper = document.getElementById("Shipper").value;
		var shipper = '';
		debugger;
		if (selectedShipper !== "")
		{
			selectedShipper = JSON.parse(selectedShipper);
			shipper = selectedShipper.Name;
		}
        var data = { Action: 'ExportFTP', Shipper: shipper };

        $.post('api/ShippingService/UserMethod',
            {UserContext: userContext, Data: JSON.stringify(data) },
            function(response, status, xhr) {
            }
        ).done(function(response) {
            debugger;
            var resp = JSON.stringify(response);
            resp = JSON.parse(resp);
            debugger;
            if (resp.Data !== "" && resp.Data !== undefined)
            {
                alert('Lastest File: \n' + DecodeReturnString(resp.Data).substring(0,resp.Data.length -1));
            }
            else if (resp.ErrorMessage !== undefined)
            {
                if (resp.ErrorCode == '104')
                {
                    alert('Lastest File: \nNo files found!');
                }
                else
                {
                    alert(resp.ErrorMessage);
                }
            }
        });
    }

			shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex].MiscReference2 = shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex - 1].MiscReference2;

// function PostLoad(value, shipmentRequest) // returns undefined
this.PostLoad = function(value, shipmentRequest) {
		//debugger;
		
		if (shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Service !== undefined && shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Service.Symbol === undefined) {
			alert("No service selected!");
		}

		if (shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ErrorMessage !== null  && shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ErrorMessage === 'validate')
		{
			// click validate button
			$('name-address[nameaddress="vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Consignee"]').find('button[ng-click="validate(nameaddress)"]').click();
			return;
		}

		if (shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ErrorMessage !== null && shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ErrorMessage.substring(0, 4) === 'pop:') {
			alert(shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ErrorMessage.substring(4));
			return;
		}

		if (shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ErrorMessage !== null && shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ErrorMessage !== '')
		{
			alert(shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ErrorMessage);
			return;
		}

		if (shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Country === 'US') {
			this.vm.shipMode = 1;
		} else {
			this.vm.shipMode = 0;
		}
		
		//getWeight(this.vm);   // TODO: disabled until scale issue resolved
		
		if (shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.MiscReference5 !== null && shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.MiscReference5 === 'autoship')
		{
			if (!this.vm.profile.ProfileSetting.DisableShip) {
				this.vm.checkShip();
			}
		}
	};

// Source: SAVERS (SAVERS)_Savers Client Side Rules_1715.cs
// function setConsigneeCountries(selectedCountries) // returns void
    function setConsigneeCountries(selectedCountries)
    {
        var countryStringValue = ('string:' + selectedCountries.join('|string:')).split('|');
        var interval = setInterval(function()

        {
            var consigneeCountries = $('name-address[address-property-name="Consignee"] select[name="Country"] option');
            if (consigneeCountries.length)
            {
                clearInterval(interval);
                Array.from(consigneeCountries).forEach(function(opt)

                {
                    if (opt.value != '')
                    {
                        if (!countryStringValue.includes(opt.value))
                        {
                            opt.remove();
                        }
                    }
                });
            }
        }, 50);            
    }

// function setCurrencyOptions(list, element) // returns void
function setCurrencyOptions(list, element)
    {
        var interval = setInterval(function() 
            {
                var currencies = $(element);
                if (currencies.length)
                {
                    clearInterval(interval);
                    currencies.each(function(){ if (!list.includes(this.text)) this.remove(); });
                }
            }, 50);
    }

// function replaceOptionValues(list, element) // returns void
 function replaceOptionValues(list, element) {
        var valuelist = list.map(function (e) { return 'string:' + e });
        var interval = setInterval(function () {
            var $element = $(element);
            if ($element.length) {
                clearInterval(interval);
                $element.each(function () {
                    if (!valuelist.includes(this.value) && this.value != '') this.remove();
                });
            }
        }, 50);
    }

// function filterPickupPaymentType() // returns void
        function filterPickupPaymentType() {
            $('body').delegate('button[ng-click="vm.createPickupRequestClick()"]', 'click', function (event) {
                var list = ['PAY_BY_SHIPPER_ACCOUNT'];
                var element = '[ng-model="vm.pickup.PaymentType"] option';
                replaceOptionValues(list, element);
            });
        }

                if (currencies.length) {
                    debugger;
                    clearInterval(interval);
                    currencies.each(function (){ if (!list.includes(this.text)) this.remove(); });
                }
            }, 50);
        }

// function PostSelectAddressBook(shipmentRequest, nameaddress) // returns void
this.PostSelectAddressBook = function(shipmentRequest, nameaddress) {

    //debugger;

    //Map Store Number to ShipperReference
    shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ShipperReference = nameaddress.Code;

    //Set Default Services Based on From and To Countries		
    var fromCountry = shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.OriginAddress.Country;
    var toCountry = nameaddress.Country;

    //Email Address Mappings
	if(nameaddress.Email != null)
	{
		shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ShipNotificationAddressEmail = nameaddress.Email.trim();
		shipmentRequest.Packages[0].DeliveryNotificationAddressEmail = nameaddress.Email.trim();
		shipmentRequest.Packages[0].DeliveryExceptionNotificationAddressEmail = nameaddress.Email.trim();
		shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ReturnDeliveryNotificationAddressEmail = nameaddress.Email.trim();
		shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ReturnDeliveryAddressEmail = nameaddress.Email.trim();
	}

    //Store Address Book ID value in MiscReference20 to signify that consignee address came from Address Book and was not manually entered.
    shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference20 = nameaddress.AddressBookId.toString();


    if (fromCountry == 'US' && toCountry == 'US')
    {
        this.SetSelectedService("UPSAPI.UPS.GND")
		this.SetCurrencyCAD(toCountry)
		this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].DeclaredValueAmount = { Currency: "USD" };
	}

    if (fromCountry == 'US' && toCountry == 'CA')
    {
        this.SetSelectedService("UPSAPI.UPS.STANDARD")
		this.SetCurrencyCAD(toCountry)
		this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].DeclaredValueAmount = { Currency: "USD" };
	}

    if (fromCountry == 'CA' && toCountry == 'CA')
    {
        this.SetSelectedService("UPSAPI.UPS.STANDARD")
		this.SetCurrencyCAD(toCountry)
		this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].DeclaredValueAmount = { Currency: "CAD" };
	}

    if (fromCountry == 'CA' && toCountry == 'US')
    {
        this.SetSelectedService("UPSAPI.UPS.STANDARD")
		this.SetCurrencyCAD(toCountry)
		this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].DeclaredValueAmount = { Currency: "CAD" };
	}
}

// function SetSelectedService(serviceSymbol) // returns void
//Select Service in Service List Box 
this.SetSelectedService = function(serviceSymbol)
    {
    if (this.vm.profile != null)
    {
        for (var i = 0; i < this.vm.profile.Services.length; i++)
        {
            if (this.vm.profile.Services[i].Symbol === serviceSymbol)
            {
                this.vm.selectedServices = [this.vm.profile.Services[i]];
                this.vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Service = this.vm.profile.Services[i];
                break;
            }
        }
    }
}

// function SetCurrencyCAD(shipToCountry) // returns void
//Set Currency to CAD
this.SetCurrencyCAD = function(shipToCountry)
{
    if (this.vm.profile != null)
    {
        if (shipToCountry === "CA")
        {
            //this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].DeclaredValueAmount = { Currency: "CAD" };
            this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].DeclaredValueCustoms = { Currency: "CAD" };
            this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].CodAmount = { Currency: "CAD" };
            this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].InvoiceDiscount = { Currency: "CAD" };
            this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].InvoiceFreight = { Currency: "CAD" };
            this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].InvoiceInsuranceFee = { Currency: "CAD" };
            this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].InvoiceOtherFee = { Currency: "CAD" };
        }
        else
        {
            //this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].DeclaredValueAmount = { Currency: "USD" };
            this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].DeclaredValueCustoms = { Currency: "USD" };
            this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].CodAmount = { Currency: "USD" };
            this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].InvoiceDiscount = { Currency: "USD" };
            this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].InvoiceFreight = { Currency: "USD" };
            this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].InvoiceInsuranceFee = { Currency: "USD" };
            this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].InvoiceOtherFee = { Currency: "USD" };
        }
    }
}

           debugger;

// function consigneeAddress() // returns address book entries array
    var consigneeAddress = function () {
       
        var userContext = client.userContext; 
        var shipper =  $('select[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Shipper"]').val();
        if(shipper != ''){
         shipper = shipper.replace('string:', '');
        }
        else{
         shipper = 'SCH_FARGO';
        }
            
        var address =  GetAddressBookEntries('Return', userContext, shipper);
        return address;
    }

// function thirdPartyBillingAddress() // returns address book entries array
    var thirdPartyBillingAddress = function () {
        var userContext = client.userContext; 
        var shipper = 'SCH_FARGO';
        var address =  GetAddressBookEntries('Return', userContext, shipper);
        return address;
    }

// function GetAddressBookEntries(addressBookName, context, shipper) // returns address book entry array or throws an error
    var GetAddressBookEntries = function (addressBookName, context, shipper) {
        var searchCriteria = { WhereClauses: [{ FieldName: "Name", FieldValue: addressBookName, Operator: 0 }] };
        var data = { CompanyId: context.CompanyId, UserId: context.UserId };
        var response = thinClientAPIRequest('GetAddressBooks', data, false).responseJSON;
        if (response.TotalRecords == 0) {
            throw ({ message: 'Address Book:"' + addressBookName + '" does not exists'});
        } else {
            var addressBookId = response.AddressBooks[0].Id;
            
            searchCriteria = { Skip: 0, WhereClauses: [{FieldName: "Code", FieldValue: shipper, Operator: 0}], OrderByClauses: [] };
            data = { AddressBookIds: [addressBookId], SearchCriteria: searchCriteria, UserContext :{Machine:""} , CompanyId: context.CompanyId, UserId: context.UserId };
            response = thinClientAPIRequest('GetAddressBookEntries', data, false).responseJSON;
            
            if (response.TotalRecords == 0) {
                throw ({ message: 'Address Book:"' + addressBookName + '" does not have any address entry'});
            } else {
                return response.AddressBookEntries;
            }
        }
    }

// Source: Schenker, Inc (schenker)_Schenker CBR 2.3 Fix_1756.cs
// this.PreShip(shipmentRequest, userParams) // returns void
    this.PreShip = function (shipmentRequest, userParams) {
        var shipperReference = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ShipperReference;
        if (!this.vm.IsValid('ShipperReference', shipperReference)) {
            throw ({ message: "Cost Center is invalid [" + shipperReference + "].", errorCode: "001" });
        }
    };

// this.NewShipment(shipmentRequest) // returns void
    this.NewShipment = function (shipmentRequest) {
        this.vm.IsValid = this.IsValidated;
        var originCustomData = shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.OriginAddress.CustomData;
        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ShipperReference = GetKeyValue('Custom1', originCustomData);

        if (!this.vm.IsValid('ShipperReference', shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ShipperReference)) {
            throw ({ message: 'Cost Center is invalid from User Custom Data', errorCode: '001' });
        }

        if (pageLoaded) {
            vm.fieldOptions["Consignee.StateProvince"].IsRequired = consigneeStateIsRequired;
            vm.fieldOptions["Consignee.Phone"].IsRequired = consigneePhoneIsRequired
            vm.fieldOptions.Description.IsRequired = descriptionIsRequired;
        }
    };

this.PageLoaded = function(location) {
		
		var vm, userContext ;
		var pickupDeliveryPane;
		
		vm = this.vm;
		
		if (location === '/shipping') {
			var interval = setInterval(function () {
				//pickupDeliveryPane = $('[ng-model="pickupDeliveryPane"]');
				pickupDeliveryPane = $('[name="pickupDeliveryForm"]')
				var loaded = pickupDeliveryPane.length;
				
				if (loaded) {
				    clearInterval(interval);
				    pickupDeliveryPaneReady(pickupDeliveryPane);
				}
			}, 50); 
		 }
    }

// this.GetDataManagementContents(apiMethod) // returns void
this.GetDataManagementContents = function (apiMethod) {
        var userContext = this.GetUserContext();
        var thinClientAPIRequest = this.thinClientAPIRequest;

        var data = { CompanyId: userContext.CompanyId };
        thinClientAPIRequest(apiMethod, data, true).done(function (result) {
            if (result.ErrorCode == 0) {
                var userObject = { Action: apiMethod, Data: JSON.stringify(result) };
                data = { Data: btoa(JSON.stringify(userObject)), UserContext: userContext };
                thinClientAPIRequest('UserMethod', data, true);//.done(function (result) { debugger; });
            };
        });
    }

// Source: Soundoff Signal (SOS)_Warehouse Shipping CBR_1803.cs
// GetNewTableMarkup(OrderData) // returns array of table row elements
  GetNewTableMarkup = (OrderData) =>
  {
    let that = this, rows = [];
    const json = new JsonData();

    //loop through the data and create the object that will be attached to each row as a .data() object
    OrderData.forEach((item, index) =>
    {
      json.TrimAllKeysAndValues(OrderData);

      //setup the row data object
      let data = {};
      //the .Count var is used when the items get placed into containers, it represents the count of items in the parent container object
      data.Count = 0;
      data.ItemNumber = item.CSpartno;
      data.ItemDescription = item.CSdescript;
      data.HarmonizedCode = (item.CSHTScode || 'Not Available');
      data.HarmonizedDescription = (item.CSHTSDESC || 'Not Available');
      data.CountryOfOrigin = (item.CSCOO || 'Not Available');
      data.OrderNumber = item.CSsono;
      data.OrderRevision = item.CSsorev;
      data.OrderString = item.CSsono + ` (${item.CSsorev})`;
      data.PurchaseOrder = item.fcustpono;
      data.QuantityOrdered = +item.CSshITMqty;
      data.QuantityPacked = 0;
      data.QuantityRemaining = +item.CSshITMqty;
      data.RowId = (Math.random() + 1).toString(36).substring(2);
      data.RowIndex = index;
      data.PackedItems = []; //.PackedItems will be {} objects with a structure of .ContainerIndex = x, .Count = y

      let row = $('tr.table-row-template').clone()
        .removeClass('table-row-template')
        .attr('row-id', data.RowId)
        .data(data);

      //add all the data to the table row
      $(row).find('td').each(function(i, td)
      {
        let key = $(td).attr('sos-key');
        $(td).find('div:first').text(data[key]);
      });

      //setup the tooltip for the description
      let title = `<div class="text-left"><span>HTS: <b>${data.HarmonizedCode}</b></span><br/>`;
      title += `<span>C/O: <b>${data.CountryOfOrigin}</b></span></div>`;
      $(row).find('td.item-description').first().attr({ 'data-toggle': "tooltip", 'data-placement': 'top', 'data-html': 'true', 'data-container': 'body', 'title': title });

      rows.push(row);
    });

    return rows;
  }

// GetNewListItemMarkup(RowData, ContainerIndex) // returns jQuery object for a list item
  GetNewListItemMarkup = (RowData, ContainerIndex) =>
  {
    let listItem = $('.list-item-template').first().clone();
    let dataKey = `C${ContainerIndex}_R${RowData.RowId}`;

    //by setting the list item .data() to the row item .data(), they stay linked
    $(listItem).removeClass('list-item-template').data(RowData)
      .attr({ 'row-id': RowData.RowId, 'row-index': RowData.RowIndex, 'item-number': RowData.ItemNumber, 'container-index': ContainerIndex, 'data-key': dataKey, 'id': dataKey })
      .find('span.li-item-number').text(RowData.ItemNumber);

    $(listItem).find('.li-item-number').attr({ 'data-toggle': "tooltip", 'data-placement': 'left', 'data-html': 'true', 'data-container': `#${dataKey}`, 'title': this.GetListItemTooltip(RowData, 1) });

    $(listItem).find('[data-toggle=tooltip]').tooltip();

    return listItem;
  }

// GetListItemTooltip(RowData, ItemCount) // returns HTML tooltip string
  GetListItemTooltip = (RowData, ItemCount) =>
  {
    let title = `<div class="text-left">`;
    title += `<div><span>Item: ${RowData.ItemNumber}</span></div>`;
    title += `<div><span>Desc: ${RowData.ItemDescription}</span></div>`;
    title += `<div><span>Count: </span><span class="item-count">${ItemCount}</span></div>`;
    title += `</div>`;

    return title;
  }

// GetTableDataPackedInBoxesTooltip(PackedItems) // returns HTML tooltip string
  GetTableDataPackedInBoxesTooltip = (PackedItems) =>
  {
    PackedItems.sort((a, b) => a.ContainerIndex - b.ContainerIndex);
    //ContainerIndex: x
    //Count: y
    let div = '<div>';

    $(PackedItems).each((a, b) =>
    {
      div += `<div>Box: ${b.ContainerIndex} Count: ${b.Count}</div>`;
    });

    div += `</div>`;

    return div;
  }

// function PostLoad(loadValue, shipmentRequest) // returns void
    this.PostLoad = function(loadValue, shipmentRequest) 
    {               
        loadselectedValue=loadValue;
        // Converting JS object to an array
        shipmentRequestObject =  JSON.parse(JSON.stringify(shipmentRequest));
        
        ChromeScrollIntoView($('[ng-model="vm.selectedServices"]'), shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Service.Symbol);

        // Check for not found error
        if(shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.MiscReference20)
        {
            if( shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.MiscReference20.substring(0,1) == '~')    
                {
                 alert(shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.MiscReference20.substring(1));
				  $("input:text").eq(0).focus();   
			  this.vm.newShipment();
	       		return;
                }
        }
        
        //Send OSCO related errors to end user
        if(shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.MiscReference20)
        {
            if (window.confirm(shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.MiscReference20 + "\nContinue with shipment?")) 
            {
              //alert("You pressed OK");
            } 
            else 
            {
                $("input:text").eq(0).focus();
            }   
        }
      
        // Check for address validation required
        if(shipmentRequest.Packages[0].UserData4)
        {
            if( shipmentRequest.Packages[0].UserData4 == 'Y')    
                {
                var interval = setInterval(function() {
                const consigneeNameAddress = $('name-address[address-property-name="Consignee"]');
                consigneeCompany = consigneeNameAddress.find('[ng-model="nameaddress.Company"]');
                consigneePostalCode = consigneeNameAddress.find('[name="postalCode"]');
                consigneeCity = consigneeNameAddress.find('[name="city"]');
                consigneeState = consigneeNameAddress.find('[name="stateProvince"]');

                var loaded = consigneeCompany.length && consigneePostalCode.length && consigneeCity.length && consigneeState.length;

                if (loaded) {
                    clearInterval(interval);
                    $('name-address[address-property-name="Consignee"] button[title="Validate Address"]').click();                    
                    }
                }, 50);
            }
        }
  
        $('[name="address1"]:eq(0)').val(shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Address1);
        
        $('[name="company"]:eq(0)').val(shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Company);
        
    //debugger;
    }

// function DrawDataInReturnForm() // returns void
    function DrawDataInReturnForm(){
        var carrierEmailReturnLabelMethod = 5;
        $('form[name="returnForm"]').find('[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].Description"]').val(RETURN_DEFAULT_DESCRIPTION);
        $('form[name="returnForm"]').find('[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].ReturnDelivery"]').prop("checked", true);
        $('select[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].ReturnDeliveryMethod"]>option:eq('+ carrierEmailReturnLabelMethod +')').prop('selected', true);
        $('input[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].ReturnDeliveryAddressEmail"]').val(shipmentRequestObject.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Email);
    }

// function MarkShipmentAsReturn() // returns void
    function MarkShipmentAsReturn(){
        for (let i = 0; i < vm.currentShipment.Packages.length; i++) 
        {
             vm.currentShipment.Packages[i].ReturnDelivery = true;
             vm.currentShipment.Packages[i].ReturnDeliveryMethod = 4;
             vm.currentShipment.Packages[i].ReturnDeliveryAddressEmail = shipmentRequestObject.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Email;
             vm.currentShipment.Packages[i].Description = RETURN_DEFAULT_DESCRIPTION;             
        }
    }

// function UnMarkShipmentAsReturn() // returns void
    function UnMarkShipmentAsReturn(){
        for (let i = 0; i < vm.currentShipment.Packages.length; i++) 
        {
             vm.currentShipment.Packages[i].ReturnDelivery = false;
             vm.currentShipment.Packages[i].ReturnDeliveryMethod = undefined;
             vm.currentShipment.Packages[i].ReturnDeliveryAddressEmail = '';
             vm.currentShipment.Packages[i].Description = '';
        }
    }

// this.PreShip(shipmentRequest, userParams) // returns void
    this.PreShip = function(shipmentRequest, userParams) {   
       debugger;
       if(shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ReturnAddress === undefined || shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ReturnAddress === null){
           if(!shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ReturnDelivery){
              var userName = this.vm.profile.UserInformation.Address.Contact;
              //alert(shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Shipper);
              var theShippers = this.vm.profile.Shippers;
              theShippers.forEach(shpr => {
                  if (shpr.Symbol === shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Shipper) {
                      shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ReturnAddress = {
                        Contact: userName,
                        Company: shpr.Company,
                        Address1: shpr.Address1,
                        Address2: shpr.Address2,
                        Address3: shpr.Address3,
                        City: shpr.City,
                        StateProvince: shpr.StateProvince,
                        PostalCode: shpr.PostalCode,
                        Country: shpr.Country,
                        Phone: shpr.Phone
                    };
                }
            });
          }
       }    
       
    };

// this.PreLoad(loadValue, shipmentRequest, userParams) // returns void
    this.PreLoad = function(loadValue, shipmentRequest, userParams) {
        debugger;
          var employeeID;
          var BU;
          var OU;
          var CR;
          var locationCode;
         var CustomData = this.vm.profile.UserInformation.Address.CustomData;
            for (var Custom in CustomData) {
                     if(CustomData[Custom].Key == "Custom1") employeeID = CustomData[Custom].Value;
                      if(CustomData[Custom].Key == "Custom2") BU = CustomData[Custom].Value;
                       if(CustomData[Custom].Key == "Custom3") OU = CustomData[Custom].Value;
                        if(CustomData[Custom].Key == "Custom4") CR = CustomData[Custom].Value;
                         if(CustomData[Custom].Key == "Custom5")  locationCode= CustomData[Custom].Value;
             }
             
         if (CR === undefined || !isFiveDigitNumber(CR)) {
            alert('Invalid Cost Center');
            }
            shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference3 = employeeID;
        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ConsigneeReference = CR;
        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference2 = CR;
         shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference4 = BU;
          shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference5 = locationCode;
    }

// Source: STAR INDIA CRAFT (STARINCRFT)_ISMEA_FTP_1583.cs
// getFTPUploaded() // returns void
function getFTPUploaded() {
        var selectedShipper = document.getElementById("Shipper").value;
		var shipper = '';
		debugger;
		if (selectedShipper !== "")
		{
			selectedShipper = JSON.parse(selectedShipper);
			shipper = selectedShipper.Name;
		}
        var data = { Action: 'ExportFTP', Shipper: shipper };

        $.post('api/ShippingService/UserMethod',
            {UserContext: userContext, Data: JSON.stringify(data) },
            function(response, status, xhr) {
            }
        ).done(function(response) {
            debugger;
            var resp = JSON.stringify(response);
            resp = JSON.parse(resp);
            debugger;
            if (resp.Data !== "" && resp.Data !== undefined)
            {
                alert('Lastest File: \n' + DecodeReturnString(resp.Data).substring(0,resp.Data.length -1));
            }
            else if (resp.ErrorMessage !== undefined)
            {
                if (resp.ErrorCode == '104')
                {
                    alert('Lastest File: \nNo files found!');
                }
                else
                {
                    alert(resp.ErrorMessage);
                }
            }
        });
    }

// Source: Sun Communities (SUNCOMMUNITIES)_SUN_Business Rules Kiosk_1600.cs
// NewShipment(shipmentRequest) // returns void
    this.NewShipment = function(shipmentRequest) {
        var originCustomData = GetCustomData(shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.OriginAddress);        
        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ShipperReference = GetKeyValue('ENTITY', originCustomData) + "-" + GetKeyValue('LOCATION', originCustomData) + "," + GetKeyValue('GL_CODE', originCustomData);        
        //shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ConsigneeReference = GetKeyValue('TMID', originCustomData);
        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference1 = GetKeyValue('ENTITY', originCustomData);        
        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference2 = GetKeyValue('GL_CODE', originCustomData);                
        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference3 = GetKeyValue('DEPARTMENT', originCustomData);
        shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.OriginAddress.Code = GetKeyValue('LOCATION', originCustomData);
        
        var location = GetKeyValue('LOCATION', originCustomData);
        
        // MOS or MOO to switch shipper to main office 
        if(location == "MOS" || location == "MOO")
            shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Shipper = "MOS";
    };

// Source: Sysco Foods (SYSCO)_Sysco_1674.cs
// PostLoad(loadValue, shipmentRequest) // returns void
function(loadValue, shipmentRequest) {
        shipmentRequest.SendViewModelToClient = this.GetViewModelFromTemplate;

        if (!angular.element('input[value="Get Weight"]').prop('disabled')){
            if (vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].Weight.Amount == undefined) {
                vm.getWeight();
            }
        }
        var startTime = new Date();
        var weightExists = setInterval(() => {
            if ((new Date().getTime() - startTime.getTime()) / 1000 >= 2) {
                clearInterval(weightExists);
            } else {
                if (vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].Weight.Amount != undefined) {
                    startTime.setMinutes(startTime.getMinutes() - 1);
                    vm.checkShip();
                    //$('#myShipBtn').click()
                }
            }
        }, 333);
    }

// Source: Tailor Made Compounding (TMC)_TailorMadeCompoundingClientTemplate_1691.cs
// PreLoad(loadValue, shipmentRequest, userParams) // returns undefined
    this.PreLoad = function(loadValue, shipmentRequest, userParams) { 
    debugger;
    var consolidatedOpportunities = $("#txtConsolidatedFields").find('*').filter(':input:visible:first').val();
    
       if) ($("#chkIsConsolidated").prop("checked") && ValidateConsolidatedOpportunitiesEntry(consolidatedOpportunities))
       {
         var shippingSession = CreateShippingSession("true",consolidatedOpportunities,loadValue);
         shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.UserData1 = shippingSession;
       }
       else
       {
            var shippingSession = CreateShippingSession("false","",loadValue);
            shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.UserData1 = shippingSession
       }
    }

// ValidateConsolidatedOpportunitiesEntry(consolidatedOpportunities) // returns boolean
    function ValidateConsolidatedOpportunitiesEntry(consolidatedOpportunities)
    {
        var rexVal = /^[A-Z0-9]+((,|-)[A-Z0-9]+)*[A-Z0-9]+$/;
        var result = true;
        if (!rexVal.test(consolidatedOpportunities.toUpperCase()))
        {
            if (consolidatedOpportunities.trim()==="")
            {
                result=true;
            }
            else
            {
                alert("Consolidated opportunities not well formed.");
                result= false;
            }
        }
        return result;
    }

// CreateShippingSession(IsConsolidatedShipping, ConsolidatedOpportunities, OpportunityLoaded) // returns string
    function CreateShippingSession(IsConsolidatedShipping,ConsolidatedOpportunities,OpportunityLoaded)
    {
        var jsonObject = {};
        jsonObject["IsConsolidatedShipping"] = IsConsolidatedShipping;
        jsonObject["ConsolidatedOpportunities"] = ConsolidatedOpportunities.split(',');
        jsonObject["OpportunityLoaded"] = OpportunityLoaded;
        return JSON.stringify(jsonObject);
    }

// IsConsolidatedChange(elementCheck) // returns undefined
    function IsConsolidatedChange(elementCheck){
        if ($("#chkIsConsolidated").prop("checked"))
        {
            $("#txtConsolidatedFields").show();   
        }
        else
        {
            $("#txtConsolidatedFields").hide();
        }
        
	}

// DecodeReturnString(data) // returns decoded parsed data or undefined on error
    function DecodeReturnString(data)
    { 
        try
        { 
            return JSON.parse($("<div />").html(data).text());
        }
        catch (error)
        { 
            console.log(error.name);
            console.log(error.message);
            console.log(data);
        }
    }

// Source: Texas EZ Corp (TexasEZ)_Texas EZ Reference Configuration Rule_1595.cs
// SendFreightCollect(shipmentRequest) // returns undefined
function SendFreightCollect(shipmentRequest) {
        var selection = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference20;
        if (selection.indexOf("-") > -1) {
            var position = selection.indexOf("-");
            shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Account = selection.substring(position + 2);
            shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Terms = "CONSIGNEE";
        } else {
            throw new error({ "number": "001", "description": "Receiver Billing Information not found." });
        }
    }

// GetKeyValue(key, arr) // returns string
function GetKeyValue(key, arr) {
        for (var index in arr) {
            if (arr[index].Key.toLowerCase() === key.toLowerCase()) return arr[index].Value;
        }
        return '';
    }

// CheckReference(referenceValue) // returns string
function CheckReference(referenceValue) {
        var returnValue;
        if (!referenceValue) {
            returnValue = "";
        } else {
            returnValue = referenceValue;
        }
        return returnValue;
    }

// function PreShip(shipmentRequest, userParams) // returns void
    this.PreShip = function (shipmentRequest, userParams) {
        if (this.vm.returnLabel && this.vm.GTSreturnLabel) {
            throw Error('You have selected to include a Return Label AND Global Tech Return Label. Please un-check one or the other and try again.');
        }

        if (this.vm.returnLabel || this.vm.GTSreturnLabel) {
            if (shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Phone === null ||
                shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Phone === '') {
                {
                    throw Error('You selected to print a return label but you did not provide the consignee phone number.');
                }
            }
        }
    }

    this.PreShip = function(shipmentRequest, userParams){
        /*var consigneeAddress = shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee;
        var userAddress = this.vm.profile.UserInformation.Address;
        if(consigneeAddress.Country!=userAddress.Country)

            shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Exporter = userAddress

                }

				    pkg.DryIceRegulationSet = 2;
				}
				
                pkg.DryIcePurpose = 2;
            }
        });
    }

// this.PreRate(shipmentRequest, userParams) // returns void
    this.PreRate = function(shipmentRequest, userParams) {
        debugger;

        var shipToEmail = returnPropertyValue(shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Email);
        var shipFromEmail = returnPropertyValue(shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.OriginAddress.Email);
        var ref1 = returnPropertyValue(shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference1);
        var ref2 = returnPropertyValue(shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference2);
        var ref3 = returnPropertyValue(shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference3);
        var ref4 = returnPropertyValue(shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference4);
        var ref5 = returnPropertyValue(shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference5);
        var ref6 = returnPropertyValue(shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference6);
        var ref7 = returnPropertyValue(shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference7);
        var ref8 = returnPropertyValue(shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference8);

        var shipperRef = ref1 + "~" + ref2 + "~" + ref3 + "~" + ref4;
        var consigneeRef = ref5 + "~" + ref6;//ref7 + "~" + ref8 + "~" +

        shipmentRequest.Packages.forEach(function (pkg)
        {
            if(pkg.MiscReference7)
            {
                if (shipmentRequest.Packages.length > 1 ) {
                    throw ({message: 'Multiple Packages Not Support with Dry Ice', errorCode: ''});
                }

                if (returnPropertyValue(pkg.MiscReference8) === '')
                {
                    throw ({message: 'Missing Dry Ice Weight', errorCode: ''});
                }
                
                var ret = ref8;
                
                var DryIceWeight = {
                    "Amount": ret.replace('kgs',''),
                    "Units": "KG"
                };
				pkg.DryIceWeight = DryIceWeight;
				
				var Country = shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Country;
				console.log(Country);
				if(Country =="US"){
				    pkg.DryIceRegulationSet = 1;
				}else{
				    pkg.DryIceRegulationSet = 2;
				}
                pkg.DryIcePurpose = 2;
            }
            pkg.ShipperReference = shipperRef;
            pkg.ConsigneeReference = consigneeRef;
            pkg.MiscReference20 = userContext.UserId;

            pkg.ShipNotificationAddressEmail = '';
            pkg.ShipNotificationEmail = shipToEmail != '' || shipFromEmail != '';
            if (shipToEmail != '') {
                pkg.ShipNotificationAddressEmail = shipToEmail;
            }

            if (shipFromEmail != '' ) {
                if (pkg.ShipNotificationAddressEmail) {
                    pkg.ShipNotificationAddressEmail += ',' + shipFromEmail;
                } else {
                    pkg.ShipNotificationAddressEmail = shipFromEmail;
                }
            }
        });
    }

// Source: Truist (BBANDT)_Truist Admin Business Rules_2463.cs
// this.PreRate(shipmentRequest, userParams) // returns void
    this.PreRate = function(shipmentRequest, userParams) {
        if (shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Country == 'US') {
            var state = String(shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.StateProvince).toLowerCase();
            if (state.length == 2) {
                state = state.toUpperCase();
            } else if (state.length > 2) {
                switch (state) {
                case "alabama":
                    state = "AL";
                    break;
                case "alaska":
                    state = "AK";
                    break;
                case "arizona":

// this.NewShipment(shipmentRequest) // returns void
    this.NewShipment = function(shipmentRequest) {
        vm = this.vm;
        //shipmentRequest.CreateShipment = this.BuildShipment;
        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ShipperReference = this.GetCustom("Custom1", "User", shipmentRequest);
        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ConsigneeReference = this.GetCustom("Custom2", "User", shipmentRequest);
    };

// this.GetCustom(fieldName, customDataType, shipmentRequest) // returns string
    this.GetCustom = function(fieldName, customDataType, shipmentRequest) {
        var returnValue = "";
        var customData = null;
        if (customDataType === "User") {
            if (shipmentRequest &&
                shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults &&
                shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.OriginAddress &&
                shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.OriginAddress.CustomData)
                customData = shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.OriginAddress.CustomData;
        }
        if (customDataType === "To") {
            if (shipmentRequest &&
                shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults &&
                shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee &&
                shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.CustomData)
                customData = shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.CustomData;
        }

        if (customData) {
            customData.forEach(function(customField) {
                if (fieldName === customField.Key) returnValue = customField.Value;
            });
        }
        return returnValue;

    };

// this.PostSelectAddressBook(shipmentRequest, nameaddress) // returns void
        this.PostSelectAddressBook = function (shipmentRequest, nameaddress) {
            var customData = nameaddress.CustomData;
            var fieldName = "Custom2"
        if (customData) {
            customData.forEach(function(customField) {
                if (fieldName === customField.Key) shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference3 = customField.Value;
        });
        }
             
            if(nameaddress.Code == "hSTI-GLENALLEN")
            {
                glenallenShipment=true;
                var service = [{Symbol: "UPSAPI.UPS.NDA", Name: "UPS Next Day Air (UPS Adapter)"}];
                vm.profile.ProfileSetting.ServiceSelectionMode = 1;
                this.vm.selectedServices = service;
                this.vm.showServiceSelection=false;
            } 
    };

// NewShipment(shipmentRequest) // returns void
  this.NewShipment = function(shipmentRequest)
  {
    shipmentRequest.TemplateInit = this.PageInitialize;

    if (!angular.isUndefined(tpbAddressBookEntries)) 
    {
      shipmentRequest.xConsigneeCodes = tpbAddressBookEntries;
    }
  };

// PreShip(shipmentRequest, userParams) // returns void
  this.PreShip = function(shipmentRequest, userParams)
  {
    var consigneeCode = $('select[ng-model="xConsigneeCode"]');
    var selectCode = consigneeCode.val().substring(7);

    if (selectCode === '')
    {
      throw ({ message: 'Please select a lab', errorCode: 43770 });
    }
    var arr = this.vm.currentShipment.xConsigneeCodes;
    var obj = arr.filter(function(nameaddress)
    {
      if (nameaddress.Code === selectCode) { return nameaddress; }
    });

    if (obj.length)
    {
      var nameaddress = obj[0];
      var consignee = shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee;
      consignee.Company = nameaddress.Company;
      consignee.Contact = nameaddress.Contact;
      consignee.Address1 = nameaddress.Address1;
      consignee.Address2 = nameaddress.Address2;
      consignee.Address3 = nameaddress.Address3;
      consignee.City = nameaddress.City;
      consignee.StateProvince = nameaddress.StateProvince;
      consignee.PostalCode = nameaddress.PostalCode;
      consignee.Country = nameaddress.Country;
      consignee.Phone = nameaddress.Phone;
      consignee.Email = nameaddress.Email;
      consignee.Account = nameaddress.Account;

      shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Shipper = GetKeyValue('shipper', nameaddress.CustomData);
      shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.OriginAddress.StateProvince = shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.OriginAddress.StateProvince.toUpperCase();
    }
  };

// PageInitialize(viewModel) // returns void
    this.PageInitialize = function(viewModel) {
        vm = viewModel;
        //console.log(client.userContext);
        var searchCriteria = {WhereClauses:[{ FieldName:"Name", FieldValue:"Company Address Book", Operator:0 }]};
        var data = { SearchCriteria: searchCriteria, CompanyId: client.userContext.CompanyId, UserId: client.userContext.UserId };
        //var data = { UserContext: client.userContext, SearchCriteria: searchCriteria };
        
		//debugger;
		
        $.when(client.thinClientAPIRequest('GetAddressBooks_Shared', data, false).done(function(response, status, xhr)
        {
            //console.log('response from inside method: ', response);

            if (response.TotalRecords > 0) 
            {
                var addressBookId = response.AddressBooks[0].Id;
    
                data = { UserContext: client.userContext, AddressBookIds: [addressBookId], CompanyId: client.userContext.CompanyId, UserId: client.userContext.UserId };
                //console.log(data);
                
                $.when(client.thinClientAPIRequest('GetAddressBookEntries_Shared', data, false).done(function(response, status, xhr)
                {
                    //console.log(response);
                    if (response.TotalRecords > 0) 
                    {
                        tpbAddressBookEntries = response.AddressBookEntries;
                        vm.currentShipment.xConsigneeCodes = tpbAddressBookEntries;
                    }                    
                    //debugger;
                }));
            }
        }));

    };

// this.PrePrint(doc, localPort, viewModel) // returns undefined
    this.PrePrint = function(doc, localPort, viewModel){
        // WORKAROUND for bug #544 where printer profile doesn't send optional settings
    	// attach control string to set defaults to start of document string
    	//if(doc.RawData){  !!
    	if((doc.DocumentSymbol == 'UPSAPI.UPS.PACKAGE_LABEL.STANDARD') && doc.RawData){
        	var printerDefaults = "^XA^LH0,0^XSY,Y^MD30^XZ\n";
        	var oldraw = atou(doc.RawData[0]);
        	var newraw = printerDefaults + oldraw;
        	doc.RawData[0] = utoa(newraw);
    	}
    };

// Source: WILLIAMS-SONOMA (WSintl) (WSintl)_WSIntl Reference Rule_75.cs
// this.NewShipment(shipmentRequest) // returns undefined
    this.NewShipment = function (shipmentRequest) {
    //shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Code = " ";
    //shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.OriginAddress = " ";
        var DC = {Units: "USD"};
        shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.DeclaredValueCustoms= DC;

        this.vm.profile.FieldOptions["CommodityContent.UnitWeight.Units"].DefaultValue = " ";
    };

// this.PreShip(shipmentRequest, userParams) // returns undefined
    this.PreShip = function (shipmentRequest, userParams) {
        this.ValidateShipment(shipmentRequest);
        //var userId = userContext.UserId;
        var ConsigneeCustomData = shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.CustomData;
        var ref1 = GetKeyValue('Custom1', ConsigneeCustomData);
        var ref2 = GetKeyValue('Custom2', ConsigneeCustomData);
        var ref3;
        var account = GetKeyValue('Custom3', ConsigneeCustomData);
        //Begin Determine Shipper
        if (account === "0000A0031E") {
            shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Shipper = "OTHER_A0031E";
        }
        if (account === "0000A0027E") {
            shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Shipper = "OTHER";
        }
        if (account === "0000872A2E") {
            shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Shipper = "OTHER_872A2E";
        }
        if (account === "000033A17X") {
            shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Shipper = "AUS";
        }
        if (account === "00007W7182") {
            shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Shipper = "UK";
        }
        if (account === "00005R86R0") {
            shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Shipper = "SG_5R86R0";
        }
        if (account === "00005R852X") {
            shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Shipper = "SG_5R852X";
        }
        //End Determine Shipper
        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ShipperReference = ref1;
        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ConsigneeReference = ref2;
        //Begin Determine Service
        var Code = shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Code;
        var SvcIdx = Code.lastIndexOf("-");
        if (SvcIdx === -1) {
            //var Service = { "Symbol": "UPSAPI.UPS.EXPEDITED", "Name": "UPS Expedited (UPS Adapter)" };
            var Service = { "Symbol": "CONNECTSHIP_UPS.UPS.EPD", "Name": "UPS Expedited (UPS ConnectShip)" };
            shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Service = Service;
        } else {
            var ServiceCode = Code.substring(SvcIdx + 1, SvcIdx + 2);
            if (ServiceCode === "E") {
                //var ServiceE = { "Symbol": "UPSAPI.UPS.EXPEDITED", "Name": "UPS Expedited (UPS Adapter)" };
                var ServiceE = { "Symbol": "CONNECTSHIP_UPS.UPS.EPD", "Name": "UPS Expedited (UPS ConnectShip)" };
                shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Service = ServiceE;
            }
            if (ServiceCode === "S") {
                //var ServiceS = { Symbol: "UPSAPI.UPS.SAVER", "Name": "UPS Saver (UPS Adapter)"  };
                var ServiceS = { "Symbol": "CONNECTSHIP_UPS.UPS.EXPSVR", "Name": "UPS Expedited (UPS ConnectShip)" };
                shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Service = ServiceS;
            }
        }
        //End Determine Service
        for (var i = 0; i < shipmentRequest.Packages.length; i++) {
            shipmentRequest.Packages[i].ShipperReference = ref1;
            if (shipmentRequest.Packages[i].MiscReference1) {
                ref3 = shipmentRequest.Packages[i].MiscReference1;
            } else {
                ref3 = "";
            }
            shipmentRequest.Packages[i].ConsigneeReference = ref2 + " " + ref3;
            //shipmentRequest.Packages[i].MiscReference19 = userId;
        }
    };

// this.ValidateShipment(shipmentRequest) // returns undefined
    this.ValidateShipment = function(shipmentRequest){
    if(shipmentRequest.Packages.length>20)
    { 
        throw {errorCode:999,message:"You cannot ship more than 20 packages."};
    }
    var weight = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].Weight;
    var weightLimit = 0;
    var totalWeight = 0;
    if(weight.Units==="LB"){
            weightLimit = 150;
    }else{
        weightLimit = 68;
    }
    var i;
    for(i = 0; i < shipmentRequest.Packages.length; i++)
    {
        var pkgWeight = parseFloat(shipmentRequest.Packages[i].Weight.Amount);
       totalWeight += pkgWeight;
    }
    if(totalWeight > weightLimit){
        throw {errorCode:999,message:"You cannot ship greater than " + weightLimit + " " + weight.Units + ".  Total Weight: "+ totalWeight + " " + weight.Units};
    }
}

        shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex].MiscReference4 = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference4;

        shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex].MiscReference12 = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference12;
        shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex].MiscReference13 = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference13;
        shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex].MiscReference14 = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference14;

        shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex].Description = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].Description;

// NewShipment(shipmentRequest) // returns undefined
    this.NewShipment = function (shipmentRequest) {
        this.vm.buildShipment = this.BuildShipment;
        this.vm.getUserContext = this.GetUserContext;
        this.vm.postalCodeLookup = this.PostalCodeLookup;
        this.vm.thinClientAPIRequest = this.ThinClientAPIRequest;
        this.vm.createShipmentAutoSubmit = this.CreateShipmentAutoSubmit;

        shipmentRequest.selectAddress = this.SelectAddress;
        shipmentRequest.updateNameAddressCSZ = this.UpdateNameAddressCSZ;
        shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Shipper = this.vm.profile.Shippers[0].Symbol;

        client.shipping.consigneeCompanyFocus();
    }

// Shipping() // returns undefined
    this.Shipping = function () {
        this.vm.profile.Services.sort(byService);

        $(client.shipping.buildShipmentModal).on('shown.bs.modal', function () {
            client.shipping.buildTotalPackagesFocus();
        });

        $('body').delegate('input[name="postalCode"]', 'keydown', this.vm, postalCodeLookUp)

        function byService(a, b) {
            var sortingArr = [
                "UPS Next Day Air EAM (UPS Adapter)",
                "UPS Next Day Air (UPS Adapter)",
                "UPS Next Day Air Saver (UPS Adapter)",
                "UPS Second Day Air AM (UPS Adapter)",
                "UPS Second Day Air (UPS Adapter)",
                "UPS Three-Day Select (UPS Adapter)",
                "UPS Ground (UPS Adapter)"
            ]
            return sortingArr.indexOf(a.Name) - sortingArr.indexOf(b.Name);
        }

        function postalCodeLookUp(e) {
            var nameAddress = $(this).parents('name-address');
            e.data.addressName = nameAddress.attr('address-property-name');
            if (e.data.addressName == "Consignee" || e.data.addressName == "ReturnAddress") {
                var keyEvent = (event.keyCode ? event.keyCode : event.which);
                if (keyEvent == 13 || keyEvent == 9) {
                    var city = nameAddress.find('[name="city"]');
                    var stateProvince = nameAddress.find('[name="stateProvince"]');
                    var postalCode = $(this).val();
                    if ((city.val() == '' || stateProvince.val() == '') && postalCode != '') {
                        $(client.shipping.cbrPostalCodeLookup).click();
                    }
                }
            }
        }
    }

// BuildShipment(ret) // returns undefined
    this.BuildShipment = function (ret) {
        client.shipping.buildShipmentModalHide();

        var weightPerPackage;
        var multiPackage = this.currentShipment.Packages.length > 1;

        if (ret.TotalWeight !== undefined && ret.TotalWeight !== 0 && ret.TotalWeight !== "")
            weightPerPackage = (ret.TotalWeight / ret.TotalPackages).toFixed(3);

        for (var i = 0; i < ret.TotalPackages; i++) {
            this.packageIndex = this.currentShipment.Packages.length - 1;
            if (i > 0 || multiPackage) {
                this.addPackage();
                multiPackage = true;
            }

            if (weightPerPackage !== undefined)
                this.currentShipment.Packages[this.packageIndex].Weight.Amount = weightPerPackage;
            if (ret.WeightUnit !== undefined)
                this.currentShipment.Packages[this.packageIndex].Weight.Units = ret.WeightUnit;
            else
                this.currentShipment.Packages[this.packageIndex].Weight.Units = this.translations.WeightUnit;
        }
        this.totalPackages = this.currentShipment.Packages.length;

        ret.TotalWeight = '';
        ret.TotalPackages = '';
    }

// PostalCodeLookup(addressName) // returns undefined
    this.PostalCodeLookup = function (addressName) {
debugger;
        var userContext = this.getUserContext(this);
        var postalCode = $('[address-property-name="' + addressName + '"] [name="postalCode"]').val();
        var content = { AddressName: addressName, PostalCode: postalCode };
        var payload = { Action: 'CSZ', Content: JSON.stringify(content) };
        var data = { Data: JSON.stringify(payload), UserContext: userContext };
        var response = this.thinClientAPIRequest('UserMethod', data, false).responseJSON;
        if (response.ErrorCode > 0) {
            client.shipping.alertModalShow(this, 'Postal Code Search', response.ErrorMessage)
        } else {
            var responseData = JSON.parse(client.htmlText(response.Data));        
            if (responseData == null) {
                client.shipping.alertModalShow(this, 'Postal Code Search', 'Invalid or Not US Postal Code');
            } else {
                if (responseData.length > 1) {
                    this.addressResults = responseData;
                    client.shipping.validateAddressModalShow();
                } else {
                    this.currentShipment.updateNameAddressCSZ(addressName, responseData[0].City, responseData[0].StateProvince)
                }
            }
        }
    }

// UpdateNameAddressCSZ(addressName, city, stateProvince) // returns undefined
    this.UpdateNameAddressCSZ = function (addressName, city, stateProvince) {
        var nameAddress = this.PackageDefaults.Consignee;
        if (addressName == 'ReturnAddress') {
            if (this.PackageDefaults.ReturnAddress == undefined)
                this.PackageDefaults.ReturnAddress = {};
            nameAddress = this.PackageDefaults.ReturnAddress;
        }
        nameAddress.City = city;
        nameAddress.StateProvince = stateProvince;
    }

// SelectAddress(address) // returns undefined
    this.SelectAddress = function (address) {
        client.shipping.validateAddressModalHide();
        this.updateNameAddressCSZ(address.AddressName, address.City, address.StateProvince);
    }

// CreateShipmentAutoSubmit(keyEvent) // returns undefined
    this.CreateShipmentAutoSubmit = function (keyEvent) {
        if (keyEvent.keyCode === 13 || keyEvent.keyCode === 9) {            
            event.preventDefault();
debugger;
            var $createShipmentBtn = $('#createShipmentBtn');
            var createShipmentInput = '#buildShipmentModalBody input';

            if (document.activeElement.id == $createShipmentBtn.attr('id')) {
                if (!isInputsEmpty($(createShipmentInput))) {
                    // click on create build button if sending tab or enter while focus is on button
                    $createShipmentBtn.click();
                }
            } else {
                if (!isInputsEmpty($(createShipmentInput))) {
                    // allow shipper chance to change weight unit
                    $createShipmentBtn.focus();
                }
            }
        }

        function isInputsEmpty($inputs) {
            var inputsIsEmpty = false;
            $inputs.each(function () {
                if (this.type == 'text') {
                    if (this.value.trim() == "") {
                        this.focus();
                        inputsIsEmpty = true;
                        return false;
                    };
                };
            });
            return inputsIsEmpty;
        }
    }

// BuildShipment(ret) // returns undefined
this.BuildShipment = function (ret) {
        $buildShipmentModal.modal('hide');

        var weightPerPackage;
        var multiPackage = vm.currentShipment.Packages.length > 1;

        if (ret.TotalWeight !== undefined && ret.TotalWeight !== 0 && ret.TotalWeight !== "")
            weightPerPackage = (ret.TotalWeight / ret.TotalPackages).toFixed(3);

        for (var i = 0; i < ret.TotalPackages; i++) {
            vm.packageIndex = vm.currentShipment.Packages.length - 1;
            if (i > 0 || multiPackage) {
                vm.addPackage();
                multiPackage = true;
            }

            if (weightPerPackage !== undefined)
                vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].Weight.Amount = weightPerPackage;
            if (ret.WeightUnit !== undefined)
                vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].Weight.Units = ret.WeightUnit;
            else
                vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].Weight.Units = vm.translations.WeightUnit;
        }

        vm.totalPackages = vm.currentShipment.Packages.length;

        ret.TotalWeight = '';
        ret.TotalPackages = '';
    }
